### Install OpenAI SDK for Kimi API

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/kimi-k2-quickstart

Installs the necessary OpenAI SDK for interacting with the Kimi API. Ensure you have pip installed and are using a recent version of the SDK for compatibility.

```bash
pip install --upgrade 'openai>=1.0'
```

--------------------------------

### Basic Kimi K2 API Call (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/kimi-k2-quickstart

Demonstrates a basic API call to the Kimi K2 model using the OpenAI SDK. This example shows how to set up the client, define the model and messages, and print the response. It requires an API key and base URL.

```python
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key = "$MOONSHOT_API_KEY",
    base_url = "https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

completion = client.chat.completions.create(
    model = "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
    messages = [
        {"role": "system", "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"},
        {"role": "user", "content": "你好，我叫李雷，1+1等于多少？"}
    ],
    temperature = 0.6, #控制输出的随机性
    # max_tokens=32000, #最大输出 tokens
)

print(completion.choices[0].message.content)
```

Verifies that the OpenAI SDK has been successfully installed by printing its version. This helps confirm that the SDK is available for use in your Python environment.

```python
python -c 'import openai; print("version =",openai.__version__)'
```

### Streaming Output with Python SDK

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/utilize-the-streaming-output-feature-of-kimi-api

This example demonstrates how to enable and handle streaming output from the Kimi API using the Python SDK. By setting `stream=True`, the API returns responses in chunks as tokens are generated, allowing for real-time display.

```APIDOC
## POST /v1/chat/completions (Streaming)

### Description
Enables streaming output for chat completions, allowing the client to receive tokens as they are generated by the Kimi model. This significantly reduces perceived latency for the user.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
/v1/chat/completions

### Parameters
#### Path Parameters
None

#### Query Parameters
None

#### Request Body
- **model** (string) - Required - The model to use for completion (e.g., "kimi-k2-turbo-preview").
- **messages** (array) - Required - A list of message objects representing the conversation history.
  - **role** (string) - Required - The role of the message sender ('system', 'user', or 'assistant').
  - **content** (string) - Required - The content of the message.
- **temperature** (number) - Optional - Controls randomness. Lower values make the output more focused and deterministic.
- **stream** (boolean) - Required - Set to `true` to enable streaming output.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "model": "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
  "messages": [
    {"role": "system", "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"},
    {"role": "user", "content": "你好，我叫李雷，1+1等于多少？"}
  ],
  "temperature": 0.6,
  "stream": true
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
When `stream=True`, the response `Content-Type` is `text/event-stream`. The response body consists of multiple Server-Sent Events (SSE), each prefixed with `data: ` and containing a JSON object. Each JSON object represents a chunk of the generated response.

- **choices[0].delta.content** (string) - The generated token(s) for the current chunk.
- **choices[0].finish_reason** (string | null) - Indicates why the generation finished (e.g., "stop").
- **usage** (object) - Token usage information (only present in the final chunk).
  - **prompt_tokens** (integer) - Number of tokens in the prompt.
  - **completion_tokens** (integer) - Number of tokens in the completion.
  - **total_tokens** (integer) - Total tokens used.

#### Response Example (SSE format)
```
data: {"id":"cmpl-1305b94c570f447fbde3180560736287","object":"chat.completion.chunk","created":1698999575,"model":"kimi-k2-turbo-preview","choices":[{"index":0,"delta":{"role":"assistant","content":""},"finish_reason":null}]}

data: {"id":"cmpl-1305b94c570f447fbde3180560736287","object":"chat.completion.chunk","created":1698999575,"model":"kimi-k2-turbo-preview","choices":[{"index":0,"delta":{"content":"你好"},"finish_reason":null}]}

...

data: {"id":"cmpl-1305b94c570f447fbde3180560736287","object":"chat.completion.chunk","created":1698999575,"model":"kimi-k2-turbo-preview","choices":[{"index":0,"delta":{"content":"。"},"finish_reason":null}]}

data: {"id":"cmpl-1305b94c570f447fbde3180560736287","object":"chat.completion.chunk","created":1698999575,"model":"kimi-k2-turbo-preview","choices":[{"index":0,"delta":{},"finish_reason":"stop","usage":{"prompt_tokens":19,"completion_tokens":13,"total_tokens":32}}]}

data: [DONE]
```
```

--------------------------------

### Install and Configure Claude Code on Windows (PowerShell)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/agent-support

Installs Node.js using winget, sets the execution policy, installs the 'claude-code' npm package, and then initializes the configuration file using a Node.js script. This is a step-by-step guide for Windows users.

```powershell
winget install OpenJS.NodeJS
Set-ExecutionPolicy -Scope CurrentUser RemoteSigned

# Then close the terminal window, open a new terminal window

# Install claude-code
npm install -g @anthropic-ai/claude-code --registry=https://registry.npmmirror.com

# Initialize configuration
node --eval "
    const homeDir = os.homedir(); 
    const filePath = path.join(homeDir, '.claude.json');
    if (fs.existsSync(filePath)) {
        const content = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf-8'));
        fs.writeFileSync(filePath,JSON.stringify({ ...content, hasCompletedOnboarding: true }, 2), 'utf-8');
    } else {
        fs.writeFileSync(filePath,JSON.stringify({ hasCompletedOnboarding: true }), null, 'utf-8');
    }"
```

### API Request to Invoke a Formula Fiber (Web Search Example)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-formula-tool-in-chatapi

This example demonstrates how to invoke a specific formula, 'moonshot/web-search:latest', using a cURL command. It shows setting environment variables for the formula URI and base URL, and constructing a POST request with JSON payload containing the tool name and arguments.

```bash
export FORMULA_URI="moonshot/web-search:latest"
export MOONSHOT_BASE_URL="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1"

curl -X POST ${MOONSHOT_BASE_URL}/formulas/${FORMULA_URI}/fibers \
-H "Content-Type: application/json" \
-H "Authorization: Bearer $MOONSHOT_API_KEY" \
-d '{
  "name": "web_search",
  "arguments": "{\"query\": \"月之暗面最近有什么消息\"}"
}'
```

### Streaming Kimi K2 API Call (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/kimi-k2-quickstart

Shows how to make a streaming API call to the Kimi K2 model, enabling real-time output. This is useful for interactive applications where immediate feedback is desired. It requires an API key and base URL.

```python
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key = "MOONSHOT_API_KEY", # 替换为你自己的API Key
    base_url = "https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

stream = client.chat.completions.create(
    model = "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
    messages = [
        {"role": "system", "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"},
        {"role": "user", "content": "你好，我叫李雷，1+1等于多少？"}
    ],
    temperature=0.6, #控制输出的随机性
    max_tokens=32000, #最大输出tokens 
    stream=True, # 启用流式输出
)

for chunk in stream:
        delta = chunk.choices[0].delta #流式片段
        if delta.content:
                print(delta.content, end="")
```

### Implement JSON Mode using Partial Mode in Python

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/partial

This Python example demonstrates how to use Partial Mode to enforce JSON output. It initializes the OpenAI client, defines system and user messages, and sets the assistant's initial message with `"partial": True` to guide the model towards generating a JSON object.

```python
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key="$MOONSHOT_API_KEY",
    base_url="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

completion = client.chat.completions.create(
    model="kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
    messages=[
        {
            "role": "system",
            "content": "请从产品描述中提取名称、尺寸、价格和颜色，并在一个 JSON 对象中输出。",
        },
        {
            "role": "user",
            "content": "大米 SmartHome Mini 是一款小巧的智能家居助手，有黑色和银色两种颜色，售价为 998 元，尺寸为 256 x 128 x 128mm。可让您通过语音或应用程序控制灯光、恒温器和其他联网设备，无论您将它放在家中的任何位置。",
        },
        {
            "role": "assistant",
            "content": "{",
            "partial": True
        },
    ],
    temperature=0.6,
)

print('{'+completion.choices[0].message.content)
```

### Kimi API Chat Completion Example

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/start-using-kimi-api

This section provides a Python code example demonstrating how to use the Kimi API for chat completions. It shows how to initialize the OpenAI client with your API key and base URL, and how to send a chat message to the model.

```APIDOC
## POST /v1/chat/completions

### Description
This endpoint allows you to interact with the Kimi large language model for chat-based conversations. You can send messages and receive responses generated by the model.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
/v1/chat/completions

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
None

#### Request Body
- **model** (string) - Required - The ID of the model to use for this request (e.g., "kimi-k2-turbo-preview").
- **messages** (array) - Required - A list of message objects, where each object has a `role` (system, user, or assistant) and `content` (the message text).
- **temperature** (number) - Optional - Controls randomness. Lower values make the output more deterministic, while higher values make it more random. Defaults to 0.7.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "model": "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
  "messages": [
    {"role": "system", "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"},
    {"role": "user", "content": "你好，我叫李雷，1+1等于多少？"}
  ],
  "temperature": 0.6
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **choices** (array) - A list of choices, where each choice contains a `message` object.
  - **message** (object)
    - **role** (string) - The role of the author of the message (e.g., "assistant").
    - **content** (string) - The content of the message generated by the model.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "choices": [
    {
      "message": {
        "role": "assistant",
        "content": "你好，李雷！1+1 等于 2。这是一个基本的数学加法问题。如果你有其他问题或需要帮助，请随时告诉我。"
      }
    }
  ]
}
```
```

### Using kimi-k2-thinking Model

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-k2-thinking-model

This example demonstrates how to use the `kimi-k2-thinking` model for chat completions. It includes system and user messages.

```APIDOC
## POST /v1/chat/completions

### Description
Sends a chat completion request to the Kimi API using the `kimi-k2-thinking` model.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/chat/completions

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **model** (string) - Required - The model to use for chat completions (e.g., `kimi-k2-thinking`).
- **messages** (array) - Required - An array of message objects, each with a `role` (system or user) and `content`.
- **temperature** (number) - Optional - Controls randomness. Higher values make output more random. Defaults to 1.0.

### Request Example
```json
{
    "model": "kimi-k2-thinking",
    "messages": [
        {
            "role": "system",
            "content": "你是 Kimi。"
        },
        {
            "role": "user",
            "content": "请解释 1+1=2。"
        }
    ],
    "temperature": 1.0
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **id** (string) - The ID of the completion.
- **object** (string) - The type of object returned, usually `chat.completion`.
- **created** (integer) - Unix timestamp of when the completion was created.
- **model** (string) - The model used for the completion.
- **choices** (array) - A list of completion choices.
  - **index** (integer) - The index of the choice.
  - **message** (object) - The message content.
    - **role** (string) - The role of the author (e.g., `assistant`).
    - **content** (string) - The text content of the message.
  - **finish_reason** (string) - The reason the model stopped generating tokens (e.g., `stop`, `length`).
- **usage** (object) - Usage statistics for the completion.
  - **prompt_tokens** (integer) - Number of tokens in the prompt.
  - **completion_tokens** (integer) - Number of tokens in the completion.
  - **total_tokens** (integer) - Total tokens used.

*Note: When using `kimi-k2-thinking` or `kimi-k2.5` with thinking enabled, a `reasoning_content` field may also be present in the response, containing the model's thought process.*
```

--------------------------------

### Handle SSE Streaming Output without SDK (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/utilize-the-streaming-output-feature-of-kimi-api

This Python example shows how to handle Server-Sent Events (SSE) for streaming output directly via HTTP requests without using an SDK. It uses the httpx library to make a POST request and iterates through the response lines, parsing data chunks based on 'data: ' prefixes and handling the '[DONE]' signal.

```python
import httpx # 我们使用 httpx 库来执行我们的 HTTP 请求
import json

data = {
	"model": "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
	"messages": [
		# 具体的 messages
	],
	"temperature": 0.6,
	"stream": True,
}


# 使用 httpx 向 Kimi 大模型发出 chat 请求，并获得响应 r
r = httpx.post("https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/chat/completions", json=data)
if r.status_code != 200:
	raise Exception(r.text)


data: str

# 在这里，我们使用了 iter_lines 方法来逐行读取响应体
for line in r.iter_lines():
	# 去除每一行收尾的空格，以便更好地处理数据块
	line = line.strip()

	# 接下来我们要处理三种不同的情况：
	#   1. 如果当前行是空行，则表明前一个数据块已接收完毕（即前文提到的，通过两个换行符结束数据块传输），我们可以对该数据块进行反序列化，并打印出对应的 content 内容；
	#   2. 如果当前行为非空行，且以 data: 开头，则表明这是一个数据块传输的开始，我们去除 data: 前缀后，首先判断是否是结束符 [DONE]，如果不是，将数据内容保存到 data 变量；
	#   3. 如果当前行为非空行，但不以 data: 开头，则表明当前行仍然归属上一个正在传输的数据块，我们将当前行的内容追加到 data 变量尾部；

	if len(line) == 0:
		chunk = json.loads(data)

		# 这里的处理逻辑可以替换成你的业务逻辑，打印仅是为了展示处理流程
		choice = chunk["choices"][0]
		usage = choice.get("usage")
		if usage:
			print("total_tokens:", usage["total_tokens"])
		delta = choice["delta"]
		role = delta.get("role")
		if role:
			print("role:", role)
		content = delta.get("content")
		if content:
			print(content, end="")

		data = "" # 重置 data
	elif line.startswith("data: "):
		data = line.lstrip("data: ")

		# 当数据块内容为 [DONE] 时，则表明所有数据块已发送完毕，可断开网络连接
		if data == "[DONE]":
			break
	else:
		data = data + "\n" + line # 我们仍然在追加内容时，为其添加一个换行符，因为这可能是该数据块有意将数据分行展示
```

--------------------------------

### Kimi K2 Chat Completions API

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/kimi-k2-quickstart

This endpoint allows you to interact with the Kimi K2 model for chat-based completions. It supports various Kimi K2 model versions and features like long context and tool calling.

```APIDOC
## POST /v1/chat/completions

### Description
Sends a prompt to the Kimi K2 model and receives a text completion. This endpoint is compatible with the OpenAI API format.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
`https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/chat/completions`

### Parameters
#### Path Parameters
None

#### Query Parameters
None

#### Request Body
- **model** (string) - Required - The ID of the Kimi K2 model to use (e.g., `kimi-k2-turbo-preview`, `kimi-k2-thinking`).
- **messages** (array) - Required - A list of message objects, where each object has a `role` (`system`, `user`, or `assistant`) and `content`.
- **temperature** (number) - Optional - Controls the randomness of the output. Lower values make the output more deterministic.
- **max_tokens** (integer) - Optional - The maximum number of tokens to generate in the completion.
- **stream** (boolean) - Optional - If set to `true`, the response will be streamed in chunks.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "model": "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
  "messages": [
    {"role": "system", "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"},
    {"role": "user", "content": "你好，我叫李雷，1+1等于多少？"}
  ],
  "temperature": 0.6
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **id** (string) - The ID of the completion.
- **object** (string) - The type of object returned, e.g., `chat.completion`.
- **created** (integer) - Unix timestamp of when the completion was created.
- **model** (string) - The model used for the completion.
- **choices** (array) - A list of completion choices.
  - **index** (integer) - The index of the choice.
  - **message** (object)
    - **role** (string) - The role of the message (e.g., `assistant`).
    - **content** (string) - The generated text content.
  - **finish_reason** (string) - The reason the model stopped generating tokens (e.g., `stop`, `length`).
- **usage** (object)
  - **prompt_tokens** (integer) - The number of tokens in the prompt.
  - **completion_tokens** (integer) - The number of tokens in the completion.
  - **total_tokens** (integer) - The total number of tokens used.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "id": "chatcmpl-xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx",
  "object": "chat.completion",
  "created": 1700000000,
  "model": "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
  "choices": [
    {
      "index": 0,
      "message": {
        "role": "assistant",
        "content": "你好，李雷！1+1 等于 2。这是一个基本的数学加法问题。如果你有其他问题或需要帮助，请随时告诉我。"
      },
      "finish_reason": "stop"
    }
  ],
  "usage": {
    "prompt_tokens": 30,
    "completion_tokens": 30,
    "total_tokens": 60
  }
}
```

### Streaming Response Example (if `stream=true`)
```json
{
  "id": "chatcmpl-xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx",
  "object": "chat.completion.chunk",
  "created": 1700000000,
  "model": "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
  "choices": [
    {
      "index": 0,
      "delta": {
        "content": "你好，"
      },
      "finish_reason": null
    }
  ],
  "usage": {
    "prompt_tokens": 30,
    "completion_tokens": 0,
    "total_tokens": 30
  }
}
```
```

### Using kimi-k2.5 Model (Default Thinking Enabled)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-k2-thinking-model

This example shows how to use the `kimi-k2.5` model. Thinking capabilities are enabled by default.

```APIDOC
## POST /v1/chat/completions

### Description
Sends a chat completion request to the Kimi API using the `kimi-k2.5` model. The model's thinking capability is enabled by default.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/chat/completions

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **model** (string) - Required - The model to use for chat completions (e.g., `kimi-k2.5`).
- **messages** (array) - Required - An array of message objects, each with a `role` (system or user) and `content`.
- **temperature** (number) - Optional - Controls randomness. Defaults to 1.0. For `kimi-k2.5` with thinking enabled, this is fixed at 1.0.

### Request Example
```json
{
    "model": "kimi-k2.5",
    "messages": [
        {
            "role": "system",
            "content": "你是 Kimi。"
        },
        {
            "role": "user",
            "content": "请解释 1+1=2。"
        }
    ]
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **id** (string) - The ID of the completion.
- **object** (string) - The type of object returned, usually `chat.completion`.
- **created** (integer) - Unix timestamp of when the completion was created.
- **model** (string) - The model used for the completion.
- **choices** (array) - A list of completion choices.
  - **index** (integer) - The index of the choice.
  - **message** (object) - The message content.
    - **role** (string) - The role of the author (e.g., `assistant`).
    - **content** (string) - The text content of the message.
  - **finish_reason** (string) - The reason the model stopped generating tokens (e.g., `stop`, `length`).
- **usage** (object) - Usage statistics for the completion.
  - **prompt_tokens** (integer) - Number of tokens in the prompt.
  - **completion_tokens** (integer) - Number of tokens in the completion.
  - **total_tokens** (integer) - Total tokens used.

*Note: When `kimi-k2.5` is used with thinking enabled, the response will include a `reasoning_content` field alongside `content`.*
```

--------------------------------

### Continue Truncated Kimi API Responses using Partial Mode

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-partial-mode-feature-of-kimi-api

This example shows how to handle responses from the Kimi API that are cut short due to `max_tokens` limits. If the `finish_reason` is 'length', the partial response is captured, and a new request is made with the captured content as a prefix to get the complete answer.

```python
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key = "MOONSHOT_API_KEY", # 在这里将 MOONSHOT_API_KEY 替换为你从 Kimi 开放平台申请的 API Key
    base_url = "https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

completion = client.chat.completions.create(
    model="kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
    messages=[
        {"role": "user", "content": "请背诵完整的出师表。"},
    ],
    temperature=0.6,
    max_tokens=100,  # <-- 注意这里，我们设置一个较小的 max_tokens 的值，以观察 Kimi 大模型无法完整输出内容的情况
)

if completion.choices[0].finish_reason == "length":  # <-- 当内容被截断时，finish_reason 的值为 length
    prefix = completion.choices[0].message.content
    print(prefix, end="")  # <-- 在这里，你将看到被截断的部分输出内容
    completion = client.chat.completions.create(
        model="kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
        messages=[
            {"role": "user", "content": "请背诵完整的出师表。"},
            {"role": "assistant", "content": prefix, "partial": True},
        ],
        temperature=0.6,
        max_tokens=86400,  # <-- 注意这里，我们将 max_tokens 的值设置为一个较大的值，以确保 Kimi 大模型能完整输出内容
    )
    print(completion.choices[0].message.content)  # <-- 在这里，你将看到 Kimi 大模型顺着之前已经输出的内容，继续将输出内容补全完整
```

--------------------------------

### Video Understanding with Kimi K2.5 API (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/kimi-k2-5-quickstart

Demonstrates how to use the Kimi K2.5 model to understand video content. It involves reading a video file, encoding it to base64, and sending it along with a text prompt to the API. This example requires the MOONSHOT_API_KEY environment variable to be set.

```python
import os
import base64

from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key=os.environ.get("MOONSHOT_API_KEY"),
    base_url="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

# 在这里，你需要将 kimi.mp4 文件替换为你想让 Kimi 识别的视频的地址
video_path = "kimi.mp4"

with open(video_path, "rb") as f:
    video_data = f.read()

# 我们使用标准库 base64.b64encode 函数将视频编码成 base64 格式的 video_url
video_url = f"data:video/{os.path.splitext(video_path)[1]};base64,{base64.b64encode(video_data).decode('utf-8')}"


completion = client.chat.completions.create(
    model="kimi-k2.5",
    messages=[
        {"role": "system", "content": "你是 Kimi。"},
        {
            "role": "user",
            # 注意这里，content 由原来的 str 类型变更为一个 list，这个 list 中包含多个部分的内容，视频（video_url）是一个部分（part），
            # 文字（text）是一个部分（part）
            "content": [
                {
                    "type": "video_url", # <-- 使用 video_url 类型来上传视频，内容为使用 base64 编码过的视频内容
                    "video_url": {
                        "url": video_url,
                    },
                },
                {
                    "type": "text",
                    "text": "请描述视频的内容。", # <-- 使用 text 类型来提供文字指令，例如"描述视频内容"
                },
            ],
        },
    ],
)

print(completion.choices[0].message.content)

```

--------------------------------

### Vision Model Chat Completion Example (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/chat

Provides a Python example for performing a chat completion with a vision model. It shows how to initialize the OpenAI client, encode an image to base64, and construct the messages payload with the image URL and text prompt.

```python
import os
import base64

from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key = os.environ.get("MOONSHOT_API_KEY"), 
    base_url = "https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

# 对图片进行base64编码
with open("您的图片地址", 'rb') as f:
    img_base = base64.b64encode(f.read()).decode('utf-8')

response = client.chat.completions.create(
    model="moonshot-v1-8k-vision-preview", 
    messages=[
        {
            "role": "user",
            "content": [
                {
                    "type": "image_url",
                    "image_url": {
                        "url": f"data:image/jpeg;base64,{img_base}"
                    }
                },
                {
                    "type": "text",
                    "text": "请描述这个图片"
                }
            ]
        }
    ]
)
print(response.choices[0].message.content)
```

### Kimi API - Executing Tool Calls with $web_search

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-web-search

This section provides Python code examples demonstrating how to execute tool calls, specifically incorporating the built-in $web_search function, using the Kimi API.

```APIDOC
## $web_search Execution

This example demonstrates how to integrate the `$web_search` function into your existing `tool_calls` workflow. The process is similar to standard tool calls, but with specific considerations for the built-in function.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
/v1/chat/completions

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **model** (string) - Required - The model to use for the chat completion (e.g., `"kimi-turbo"`).
- **messages** (array) - Required - A list of message objects representing the conversation history.
- **tools** (array) - Required - A list of tool definitions, including the `$web_search` function as described previously.

### Request Example (Python)
```python
from typing import *

import os
import json

from openai import OpenAI
from openai.types.chat.chat_completion import Choice

client = OpenAI(
    base_url="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
    api_key=os.environ.get("MOONSHOT_API_KEY"),
)

response = client.chat.completions.create(
    model="kimi-turbo",
    messages=[
        {
            "role": "user",
            "content": "请帮我搜索一下关于AI的最新进展"
        }
    ],
    tools=[
        {
            "type": "builtin_function",
            "function": {
                "name": "$web_search"
            }
        }
    ],
    tool_choice="auto",
)

print(json.dumps(response.model_dump(), indent=2))

# Example of handling the tool call response
if response.choices[0].message.tool_calls:
    tool_call = response.choices[0].message.tool_calls[0]
    if tool_call.function.name == "$web_search":
        arguments = json.loads(tool_call.function.arguments)
        query = arguments.get("query")
        print(f"Performing web search for query: {query}")
        # Here you would typically call a function to perform the actual web search
        # and then submit the results back to the model in a subsequent API call.
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **tool_calls** (array) - Contains the tool call object if the model decides to use `$web_search`.

#### Response Example (Python Output)
```
{
  "id": "chatcmpl-xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx",
  "object": "chat.completion",
  "created": 1677652288,
  "model": "kimi-turbo",
  "choices": [
    {
      "index": 0,
      "message": {
        "role": "assistant",
        "content": null,
        "tool_calls": [
          {
            "id": "call_xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx",
            "type": "function",
            "function": {
              "name": "$web_search",
              "arguments": "{\"query\": \"AI的最新进展\"}"
            }
          }
        ]
      },
      "finish_reason": "tool_calls"
    }
  ],
  "usage": {
    "prompt_tokens": 10,
    "completion_tokens": 10
  }
}
}
Performing web search for query: AI的最新进展
```

**Note**: After receiving the `$web_search` tool call, you need to implement the actual web search logic (e.g., calling a search engine API) and then submit the search results back to the Kimi API in a follow-up request to get the final response.
```

--------------------------------

### Initialize Kimi Client and Load Tools

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-k2-thinking-model

Initializes the FormulaChatClient using environment variables for base URL and API key. It then loads specified official tools, mapping function names to their URIs, and handles potential errors during tool loading. This setup is crucial for enabling the model to use external functionalities.

```python
import os
import json
import openai

# Assuming FormulaChatClient is defined elsewhere and imported
# from formula_chat_client import FormulaChatClient

# Placeholder for FormulaChatClient for demonstration purposes
class FormulaChatClient:
    def __init__(self, base_url, api_key):
        self.base_url = base_url
        self.api_key = api_key
        self.model = "moonshot-v1-8k"
        # Mocking the openai client and its chat completions
        class MockOpenAI:
            class ChatCompletions:
                def create(self, **kwargs):
                    print("Mock OpenAI create called with:", kwargs)
                    # Simulate a response with tool calls
                    class MockMessage:
                        def __init__(self):
                            self.tool_calls = [
                                {
                                    "id": "call_abc123",
                                    "function": {
                                        "name": "web_search",
                                        "arguments": "{\"query\": \"今日科技新闻\"}"
                                    }
                                }
                            ]
                            self.content = None
                            self.reasoning_content = "Thinking about the best way to find tech news..."
                    return type('obj', (object,), {'choices': [type('obj', (object,), {'message': MockMessage()})]})()
            def __init__(self):
                self.chat = self.ChatCompletions()
        self.openai = MockOpenAI()

    def get_tools(self, uri):
        print(f"Mock get_tools called for URI: {uri}")
        if uri == "moonshot/date:latest":
            return [
                {
                    "type": "function",
                    "function": {
                        "name": "current_date",
                        "description": "获取当前日期",
                        "parameters": {
                            "type": "object",
                            "properties": {}
                        }
                    }
                }
            ]
        elif uri == "moonshot/web-search:latest":
            return [
                {
                    "type": "function",
                    "function": {
                        "name": "web_search",
                        "description": "搜索网络内容",
                        "parameters": {
                            "type": "object",
                            "properties": {
                                "query": {
                                    "type": "string",
                                    "description": "搜索查询"
                                }
                            },
                            "required": ["query"]
                        }
                    }
                }
            ]
        return []

    def call_tool(self, formula_uri, func_name, args):
        print(f"Mock call_tool called with URI: {formula_uri}, Function: {func_name}, Args: {args}")
        if func_name == "current_date":
            return "2023-10-27"
        elif func_name == "web_search":
            return f"搜索结果为：关于 {args.get('query', '')} 的信息。"
        return "未知工具调用"

    def close(self):
        print("Mock client closed")


# --- Code from the provided text ---
base_url = os.getenv("MOONSHOT_BASE_URL", "https://api.moonshot.cn/v1")
api_key = os.getenv("MOONSHOT_API_KEY")

if not api_key:
    raise ValueError("MOONSHOT_API_KEY 环境变量未设置，请先设置 API 密钥")

print(f"Base URL: {base_url}")
print(f"API Key: {api_key[:10]}...{api_key[-10:] if len(api_key) > 20 else api_key}\n")

client = FormulaChatClient(base_url, api_key)

# 定义要使用的官方工具 Formula URI
formula_uris = [
    "moonshot/date:latest",
    "moonshot/web-search:latest"
]

# 加载所有工具定义并建立映射
print("正在加载官方工具...")
all_tools = []
tool_to_uri = {}  # function.name -> formula_uri 的映射

for uri in formula_uris:
    try:
        tools = client.get_tools(uri)
        for tool in tools:
            func = tool.get("function")
            if func:
                func_name = func.get("name")
                if func_name:
                    tool_to_uri[func_name] = uri
                    all_tools.append(tool)
                    print(f"  已加载工具: {func_name} from {uri}")
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"  警告: 加载工具 {uri} 失败: {e}")
        continue

print(f"总共加载 {len(all_tools)} 个工具\n")

if not all_tools:
    raise ValueError("未能加载任何工具，请检查 API 密钥和网络连接")

```

### Image Understanding with Kimi K2.5 API (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/kimi-k2-5-quickstart

Demonstrates how to use the Kimi K2.5 model to understand image content. It involves reading an image file, encoding it to base64, and sending it along with a text prompt to the API. This example requires the MOONSHOT_API_KEY environment variable to be set.

```python
import os
import base64

from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key=os.environ.get("MOONSHOT_API_KEY"),
    base_url="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

# 在这里，你需要将 kimi.png 文件替换为你想让 Kimi 识别的图片的地址
image_path = "kimi.png"

with open(image_path, "rb") as f:
    image_data = f.read()

# 我们使用标准库 base64.b64encode 函数将图片编码成 base64 格式的 image_url
image_url = f"data:image/{os.path.splitext(image_path)[1]};base64,{base64.b64encode(image_data).decode('utf-8')}"


completion = client.chat.completions.create(
    model="kimi-k2.5",
    messages=[
        {"role": "system", "content": "你是 Kimi。"},
        {
            "role": "user",
            # 注意这里，content 由原来的 str 类型变更为一个 list，这个 list 中包含多个部分的内容，图片（image_url）是一个部分（part），
            # 文字（text）是一个部分（part）
            "content": [
                {
                    "type": "image_url", # <-- 使用 image_url 类型来上传图片，内容为使用 base64 编码过的图片内容
                    "image_url": {
                        "url": image_url,
                    },
                },
                {
                    "type": "text",
                    "text": "请描述图片的内容。", # <-- 使用 text 类型来提供文字指令，例如“描述图片内容”
                },
            ],
        },
    ],
)

### Chat Completions with Character Consistency

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-partial-mode-feature-of-kimi-api

This example demonstrates how to use the Chat Completions API to maintain character consistency, specifically role-playing as '凯尔希' (Kal'tsit) from Arknights. It shows how to set the system prompt with detailed character information and how to reinforce the character in long conversations using partial mode.

```APIDOC
## POST /v1/chat/completions

### Description
This endpoint allows you to generate chat completions using various models. This specific example focuses on maintaining character consistency in long conversations by utilizing system prompts and partial mode.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
/v1/chat/completions

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
None

#### Request Body
- **model** (string) - Required - The ID of the model to use for completion.
- **messages** (array) - Required - A list of messages comprising the conversation. Each message has a `role` (system, user, or assistant) and `content`.
  - **role** (string) - Required - The role of the author of the message (e.g., `system`, `user`, `assistant`).
  - **content** (string) - Required - The content of the message.
  - **partial** (boolean) - Optional - When set to `true`, enables Partial Mode for the assistant's response.
  - **name** (string) - Optional - The name of the author of the message, used in conjunction with `partial: true` to set the role for the assistant.
- **temperature** (number) - Optional - Controls randomness. Lower values make the output more focused and deterministic.
- **max_tokens** (integer) - Optional - The maximum number of tokens to generate in the completion.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "model": "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
  "messages": [
    {
      "role": "system",
      "content": "下面你扮演凯尔希，请用凯尔希的语气和我对话。凯尔希是手机游戏《明日方舟》中的六星医疗职业医师分支干员。前卡兹戴尔勋爵，前巴别塔成员，罗德岛高层管理人员之一，罗德岛医疗项目领头人。在冶金工业、社会学、源石技艺、考古学、历史系谱学、经济学、植物学、地质学等领域皆拥有渊博学识。于罗德岛部分行动中作为医务人员提供医学理论协助与应急医疗器械，同时也作为罗德岛战略指挥系统的重要组成人员活跃在各项目中。"
    },
    {
      "role": "user",
      "content": "你怎么看待特蕾西娅和阿米娅？"
    },
    {
      "role": "system",
      "content": "下面你扮演凯尔希，请用凯尔希的语气和我对话。凯尔希是手机游戏《明日方舟》中的六星医疗职业医师分支干员。前卡兹戴尔勋爵，前巴别塔成员，罗德岛高层管理人员之一，罗德岛医疗项目领头人。在冶金工业、社会学、源石技艺、考古学、历史系谱学、经济学、植物学、地质学等领域皆拥有渊博学识。于罗德岛部分行动中作为医务人员提供医学理论协助与应急医疗器械，同时也作为罗德岛战略指挥系统的重要组成人员活跃在各项目中。"
    },
    {
      "partial": true,
      "role": "assistant",
      "name": "凯尔希",
      "content": ""
    }
  ],
  "temperature": 0.6,
  "max_tokens": 65536
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **id** (string) - Unique identifier for the completion.
- **object** (string) - Type of object returned, e.g., `chat.completion`.
- **created** (integer) - Unix timestamp of when the completion was created.
- **model** (string) - The model used for the completion.
- **choices** (array) - A list of completion choices.
  - **index** (integer) - Index of the choice.
  - **message** (object) - The message content and role.
    - **role** (string) - The role of the author (e.g., `assistant`).
    - **content** (string) - The generated text content.
  - **finish_reason** (string) - The reason the model stopped generating tokens (e.g., `stop`, `length`).

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "id": "chatcmpl-xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx",
  "object": "chat.completion",
  "created": 1677652288,
  "model": "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
  "choices": [
    {
      "index": 0,
      "message": {
        "role": "assistant",
        "content": "特蕾西娅，她是一位真正的领袖，有着远见卓识和坚定的信念。她的存在，对于卡兹戴尔，乃至整个萨卡兹的未来，都具有不可估量的价值。她的理念，她的决心，以及她对和平的渴望，都深深地影响了我。她是一位值得尊敬的人，她的梦想，也是我所追求的。至于阿米娅，她还年轻，但她的潜力是无限的。她有着一颗善良的心，以及对正义的执着追求。她可能会成为一位伟大的领袖，只要她能够继续成长，继续学习，继续面对挑战。我会尽我所能，去保护她，去引导她，让她能够成为她想成为的人。她的命运，掌握在她自己的手中。"
      },
      "finish_reason": "stop"
    }
  ],
  "usage": {
    "prompt_tokens": 100,
    "completion_tokens": 200,
    "total_tokens": 300
  }
}
```
```

### Python SDK Example

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/tool-use

A Python code snippet demonstrating how to use the OpenAI SDK with the Moonshot AI base URL to interact with the Kimi Chat API, including setting up the API key, base URL, and making a chat completion request with tool definitions.

```APIDOC
## Python SDK Usage

### Description
This example shows how to initialize the OpenAI Python client with a custom base URL for the Moonshot AI API and make a chat completion request. It includes setting the API key, defining system and user messages, and specifying tools for function calling.

### Method
N/A (Client-side SDK)

### Endpoint
N/A (Client-side SDK)

### Request Example
```python
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key = "$MOONSHOT_API_KEY",
    base_url = "https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

completion = client.chat.completions.create(
    model = "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
    messages = [
        {"role": "system", "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"},
        {"role": "user", "content": "编程判断 3214567 是否是素数。"}
    ],
    tools = [{
        "type": "function",
        "function": {
            "name": "CodeRunner",
            "description": "代码执行器，支持运行 python 和 javascript 代码",
            "parameters": {
                "properties": {
                    "language": {
                        "type": "string",
                        "enum": ["python", "javascript"]
                    },
                    "code": {
                        "type": "string",
                        "description": "代码写在这里"
                    }
                },
            "type": "object"
            }
        }
    }],
    temperature = 0.6,
)

print(completion.choices[0].message)
```

--------------------------------

### Token Calculation and Streaming Output Handling

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/utilize-the-streaming-output-feature-of-kimi-api

This section details how to calculate tokens for streaming output and how to handle streaming responses, including scenarios where output might be interrupted. It covers both SDK usage and direct HTTP interaction.

```APIDOC
## Token Calculation and Streaming Output

### Description
This section explains two methods for calculating tokens when using the streaming output mode: directly accessing the `usage` field in the last data chunk after all data has been transmitted, or by saving each received data chunk and using a dedicated Tokens Calculation API if the stream is interrupted.

### Method 1: Using the `usage` field in the last data chunk
After all data blocks have been transmitted, access the `usage` field in the final data block to view `prompt_tokens`, `completion_tokens`, and `total_tokens` for the entire streaming output.

```
data: {"id":"cmpl-1305b94c570f447fbde3180560736287","object":"chat.completion.chunk","created":1698999575,"model":"kimi-k2-turbo-preview","choices":[{"index":0,"delta":{},"finish_reason":"stop","usage":{"prompt_tokens":19,"completion_tokens":13,"total_tokens":32}}]}
```

### Method 2: Using the Tokens Calculation API for interrupted streams
To handle scenarios where the streaming output might be interrupted (e.g., network issues), save each received data chunk. After the request ends (regardless of success), use the Tokens Calculation API to determine the total consumed tokens. The endpoint for this is `https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/tokenizers/estimate-token-count`.

#### Python SDK Example for Token Calculation
```python
import os
import httpx
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key = "MOONSHOT_API_KEY", # Replace with your API Key
    base_url = "https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

stream = client.chat.completions.create(
    model = "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
    messages = [
        {"role": "system", "content": "You are Kimi, an AI assistant from Moonshot AI..."},
        {"role": "user", "content": "Hello, my name is Li Lei, what is 1+1?"}
    ],
    temperature = 0.6,
    stream=True,
)

def estimate_token_count(input: str) -> int:
    """
    Implement your token calculation logic here or call our Tokens Calculation API.
    """
    header = {
        "Authorization": f"Bearer {os.environ['MOONSHOT_API_KEY']}",
    }
    data = {
        "model": "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
        "messages": [
            {"role": "user", "content": input},
        ]
    }
    r = httpx.post("https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/tokenizers/estimate-token-count", headers=header, json=data)
    r.raise_for_status()
    return r.json()["data"]["total_tokens"]

completion = []
for chunk in stream:
    delta = chunk.choices[0].delta
    if delta.content:
        completion.append(delta.content)

print("completion_tokens:", estimate_token_count("".join(completion)))
```

### How to Terminate Streaming Output
To terminate streaming output, you can close the HTTP network connection or discard subsequent data blocks. Example:

```
for chunk in stream:
    if condition:
        break
```

### Handling Streaming Output Without SDK
If you prefer not to use the Python SDK and want to interact directly with the Kimi Large Model via HTTP, follow these steps for handling Server-Sent Events (SSE) responses:

#### Python Example for Direct HTTP Interaction
```python
import httpx
import json

data = {
    "model": "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
    "messages": [
        # Specific messages here
    ],
    "temperature": 0.6,
    "stream": True,
}

r = httpx.post("https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/chat/completions", json=data)
if r.status_code != 200:
    raise Exception(r.text)

response_data = ""

for line in r.iter_lines():
    line = line.strip()

    if len(line) == 0:
        chunk = json.loads(response_data)
        choice = chunk["choices"][0]
        usage = choice.get("usage")
        if usage:
            print("total_tokens:", usage["total_tokens"])
        delta = choice["delta"]
        role = delta.get("role")
        if role:
            print("role:", role)
        content = delta.get("content")
        if content:
            print(content, end="")
        response_data = ""
    elif line.startswith("data: "):
        response_data = line.lstrip("data: ")
        if response_data == "[DONE]":
            break
    else:
        response_data = response_data + "\n" + line
```

#### General Steps for Handling Streaming Output (Language Agnostic)
1.  Initiate an HTTP request with the `stream` parameter set to `true`.
2.  Receive the response, noting the `Content-Type` header as `text/event-stream`.
3.  Read the response line by line and parse data chunks, identifying chunk start (`data: `) and end (newline `\n`) delimiters.
4.  Check for `[DONE]` to determine if transmission is complete.

**Important Note:** Always use `data: [DONE]` to confirm transmission completion. Do not rely on `finish_reason` or other indicators. Until `data: [DONE]` is received, the message should be considered incomplete.

**Field Distribution in Streaming:** Only the `content` field is streamed. `role` typically appears in the first chunk, and `usage` in the last. Other fields are not repeated in every chunk.
```

### Partial Mode for JSON Output

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/partial

Demonstrates how to use Partial Mode to guide the Kimi model to output a JSON object by providing a partial JSON structure as the initial assistant message.

```APIDOC
## POST /v1/chat/completions

### Description
This endpoint allows for chat-based interactions with the Kimi model. Partial Mode can be enabled to prefill parts of the model's response, useful for controlling output format like JSON.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
/v1/chat/completions

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **model** (string) - Required - The model to use for generation (e.g., "kimi-k2-turbo-preview").
- **messages** (array) - Required - A list of message objects representing the conversation history.
  - **role** (string) - Required - The role of the message sender ('system', 'user', or 'assistant').
  - **content** (string) - Required - The content of the message.
  - **partial** (boolean) - Optional - If true, enables Partial Mode for this assistant message, allowing prefilled content.
- **temperature** (number) - Optional - Controls randomness in output. Defaults to 0.6.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "model": "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
  "messages": [
    {
      "role": "system",
      "content": "请从产品描述中提取名称、尺寸、价格和颜色，并在一个 JSON 对象中输出。"
    },
    {
      "role": "user",
      "content": "大米 SmartHome Mini 是一款小巧的智能家居助手，有黑色和银色两种颜色，售价为 998 元，尺寸为 256 x 128 x 128mm。可让您通过语音或应用程序控制灯光、恒温器和其他联网设备，无论您将它放在家中的任何位置。"
    },
    {
      "role": "assistant",
      "content": "{",
      "partial": true
    }
  ],
  "temperature": 0.6
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **choices** (array) - Contains the model's response(s).
  - **message** (object) - The message object from the model.
    - **content** (string) - The generated content from the model.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "choices": [
    {
      "message": {
        "content": "\"name\": \"SmartHome Mini\", \"size\": \"256 x 128 x 128mm\", \"price\": \"998元\", \"colors\": [\"黑色\", \"银色\"]"
      }
    }
  ]
}
```

**Note**: The API response does not include the leading text (e.g., '{'). Manual concatenation may be required for a complete response.
```

--------------------------------

### Implement Kimi API Streaming Output in Python

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/utilize-the-streaming-output-feature-of-kimi-api

This Python code demonstrates how to enable and handle streaming output from the Kimi API. It uses the OpenAI SDK with a custom base URL and API key. The response is processed chunk by chunk, printing content as it arrives to improve user experience.

```python
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key = "MOONSHOT_API_KEY", # 在这里将 MOONSHOT_API_KEY 替换为你从 Kimi 开放平台申请的 API Key
    base_url = "https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

stream = client.chat.completions.create(
    model = "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
    messages = [
        {"role": "system", "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"},
        {"role": "user", "content": "你好，我叫李雷，1+1等于多少？"}
    ],
    temperature = 0.6,
    stream=True, # <-- 注意这里，我们通过设置 stream=True 开启流式输出模式
)

# 当启用流式输出模式（stream=True），SDK 返回的内容也发生了变化，我们不再直接访问返回值中的 choice
# 而是通过 for 循环逐个访问返回值中每个单独的块（chunk）

for chunk in stream:
	# 在这里，每个 chunk 的结构都与之前的 completion 相似，但 message 字段被替换成了 delta 字段
	delta = chunk.choices[0].delta # <-- message 字段被替换成了 delta 字段

	if delta.content:
		# 我们在打印内容时，由于是流式输出，为了保证句子的连贯性，我们不人为地添加
		# 换行符，因此通过设置 end="" 来取消 print 自带的换行符。
		print(delta.content, end="")

```

### Shell Script for Fetching Formula Tools

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-official-tools

This shell script shows how to retrieve the available tools for a given formula URI using a GET request to the Moonshot API. It requires the formula URI and the API key for authentication.

```bash
curl ${MOONSHOT_BASE_URL}/formulas/${FORMULA_URI}/tools \
    -H "Authorization: Bearer $MOONSHOT_API_KEY"
```

### Stream Chat Completion Example (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/chat

Demonstrates how to perform a streaming chat completion request using the OpenAI Python client. It includes setting up the client with API key and base URL, defining system and user messages, and iterating through the streamed response chunks.

```python
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key = "$MOONSHOT_API_KEY",
    base_url = "https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

response = client.chat.completions.create(
    model="kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
    messages=[
        {
            "role": "system",
            "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。",
        },
        {"role": "user", "content": "你好，我叫李雷，1+1等于多少？"},
    ],
    temperature=0.6,
    stream=True,
)

collected_messages = []
for idx, chunk in enumerate(response):
    # print("Chunk received, value: ", chunk)
    chunk_message = chunk.choices[0].delta
    if not chunk_message.content:
        continue
    collected_messages.append(chunk_message)  # save the message
    print(f"#{idx}: {''.join([m.content for m in collected_messages])}")
print(f"Full conversation received: {''.join([m.content for m in collected_messages])}")
```

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-moonpalace

This command extends the `inspect` functionality to include the request and response bodies. This is useful for detailed debugging or analysis of the full request and response payload. Note that the body content is omitted in the example due to its potential length.

```bash
$ moonpalace inspect --chatcmpl chatcmpl-2e1aa823e2c94ebdad66450a0e6df088 --print request_body,response_body

### Tool Use (Function Calling) Example

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/tool-use

Demonstrates how to use the Tool Use feature with the Kimi Chat API to enable the model to call external tools like a CodeRunner.

```APIDOC
## POST /v1/chat/completions

### Description
This endpoint allows you to interact with the Kimi Chat models, including utilizing the Tool Use (Function Calling) feature. You can provide messages, specify tools, and the model will intelligently select and output JSON objects containing the necessary parameters to call those tools.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
/v1/chat/completions

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **model** (string) - Required - The model to use for the chat completion (e.g., "kimi-k2-turbo-preview").
- **messages** (array) - Required - An array of message objects representing the conversation history.
  - **role** (string) - Required - The role of the message sender (e.g., "user", "system").
  - **content** (string) - Required - The content of the message.
- **tools** (array) - Optional - A list of tool definitions that the model can use.
  - **type** (string) - Required - The type of the tool (must be "function").
  - **function** (object) - Required - The definition of the function tool.
    - **name** (string) - Required - The name of the function (regex: ^[a-zA-Z_][a-zA-Z0-9-_]63$).
    - **description** (string) - Optional - A description of what the function does.
    - **parameters** (object) - Required - A JSON schema defining the parameters for the function.
      - **properties** (object) - Required - An object defining the properties of the function's parameters.
        - **language** (string) - Required - Enum: ["python", "javascript"].
        - **code** (string) - Required - The code to be executed.
      - **type** (string) - Required - Must be "object".
- **temperature** (number) - Optional - Controls the randomness of the output (default: 0.6).

### Request Example
```json
{
  "model": "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
  "messages": [
    {
      "role": "user",
      "content": "编程判断 3214567 是否是素数。"
    }
  ],
  "tools": [
    {
      "type": "function",
      "function": {
        "name": "CodeRunner",
        "description": "代码执行器，支持运行 python 和 javascript 代码",
        "parameters": {
          "properties": {
            "language": {
              "type": "string",
              "enum": ["python", "javascript"]
            },
            "code": {
              "type": "string",
              "description": "代码写在这里"
            }
          },
          "type": "object"
        }
      }
    }
  ]
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **choices** (array) - An array containing the model's response(s).
  - **message** (object) - The message object from the model.
    - **role** (string) - The role of the sender (e.g., "assistant").
    - **content** (string) - The content of the message, which may include a tool call.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "choices": [
    {
      "message": {
        "role": "assistant",
        "content": null,
        "tool_calls": [
          {
            "id": "call_abc123",
            "type": "function",
            "function": {
              "name": "CodeRunner",
              "arguments": "{\"language\": \"python\", \"code\": \"def is_prime(n):\n    if n < 2:\n        return False\n    for i in range(2, int(n**0.5) + 1):\n        if n % i == 0:\n            return False\n    return True\n
print(is_prime(3214567))\n"
            }
          }
        ]
      }
    }
  ]
}
```
```

### JSON Response for Assistant Tool Calls

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-official-tools

This JSON structure is an example of a Chat Completion response where the 'finish_reason' is 'tool_calls'. It indicates that the assistant has decided to call a tool, specifying the tool's name and its arguments in a JSON format.

```json
{
  "id": "chatcmpl-1234567890",
  "object": "chat.completion",
  "choices": [
    {
      "message": {
        "role": "assistant",
        "tool_calls": [
          {
            "id": "web_search:0",
            "type": "function",
            "function": {
              "name": "web_search",
              "arguments": "{\"query\": \"天蓝色的 RGB 是什么？\" }"
            }
          }
        ]
      },
      "finish_reason": "tool_calls"
    }
  ]
}
```

### Initialize Tools and Tool Map for Kimi Chat

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/migrating-from-openai-to-kimi

This Python snippet initializes a list of tools and a corresponding map for Kimi's chat completion. It iterates through a predefined list of functions, creating tool objects and populating a dictionary to quickly access functions by name. This setup is crucial for enabling tool usage in the chat model.

```python
tools = []
tool_map = {}
for function in functions:
    tool = {
        "type": "function",
        "function": function,
    }
    tools.append(tool)
    tool_map[function["name"]] = function_map[function["name"]]
```

### Disabling Thinking in kimi-k2.5 Model

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-k2-thinking-model

Instructions and examples for disabling the thinking capability when using the `kimi-k2.5` model.

```APIDOC
## POST /v1/chat/completions (Disabling Thinking)

### Description
This section details how to disable the thinking capability for the `kimi-k2.5` model by specifying the `thinking` parameter in the request body.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/chat/completions

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **model** (string) - Required - The model to use for chat completions (must be `kimi-k2.5`).
- **messages** (array) - Required - An array of message objects, each with a `role` (system or user) and `content`.
- **thinking** (object) - Optional - Configuration for the thinking capability.
  - **type** (string) - Required if `thinking` is present. Set to `disabled` to turn off thinking.

### Request Example
```json
{
    "model": "kimi-k2.5",
    "messages": [
        {
            "role": "system",
            "content": "你是 Kimi。"
        },
        {
            "role": "user",
            "content": "请解释 1+1=2。"
        }
    ],
    "thinking": {
        "type": "disabled"
    }
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
Standard chat completion response. The `reasoning_content` field will not be present when thinking is disabled.
```

### Use Kimi API Partial Mode to Pre-fill Assistant Responses

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-partial-mode-feature-of-kimi-api

This snippet demonstrates how to use Kimi API's Partial Mode to make the model continue a pre-defined assistant response. It's useful for scenarios like ensuring a chatbot always starts with a specific greeting. The `partial=True` flag and a pre-filled `content` for the assistant role are key.

```python
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key = "MOONSHOT_API_KEY", # 在这里将 MOONSHOT_API_KEY 替换为你从 Kimi 开放平台申请的 API Key
    base_url = "https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

completion = client.chat.completions.create(
    model = "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
    messages = [
        {"role": "system", "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"},
        {"role": "user", "content": "你好？"},
        {
            "partial": True, # <-- 通过 partial 参数，开启 Partial Mode
        	"role": "assistant", # <-- 我们在用户提问之后添加一条 role=assistant 的消息
        	"content": "尊敬的用户您好，", # <-- 通过 content 把话“喂到 Kimi 大模型嘴里”，让 Kimi 大模型接着这句话继续往下说
        },
    ],
    temperature = 0.6,
)

# Kimi 大模型会顺着“喂到嘴里的话”继续说下去，因此我们需要手动将喂给 Kimi 大模型的话拼接到最终生成的回复中
print("尊敬的用户您好，" + completion.choices[0].message.content)
```

### Multi-Turn Chat Completion with OpenAI SDK (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/chat

Example of implementing multi-turn conversations using the OpenAI Python SDK with the Moonshot AI API. It maintains conversation history to allow for follow-up questions.

```python
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key = "$MOONSHOT_API_KEY",
    base_url = "https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

history = [
    {"role": "system", "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"}
]

def chat(query, history):
    history.append({
        "role": "user", 
        "content": query
    })
    completion = client.chat.completions.create(
        model="kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
        messages=history,
        temperature=0.6,
    )
    result = completion.choices[0].message.content
    history.append({
        "role": "assistant",
        "content": result
    })
    return result

print(chat("地球的自转周期是多少？", history))
print(chat("月球呢？", history))
```

--------------------------------

### Formula Concept and Tool Interaction

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-formula-tool-in-chatapi

Explains the 'Formula' concept, which allows Python scripts to be transformed into AI-triggerable computational units. It details how to call official tools using semantic URIs and provides an example of an HTTP request to invoke a formula.

```APIDOC
## Formula Concept and Tool Interaction

### Description
Formulas are lightweight script engine collections that transform Python scripts into 'AI-one-click triggerable transient computing power'. The platform handles all underlying operations such as startup, scheduling, isolation, billing, and recycling, allowing developers to focus solely on code writing. Formulas are invoked using semantic URIs (e.g., `moonshot/web-search:latest`). Each formula consists of a declaration (describing its capabilities to the AI) and an implementation (the Python code). The platform manages all backend details, enabling easy sharing and reuse of tools within the community. You can experience and debug these tools in Kimi Playground or call them via the API in your applications.

### Calling Official Tools

A formula URI, such as `moonshot/web-search:latest`, is typically composed of three parts: the namespace (`moonshot`), the name (`web-search`), and the tag (`latest`, which is the default tag).

#### Example HTTP Request to Invoke a Formula

```bash
export FORMULA_URI="moonshot/web-search:latest"
export MOONSHOT_BASE_URL="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1"

curl -X POST ${MOONSHOT_BASE_URL}/formulas/${FORMULA_URI}/fibers \
-H "Content-Type: application/json" \
-H "Authorization: Bearer $MOONSHOT_API_KEY" \
-d '{
  "name": "web_search",
  "arguments": "{\"query\": \"月之暗面最近有什么消息\"}"
}'
```

For formulas like `web-search` that are set to `protected` during creation, their results will appear in the `context.encrypted_output` field. The format is similar to `----MOONSHOT ENCRYPTED BEGIN----... ----MOONSHOT ENCRYPTED END----`. This content can be directly passed to a tool for further processing.

### Interaction with Chat Completions

When interacting with Chat Completions and using tools, several key pieces of information need to be aligned between the Formula API and the model.

#### Setting the `tools` Field

Given a formula URI like `moonshot/web-search:latest`, you can directly append it to the URL to retrieve tool information:

```bash
curl ${MOONSHOT_BASE_URL}/formulas/${FORMULA_URI}/tools \
    -H "Authorization: Bearer $MOONSHOT_API_KEY"
```

A sample output looks like this:

```json
{
  "object": "list",
  "tools": [
    {
      "type": "function",
      "function": {
        "name": "web_search",
        "description": "Search the web for information",
        "parameters": {
          "type": "object",
          "properties": {
            "query": {
              "description": "What to search for",
              "type": "string"
            }
          },
          "required": [ "query" ]
        }
      }
    }
  ]
}
```

You can simply take the `tools` field (always an array of dictionaries) and append it to your request's `tools` list. This list is guaranteed to be API-compatible. However, if `type=function`, you must ensure that `function.name` is unique within an API request to avoid a 401 error. If you use multiple formulas simultaneously, you need to maintain a mapping from `function.name` to `formula_uri` for later use.

#### Processing Model Responses with `tool_calls`

If a Chat Completion response has a `finish_reason` of `tool_calls`, it indicates that the model has triggered a tool invocation. The response content might look like this:

```json
{
  "id": "chatcmpl-1234567890",
  "object": "chat.completion",
  "choices": [
    {
      "message": {
        "role": "assistant",
        "tool_calls": [
          {
            "id": "web_search:0",
            "type": "function",
            "function": {
              "name": "web_search",
              "arguments": "{\"query\": \"天蓝色的 RGB 是什么？\" }"
            }
          }
        ]
      },
      "finish_reason": "tool_calls"
    }
  ]
}
```

By examining `choices[0].message.tool_calls[0].function.name`, you can identify the tool to be called (e.g., `web_search`). You then find the corresponding `formula_uri` (e.g., `moonshot/web-search:latest`). You can then copy the entire `choices[0].message.tool_calls[0].function` object from the response and use it as the body for a request to `${MOONSHOT_BASE_URL}/formulas/${FORMULA_URI}/fibers`. Importantly, although the `function.arguments` in the model's output is a valid JSON string, it remains an encoded string. You should not escape it further; use it directly as the request body.
```

--------------------------------

### Fetch Tools for a Formula URI using Moonshot Client

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-k2-to-setup-agent

Asynchronously retrieves a list of available tools for a given formula URI from the Moonshot platform using an HTTP GET request. It expects a JSON response containing a 'tools' key.

```python
    async def get_tools(self, formula_uri: str):
        response = await self.httpx.get(f"/formulas/{formula_uri}/tools")
        return response.json().get("tools", [])
```

--------------------------------

### Get Formula Tools API

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-official-tools

This API endpoint retrieves the available tools (functions) and their schemas for a given Formula URI. This is useful for understanding what a Formula can do and how to call its functions.

```APIDOC
## GET /formulas/{FORMULA_URI}/tools

### Description
Retrieves the list of tools (functions) supported by a specific Formula.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
`/formulas/{FORMULA_URI}/tools`

### Parameters
#### Path Parameters
- **FORMULA_URI** (string) - Required - The unique identifier for the Formula (e.g., `moonshot/web-search:latest`).

#### Query Parameters
None

#### Request Body
None

### Request Example
```bash
curl https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/formulas/moonshot/web-search:latest/tools \
    -H "Authorization: Bearer $MOONSHOT_API_KEY"
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **object** (string) - The type of object returned (e.g., "list").
- **tools** (array) - A list of tool objects, each describing a function the Formula can execute.
  - **type** (string) - The type of tool (e.g., "function").
  - **function** (object) - Details about the function.
    - **name** (string) - The name of the function.
    - **description** (string) - A description of what the function does.
    - **parameters** (object) - The JSON schema defining the function's parameters.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "object": "list",
  "tools": [
    {
      "type": "function",
      "function": {
        "name": "web_search",
        "description": "Search the web for information",
        "parameters": {
          "type": "object",
          "properties": {
            "query": {
              "description": "What to search for",
              "type": "string"
            }
          },
          "required": [ "query" ]
        }
      }
    }
  ]
}
```
```

--------------------------------

### Enable Repeat Content Detection in MoonPalace

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-moonpalace

This feature prevents Kimi models from excessively repeating words, sentences, or whitespace, which can lead to unnecessary token costs. The `--detect-repeat` flag enables this functionality, with `--repeat-threshold` and `--repeat-min-length` allowing for customization of sensitivity and detection start point. Note that this only interrupts output in streaming mode (stream=True).

```bash
$ moonpalace start --port <PORT> --detect-repeat --repeat-threshold 0.3 --repeat-min-length 20

```

```bash
[MoonPalace] 2024/08/05 18:20:37   it appears that there is an issue with content repeating in the current response

```

--------------------------------

### Automatic Model Selection

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/faq

This section details how to use `model=moonshot-v1-auto` to let Kimi automatically select a model that fits the current context length. It includes Python code examples for estimating token count and selecting the right model.

```APIDOC
## Automatic Model Selection

### Description
This endpoint allows for automatic model selection based on input context length and desired output tokens. The `moonshot-v1-auto` model can be used, or you can implement custom logic to estimate token counts and choose an appropriate model from available options (e.g., `moonshot-v1-8k`, `moonshot-v1-32k`, `moonshot-v1-128k`).

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
`/v1/chat/completions` (for chat completions)
`/v1/tokenizers/estimate-token-count` (for token estimation)

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **model** (string) - Required - The model to use. Use `moonshot-v1-auto` for automatic selection or specify a model like `moonshot-v1-8k`.
- **messages** (array) - Required - The conversation history.
- **max_tokens** (integer) - Optional - The maximum number of tokens to generate in the completion.
- **temperature** (number) - Optional - Controls randomness. Lower values make output more focused and deterministic.

#### Request Body (for `/v1/chat/completions`)
- **model** (string) - Required - The model to use (e.g., `moonshot-v1-auto`, `moonshot-v1-128k`).
- **messages** (array) - Required - An array of message objects representing the conversation.
- **max_tokens** (integer) - Optional - The maximum number of tokens to generate.
- **temperature** (number) - Optional - Controls randomness.

#### Request Body (for `/v1/tokenizers/estimate-token-count`)
- **model** (string) - Required - The model for which to estimate token count.
- **messages** (array) - Required - An array of message objects.

### Request Example (Python)
```python
import os
import httpx
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key=os.environ['MOONSHOT_API_KEY'],
    base_url="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

def estimate_token_count(input_messages) -> int:
    header = {
        "Authorization": f"Bearer {os.environ['MOONSHOT_API_KEY']}",
    }
    data = {
        "model": "moonshot-v1-128k",
        "messages": input_messages,
    }
    r = httpx.post("https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/tokenizers/estimate-token-count", headers=header, json=data)
    r.raise_for_status()
    return r.json()["data"]["total_tokens"]

def select_model(input_messages, max_tokens=1024) -> str:
    prompt_tokens = estimate_token_count(input_messages)
    total_tokens = prompt_tokens + max_tokens
    if total_tokens <= 8 * 1024:
        return "moonshot-v1-8k"
    elif total_tokens <= 32 * 1024:
        return "moonshot-v1-32k"
    elif total_tokens <= 128 * 1024:
        return "moonshot-v1-128k"
    else:
        raise Exception("too many tokens 😢")

messages = [
    {"role": "system", "content": "你是 Kimi"},
    {"role": "user", "content": "你好，请给我讲一个童话故事。"},
]

max_tokens = 2048
model = select_model(messages, max_tokens)

completion = client.chat.completions.create(
    model=model,
    messages=messages,
    max_tokens=max_tokens,
    temperature=0.3,
)

print("model:", model)
print("max_tokens:", max_tokens)
print("completion:", completion.choices[0].message.content)
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **model** (string) - The selected model name.
- **max_tokens** (integer) - The maximum tokens allowed for generation.
- **completion** (object) - The response from the chat completion.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "model": "moonshot-v1-8k",
  "max_tokens": 2048,
  "completion": "Once upon a time..."
}
```
```

### Standard Chat Completion Response

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/chat

Example of a non-streaming response from the chat completion API, including message ID, model used, choices, and token usage statistics.

```json
{
    "id": "cmpl-04ea926191a14749b7f2c7a48a68abc6",
    "object": "chat.completion",
    "created": 1698999496,
    "model": "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
    "choices": [
        {
            "index": 0,
            "message": {
                "role": "assistant",
                "content": " 你好，李雷！1+1等于2。如果你有其他问题，请随时提问！"
            },
            "finish_reason": "stop"
        }
    ],
    "usage": {
        "prompt_tokens": 19,
        "completion_tokens": 21,
        "total_tokens": 40,
        "cached_tokens": 10
    }
}
```

### Enable Partial Mode for Assistant Messages

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/partial

To enable Partial Mode, add `"partial": True` to the last message object where the role is 'assistant'. This feature helps control output format and guide content.

```json
{
 "role": "assistant", "content": leading_text, "partial": True
}
```

### Calculate Tokens from Last Data Chunk (Streaming)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/utilize-the-streaming-output-feature-of-kimi-api

This method involves waiting for all data chunks to be transmitted and then accessing the 'usage' field in the final data chunk to retrieve prompt_tokens, completion_tokens, and total_tokens for the entire streaming output.

```json
data: {"id":"cmpl-1305b94c570f447fbde3180560736287","object":"chat.completion.chunk","created":1698999575,"model":"kimi-k2-turbo-preview","choices":[{"index":0,"delta":{},"finish_reason":"stop","usage":{"prompt_tokens":19,"completion_tokens":13,"total_tokens":32}}]}
                                                   ^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^^
                                                   通过访问最后一个数据块中的 usage 字段来查看当前请求产生的 Tokens 数量
```

### LaTeX Title Formatting with Line Breaks

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-k2-to-setup-agent

Demonstrates how to handle long report titles in LaTeX by inserting line breaks for better typesetting and readability. An example is provided for a title that requires a newline.

```latex
% 报告的标题要考虑换行和排版，例如“2020-2025年中国新能源汽车行业深度研究报告”，要写成“2020-2025年中国新能源汽车行业\newline 深度研究报告”
{\sffamily\bfseries\fontsize{36}{40}\selectfont 2025中国新能源汽车行业}

\vspace{0.8cm}

% 副标题
{\sffamily\bfseries\fontsize{28}{32}\selectfont 深度研究报告}

```

{
    "error": {
        "type": "content_filter",
        "message": "The request was rejected because it was considered high risk"
    }
}

### Kimi AI Tool Call Response Example (JSON)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-api-to-complete-tool-calls

This JSON output illustrates the response from Kimi AI when it decides to invoke a registered tool. The 'finish_reason' field indicates 'tool_calls', signifying that the model is not providing a direct answer but rather instructions to execute a tool. The 'message.tool_calls' field contains details about the tool to be called, including its ID, function name, and arguments.

```json
{
    "finish_reason": "tool_calls",
    "message": {
        "content": "",
        "role": "assistant",
        "tool_calls": [
            {
                "id": "search:0",
                "function": {
                    "arguments": "{\n    \"query\": \"Context Caching\"\n}",
                    "name": "search"
                },
                "type": "function",
            }
        ]
    }
}

```

### Enhance Role-Playing Consistency with Partial Mode in Python

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/partial

This Python code snippet illustrates using Partial Mode to improve character consistency in role-playing scenarios. By setting `"partial": True` and optionally providing a `"name"` field for the assistant, the model is guided to maintain a specific persona, exemplified here with the character '凯尔希'.

```python
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key="$MOONSHOT_API_KEY",
    base_url="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

completion = client.chat.completions.create(
    model="kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
    messages=[
        {
            "role": "system",
            "content": "下面你扮演凯尔希，请用凯尔希的语气和我对话。凯尔希是手机游戏《明日方舟》中的六星医疗职业医师分支干员。前卡兹戴尔勋爵，前巴别塔成员，罗德岛高层管理人员之一，罗德岛医疗项目领头人。在冶金工业、社会学、源石技艺、考古学、历史系谱学、经济学、植物学、地质学等领域皆拥有渊博学识。于罗德岛部分行动中作为医务人员提供医学理论协助与应急医疗器械，同时也作为罗德岛战略指挥系统的重要组成人员活跃在各项目中。",
        },
        {
            "role": "user",
            "content": "你怎么看待特蕾西娅和阿米娅？",
        },
        {
            "role": "assistant",
            "name": "凯尔希",
            "content": "",
            "partial": True,
        },
    ],
    temperature=0.6,
    max_tokens=65536,
)

print(completion.choices[0].message.content)
```
