### Terminate Streaming Output

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/utilize-the-streaming-output-feature-of-kimi-api

Streaming output can be terminated by closing the HTTP network connection or by discarding subsequent data chunks. The provided code snippet demonstrates breaking out of the loop if a specific condition is met.

```python
for chunk in stream:
	if condition:
		break
```

--------------------------------

### Process Streamed Output with n>1 in Python

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/utilize-the-streaming-output-feature-of-kimi-api

This Python snippet demonstrates how to handle streamed API responses when requesting multiple outputs (n>1). It uses the httpx library to make the request and then iterates through the streamed lines, parsing JSON chunks and assembling responses based on the 'index' provided in each chunk. It handles empty lines, 'data: ' prefixes, and the '[DONE]' signal.

```python
import httpx
import json

data = {
	"model": "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
	"messages": [
		# 具体的 messages
	],
	"temperature": 0.6,
	"stream": True,
	"n": 2, # <-- 注意这里，我们要求 Kimi 大模型输出 2 个回复
}

# 使用 httpx 向 Kimi 大模型发出 chat 请求，并获得响应 r
r = httpx.post("https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/chat/completions", json=data)
if r.status_code != 200:
	raise Exception(r.text)


data: str

# 在这里，我们预先构建一个 List，用于存放不同的回复消息，由于我们设置了 n=2，因此我们将 List 初始化为 2 个元素
messages = [{}, {}]

# 在这里，我们使用了 iter_lines 方法来逐行读取响应体
for line in r.iter_lines():
	# 去除每一行收尾的空格，以便更好地处理数据块
	line = line.strip()

	# 接下来我们要处理三种不同的情况：
	#   1. 如果当前行是空行，则表明前一个数据块已接收完毕（即前文提到的，通过两个换行符结束数据块传输），我们可以对该数据块进行反序列化，并打印出对应的 content 内容；
	#   2. 如果当前行为非空行，且以 data: 开头，则表明这是一个数据块传输的开始，我们去除 data: 前缀后，首先判断是否是结束符 [DONE]，如果不是，将数据内容保存到 data 变量；
	#   3. 如果当前行为非空行，但不以 data: 开头，则表明当前行仍然归属上一个正在传输的数据块，我们将当前行的内容追加到 data 变量尾部；

	if len(line) == 0:
		chunk = json.loads(data)

		# 通过循环获取每个数据块中所有的 choice，并获取 index 对应的 message 对象
		for choice in chunk["choices"]:
			index = choice["index"]
			message = messages[index]
			usage = choice.get("usage")
			if usage:
				message["usage"] = usage
			delta = choice["delta"]
			role = delta.get("role")
			if role:
				message["role"] = role
			content = delta.get("content")
			if content:
				message["content"] = message["content"] + content

			data = "" # 重置 data
	elif line.startswith("data: "):
		data = line.lstrip("data: ")

		# 当数据块内容为 [DONE] 时，则表明所有数据块已发送完毕，可断开网络连接
		if data == "[DONE]":
			break
	else:
		data = data + "\n" + line # 我们仍然在追加内容时，为其添加一个换行符，因为这可能是该数据块有意将数据分行展示


# 在组装完所有 messages 后，我们分别打印其内容
for index, message in enumerate(messages):
	print("index:", index)
	print("message:", json.dumps(message, ensure_ascii=False))

```

--------------------------------

### Convert LaTeX to PDF with Cleanup and Error Handling (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-k2-to-setup-agent

This function converts a .tex file to a PDF using xelatex. It cleans up auxiliary files (.aux, .log, .out) before compilation and includes error handling for FileNotFoundError (xelatex not installed), subprocess.CalledProcessError (LaTeX compilation errors), and general exceptions. It prints status messages indicating success or failure.

```python
def convert_tex_to_pdf(self, tex_file):
        try:
            work_dir = os.path.dirname(tex_file)
            tex_name = os.path.basename(tex_file)
            pdf_file = os.path.join(work_dir if work_dir else '.', tex_name.replace('.tex', '.pdf'))
            subprocess.run(
                ['xelatex', '-interaction=nonstopmode', tex_file],
                cwd=work_dir if work_dir else '.',
            )
            for ext in ['.aux', '.log', '.out']:
                temp_file = os.path.join(work_dir if work_dir else '.', tex_name.replace('.tex', ext))
                if os.path.exists(temp_file):
                    try:
                        os.remove(temp_file)
                    except Exception:
                        pass
            print(f"  [已生成PDF: {pdf_file}]")
        except FileNotFoundError:
            print("  [PDF转换失败: xelatex未安装]")
        except subprocess.CalledProcessError as e:
            print("  [PDF转换失败: LaTeX编译出错]")
            if e.stdout:
                print(f"  错误输出: {e.stdout[-500:]}")
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"  [PDF转换失败: {str(e)}]")
```

### Multiple File Q&A with Kimi API

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-api-for-file-based-qa

Demonstrates how to upload multiple files and include their extracted content as separate system prompts for a single Q&A request.

```APIDOC
## Handling Multiple Files for Q&A

### Description
This function uploads multiple files and prepares them as system messages for a chat completion request, allowing Q&A across several documents.

### Method
N/A (Client-side function)

### Endpoint
N/A (Uses `/v1/files` internally)

### Parameters
#### Path Parameters
None

#### Query Parameters
None

#### Request Body
None (Function parameters)
- **files** (List[str]) - Required - A list of file paths to upload.

### Request Example
```python
from typing import *
import os
import json
from pathlib import Path
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key="MOONSHOT_API_KEY",
    base_url="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

def upload_files(files: List[str]) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
    messages = []
    for file in files:
        file_object = client.files.create(file=Path(file), purpose="file-extract")
        file_content = client.files.content(file_id=file_object.id).text
        messages.append({
            "role": "system",
            "content": file_content,
        })
    return messages

def main():
    file_messages = upload_files(files=["file1.txt", "file2.pdf"])

    messages = [
        *file_messages,
        {
            "role": "system",
            "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手..."
        },
        {
            "role": "user",
            "content": "总结一下这些文件的内容。"
        },
    ]

    print(json.dumps(messages, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False))

    completion = client.chat.completions.create(
        model="kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
        messages=messages,
    )

    print(completion.choices[0].message.content)

if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **messages** (array) - A list of message objects, where each file's content is a "system" role message.

#### Response Example
```json
[
  {
    "role": "system",
    "content": "Content of file1.txt..."
  },
  {
    "role": "system",
    "content": "Content of file2.pdf..."
  },
  {
    "role": "system",
    "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手..."
  },
  {
    "role": "user",
    "content": "总结一下这些文件的内容。"
  }
]
```
```

### Estimate Token Count using API (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/utilize-the-streaming-output-feature-of-kimi-api

This Python function estimates token count by sending the collected completion content to the Moonshot API's tokenizers/estimate-token-count endpoint. It requires the MOONSHOT_API_KEY to be set as an environment variable and uses the httpx library for making the POST request.

```python
import os
import httpx
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key = "MOONSHOT_API_KEY", # 在这里将 MOONSHOT_API_KEY 替换为你从 Kimi 开放平台申请的 API Key
    base_url = "https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

stream = client.chat.completions.create(
    model = "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
    messages = [
        {"role": "system", "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"},
        {"role": "user", "content": "你好，我叫李雷，1+1等于多少？"}
    ],
    temperature = 0.6,
    stream=True, # <-- 注意这里，我们通过设置 stream=True 开启流式输出模式
)

def estimate_token_count(input: str) -> int:
    """
    在这里实现你的 Tokens 计算逻辑，或是直接调用我们的 Tokens 计算接口计算 Tokens

    https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/tokenizers/estimate-token-count
    """
    header = {
        "Authorization": f"Bearer {os.environ['MOONSHOT_API_KEY']}",
    }
    data = {
        "model": "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
        "messages": [
            {"role": "user", "content": input},
        ]
    }
    r = httpx.post("https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/tokenizers/estimate-token-count", headers=header, json=data)
    r.raise_for_status()
    return r.json()["data"]["total_tokens"]


completion = []
for chunk in stream:
	delta = chunk.choices[0].delta
	if delta.content:
		completion.append(delta.content)


print("completion_tokens:", estimate_token_count("".join(completion)))
```

### Convert LaTeX to PDF using xelatex

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-k2-to-setup-agent

Converts a given LaTeX file (.tex) into a PDF file. It determines the working directory and the base name of the LaTeX file and then executes the 'xelatex' command with non-stop mode for compilation. This function is intended for local execution and requires 'xelatex' to be installed and in the system's PATH.

```python
    def convert_tex_to_pdf(self, tex_file):
        pdf_file = tex_file.replace('.tex', '.pdf')
        # 获取tex文件所在目录
        work_dir = os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(tex_file))
        tex_name = os.path.basename(tex_file)
        
        try:
            subprocess.run(
                ['xelatex', '-interaction=nonstopmode', tex_file],
                capture_output=True,
                text=True,
            )
```

### Enforce Character Persona in Kimi API using Partial Mode and 'name'

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-partial-mode-feature-of-kimi-api

This example demonstrates using Partial Mode with the `name` field in the Kimi API to enforce a specific character persona for the model's responses. By setting `"name": "凯尔希"` and providing a detailed system prompt, the model adopts the specified character's tone and background.

```python
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key="$MOONSHOT_API_KEY",
    base_url="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

completion = client.chat.completions.create(
    model="kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
    messages=[
        {
            "role": "system",
            "content": "下面你扮演凯尔希，请用凯尔希的语气和我对话。凯尔希是手机游戏《明日方舟》中的六星医疗职业医师分支干员。前卡兹戴尔勋爵，前巴别塔成员，罗德岛高层管理人员之一，罗德岛医疗项目领头人。在冶金工业、社会学、源石技艺、考古学、历史系谱学、经济学、植物学、地质学等领域皆拥有渊博学识。于罗德岛部分行动中作为医务人员提供医学理论协助与应急医疗器械，同时也作为罗德岛战略指挥系统的重要组成人员活跃在各项目中。", # <-- 在系统提示词 system prompt 中设定 Kimi 大模型的角色，即凯尔希医生的个性、背景、特征和怪癖等
        },
        {
            "role": "user",
            "content": "你怎么看待特蕾西娅和阿米娅？",
        },
        {
            "partial": True, # <-- 通过设置 partial 字段来启用 Partial Mode
            "role": "assistant", # <-- 同样地，我们使用一个 role=assistant 的消息来启用 Partial Mode
            "name": "凯尔希", # <-- 通过 name 字段为 Kimi 大模型设置角色，角色也被视为输出前缀的一部分
            "content": "", # <-- 在这里，我们只限定 Kimi 大模型的角色，而不是其具体输出的内容，因此将 content 字段留空
        },
    ],
    temperature=0.6,
    max_tokens=65536,
)

# 在此处，Kimi 大模型将会以凯尔希医生的口吻进行回复：
#
#  特蕾西娅，她是一位真正的领袖，有着远见卓识和坚定的信念。她的存在，对于卡兹戴尔，乃至整个萨卡兹的未来，
#  都具有不可估量的价值。她的理念，她的决心，以及她对和平的渴望，都深深地影响了我。她是一位值得尊敬的人，
#  她的梦想，也是我所追求的。
#  
#  至于阿米娅，她还年轻，但她的潜力是无限的。她有着一颗善良的心，以及对正义的执着追求。她可能会成为一位伟大的领袖，
#  只要她能够继续成长，继续学习，继续面对挑战。我会尽我所能，去保护她，去引导她，让她能够成为她想成为的人。她的命运，
#  掌握在她自己的手中。
# 
print(completion.choices[0].message.content)
```

### Initialize Configuration for Claude Code (Node.js)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/agent-support

Initializes the .claude.json configuration file to set 'hasCompletedOnboarding' to true. This script checks if the file exists, updates it if it does, or creates it with the onboarding flag if it doesn't. It uses Node.js built-in modules like 'fs' and 'path'.

```javascript
const homeDir = os.homedir(); 
const filePath = path.join(homeDir, '.claude.json');
if (fs.existsSync(filePath)) {
    const content = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf-8'));
    fs.writeFileSync(filePath,JSON.stringify({ ...content, hasCompletedOnboarding: true }, 2), 'utf-8');
} else {
    fs.writeFileSync(filePath,JSON.stringify({ hasCompletedOnboarding: true }), null, 'utf-8');
}
```

### Process Streaming Response Lines in Python

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-api-to-complete-tool-calls

This Python code snippet demonstrates how to iterate over a streaming response line by line using `r.iter_lines()`. It handles empty lines to deserialize JSON data, lines starting with 'data: ' to extract data chunks (including the '[DONE]' signal), and other lines that are appended to the current data chunk. It then processes the deserialized JSON to extract message content and tool calls, managing nested structures and concatenating arguments for tool functions.

```python
import json

# Assuming 'r' is a response object from a library like requests
# and 'messages' is a pre-initialized dictionary or list to store messages

data = ""
for line in r.iter_lines():
    line = line.strip()
 
    if len(line) == 0:
        chunk = json.loads(data)

        for choice in chunk["choices"]:
            index = choice["index"]
            message = messages[index]
            usage = choice.get("usage")
            if usage:
                message["usage"] = usage
            delta = choice["delta"]
            role = delta.get("role")
            if role:
                message["role"] = role
            content = delta.get("content")
            if content:
            	if "content" not in message:
            		message["content"] = content
            	else:
                	message["content"] = message["content"] + content

            tool_calls = delta.get("tool_calls")
            if tool_calls:
                if "tool_calls" not in message:
                    message["tool_calls"] = []
                for tool_call in tool_calls:
                    tool_call_index = tool_call["index"]
                    if len(message["tool_calls"]) < (
                            tool_call_index + 1):
                        message["tool_calls"].extend([{}] * (tool_call_index + 1 - len(message["tool_calls"])))
                    tool_call_object = message["tool_calls"][tool_call_index]
                    tool_call_object["index"] = tool_call_index

                    tool_call_id = tool_call.get("id")
                    if tool_call_id:
                        tool_call_object["id"] = tool_call_id
                    tool_call_type = tool_call.get("type")
                    if tool_call_type:
                        tool_call_object["type"] = tool_call_type
                    tool_call_function = tool_call.get("function")
                    if tool_call_function:
                        if "function" not in tool_call_object:
                            tool_call_object["function"] = {}
                        tool_call_function_name = tool_call_function.get("name")
                        if tool_call_function_name:
                            tool_call_object["function"]["name"] = tool_call_function_name
                        tool_call_function_arguments = tool_call_function.get("arguments")
                        if tool_call_function_arguments:
                            if "arguments" not in tool_call_object["function"]:
                                tool_call_object["function"]["arguments"] = tool_call_function_arguments
                            else:
                                tool_call_object["function"]["arguments"] = tool_call_object["function"][
                                                                            "arguments"] + tool_call_function_arguments
                    message["tool_calls"][tool_call_index] = tool_call_object

            data = ""
    elif line.startswith("data: "):
        data = line.lstrip("data: ")

        if data == "[DONE]":
            break
    else:
        data = data + "\n" + line

```

### Single File Q&A with Kimi API

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-api-for-file-based-qa

This section details how to upload a single file, extract its content, and then use that content within a system prompt to ask questions using the Kimi API.

```APIDOC
## POST /v1/files

### Description
Uploads a file to be processed and used for Q&A.

### Method

/v1/files

from pathlib import Path

client = OpenAI(
    api_key="MOONSHOT_API_KEY",

## POST /v1/chat/completions (with file content)

### Description
Sends a chat completion request including extracted file content in the system prompt.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
/v1/chat/completions

### Parameters
#### Path Parameters
None

#### Query Parameters
None

#### Request Body
- **model** (string) - Required - The model to use (e.g., "kimi-k2-turbo-preview").
- **messages** (array) - Required - A list of message objects.
  - **role** (string) - The role of the message (e.g., "system", "user").
  - **content** (string) - The content of the message.
- **temperature** (number) - Optional - Controls randomness. Defaults to 0.6.

### Request Example
```python
messages = [
    {
        "role": "system",
        "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手..."
    },
    {
        "role": "system",
        "content": file_content  # Extracted file content
    },
    {"role": "user", "content": "请简单介绍 moonshot.pdf 的具体内容"},
]

completion = client.chat.completions.create(
  model="kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
  messages=messages,
  temperature=0.6,
)

print(completion.choices[0].message)
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **choices** (array) - A list of message choices.
  - **message** (object) - The message object.
    - **role** (string) - The role of the message.
    - **content** (string) - The content of the message.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "choices": [
    {
      "message": {
        "role": "assistant",
        "content": "This PDF file provides an overview of the Moonshot AI platform..."
      }
    }
  ]
}
```

### Python Script for Tool Loading and Chat Interaction

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-official-tools

This Python script loads tools from formulas, checks for duplicates, and then initiates a chat interaction with the AI. It handles system messages, user questions, and enters a chat loop if no question is provided. It ensures the client is closed properly.

```python
continue
            func_name = func.get("name")
            assert func_name, f"Tool missing name: {tool}"
            assert (
                func_name not in tool_to_uri
            ), f"ERROR: Tool '{func_name}' conflicts between {tool_to_uri.get(func_name)} and {uri}"
 
            if func_name in function_names:
                print(
                    f"ERROR: Duplicate function name '{func_name}' found across formulas"
                )
                print(f"Function {func_name} already exists in another formula")
                await client.close()
                return
 
            function_names.add(func_name)
            all_tools.append(tool)
            tool_to_uri[func_name] = uri
            print(f"  - {func_name}: {func.get('description', 'N/A')}")
 
    print(f"\nTotal unique tools loaded: {len(all_tools)}")
    if not all_tools:
        print("Warning: No tools found in any formula")
        return
 
    try:
        messages = [
            {
                "role": "system",
                "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。",
            }
        ]
        if args.question:
            print(f"\nUser: {args.question}")
            await client.chat(args.question, messages, all_tools, tool_to_uri)
        else:
            print("Chat mode (type 'q' to quit)")
            while True:
                question = input("\nQ: ").strip()
                if question.lower() == "q":
                    break
                if question:
                    await client.chat(question, messages, all_tools, tool_to_uri)
 
    finally:
        await client.close()
 
 
if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(main())

```

### Upload Video and Describe with Moonshot API

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-vision-model

This Python snippet demonstrates how to upload a video file to Moonshot and then use the Vision API to generate a description. It requires the 'openai' library and a valid Moonshot API key. The video is uploaded using `client.files.create` with `purpose='video'`, and then referenced in the chat completion request using a `ms://<file-id>` URL.

```python
import os
from pathlib import Path

from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key=os.environ.get("MOONSHOT_API_KEY"),
    base_url="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

# Replace video.mp4 with the actual path to your image or video file
video_path = "video.mp4"

file_object = client.files.create(file=Path(video_path), purpose="video")  # Upload image to Moonshot

completion = client.chat.completions.create(
    model="kimi-k2.5",
    messages=[
        {
            "role": "system",
            "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"
        },
        {
            "role": "user",
            "content":
            [
                {
                    "type": "video_url",
                    "video_url":
                    {
                        "url": f"ms://{file_object.id}"  # Note: ms:// instead of base64 encoded image
                    }
                },
                {
                    "type": "text",
                    "text": "请描述这个视频"
                }
            ]
        }
    ]
)

print(completion.choices[0].message.content)
```

### Define and Submit 'search' Tool to Kimi AI (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-api-to-complete-tool-calls

This Python code snippet demonstrates how to define a 'search' tool with its description and parameters, and then submit it to the Kimi AI model for potential invocation. It utilizes the OpenAI Python library and requires an API key and base URL for the Moonshot AI platform. The tool is designed to search the internet based on a user-provided query.

```python
from openai import OpenAI


client = OpenAI(
    api_key="MOONSHOT_API_KEY", # 在这里将 MOONSHOT_API_KEY 替换为你从 Kimi 开放平台申请的 API Key
    base_url="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

tools = [
	{
		"type": "function", # 约定的字段 type，目前支持 function 作为值
		"function": { # 当 type 为 function 时，使用 function 字段定义具体的函数内容
			"name": "search", # 函数的名称，请使用英文大小写字母、数据加上减号和下划线作为函数名称
			"description": """
				通过搜索引擎搜索互联网上的内容。

				当你的知识无法回答用户提出的问题，或用户请求你进行联网搜索时，调用此工具。请从与用户的对话中提取用户想要搜索的内容作为 query 参数的值。
				搜索结果包含网站的标题、网站的地址（URL）以及网站简介。
			""", # 函数的介绍，在这里写上函数的具体作用以及使用场景，以便 Kimi 大模型能正确地选择使用哪些函数
			"parameters": { # 使用 parameters 字段来定义函数接收的参数
				"type": "object", # 固定使用 type: object 来使 Kimi 大模型生成一个 JSON Object 参数
				"required": ["query"], # 使用 required 字段告诉 Kimi 大模型哪些参数是必填项
				"properties": { # properties 中是具体的参数定义，你可以定义多个参数
					"query": { # 在这里，key 是参数名称，value 是参数的具体定义
						"type": "string", # 使用 type 定义参数类型
						"description": """
							用户搜索的内容，请从用户的提问或聊天上下文中提取。
						""" # 使用 description 描述参数以便 Kimi 大模型更好地生成参数
					}
				}
			}
		}
	},
	# {
	# 	"type": "function", # 约定的字段 type，目前支持 function 作为值
	# 	"function": { # 当 type 为 function 时，使用 function 字段定义具体的函数内容
	# 		"name": "crawl", # 函数的名称，请使用英文大小写字母、数据加上减号和下划线作为函数名称
	# 		"description": """
	# 			根据网站地址（URL）获取网页内容。
	# 		""", # 函数的介绍，在这里写上函数的具体作用以及使用场景，以便 Kimi 大模型能正确地选择使用哪些函数
	# 		"parameters": { # 使用 parameters 字段来定义函数接收的参数
	# 			"type": "object", # 固定使用 type: object 来使 Kimi 大模型生成一个 JSON Object 参数
	# 			"required": ["url"], # 使用 required 字段告诉 Kimi 大模型哪些参数是必填项
	# 			"properties": { # properties 中是具体的参数定义，你可以定义多个参数
	# 				"url": { # 在这里，key 是参数名称，value 是参数的具体定义
	# 					"type": "string", # 使用 type 定义参数类型
	# 					"description": """
	# 						需要获取内容的网站地址（URL），通常情况下从搜索结果中可以获取网站的地址。
	# 					""" # 使用 description 描述参数以便 Kimi 大模型更好地生成参数
	# 				}
	# 				}
	# 		}
	# 	}
	# }
]

completion = client.chat.completions.create(
    model="kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
    messages=[
        {"role": "system", "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"},
        {"role": "user", "content": "请联网搜索 Context Caching，并告诉我它是什么。"} # 在提问中要求 Kimi 大模型联网搜索
    ],
    temperature=0.6,
    tools=tools, # <-- 我们通过 tools 参数，将定义好的 tools 提交给 Kimi 大模型
)

print(completion.choices[0].model_dump_json(indent=4))

```

### Partial Mode for Role-Playing Consistency

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/partial

Illustrates using Partial Mode along with a 'name' field in the assistant's message to enhance character consistency during role-playing scenarios.

```APIDOC
## POST /v1/chat/completions

### Description
This endpoint facilitates chat interactions. Partial Mode, combined with specifying a character's name, can be used to maintain consistent persona and dialogue style in role-playing.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
/v1/chat/completions

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **model** (string) - Required - The model to use (e.g., "kimi-k2-turbo-preview").
- **messages** (array) - Required - Conversation history.
  - **role** (string) - Required - Sender's role ('system', 'user', or 'assistant').
  - **content** (string) - Required - Message content.
  - **partial** (boolean) - Optional - Enables Partial Mode for prefilling assistant responses.
  - **name** (string) - Optional - Specifies the name of the character the assistant is role-playing as.
- **temperature** (number) - Optional - Controls output randomness. Defaults to 0.6.
- **max_tokens** (integer) - Optional - Maximum number of tokens to generate. Set to 65536 in the example.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "model": "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
  "messages": [
    {
      "role": "system",
      "content": "下面你扮演凯尔希，请用凯尔希的语气和我对话。凯尔希是手机游戏《明日方舟》中的六星医疗职业医师分支干员。前卡兹戴尔勋爵，前巴别塔成员，罗德岛高层管理人员之一，罗德岛医疗项目领头人。在冶金工业、社会学、源石技艺、考古学、历史系谱学、经济学、植物学、地质学等领域皆拥有渊博学识。于罗德岛部分行动中作为医务人员提供医学理论协助与应急医疗器械，同时也作为罗德岛战略指挥系统的重要组成人员活跃在各项目中。"
    },
    {
      "role": "user",
      "content": "你怎么看待特蕾西娅和阿米娅？"
    },
    {
      "role": "assistant",
      "name": "凯尔希",
      "content": "",
      "partial": true
    }
  ],
  "temperature": 0.6,
  "max_tokens": 65536
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **choices** (array) - Contains the model's response(s).
  - **message** (object) - The message object from the model.
    - **content** (string) - The generated content from the model.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "choices": [
    {
      "message": {
        "content": "特蕾西娅，她是一位真正的领袖，有着远见卓识和坚定的信念。她的存在，对于卡兹戴尔，乃至整个萨卡兹的未来，都具有不可估量的价值。她的理念，她的决心，以及她对和平的渴望，都深深地影响了我。她是一位值得尊敬的人，她的梦想，也是我所追求的。\n至于阿米娅，她还年轻，但她的潜力是无限的。她有着一颗善良的心，以及对正义的执着追求。她可能会成为一位伟大的领袖，只要她能够继续成长，继续学习，继续面对挑战。我会尽我所能，去保护她，去引导她，让她能够成为她想成为的人。她的命运，掌握在她自己的手中。"
      }
    }
  ]
}
```

#### Other Techniques for Role Consistency
- Provide clear character descriptions detailing personality, background, and traits.
- Include specific details about the character's speech patterns, style, and motivations.
- Guide the model on how to act in various situations and respond to specific user inputs.
- Periodically reinforce character settings in long conversations, especially if the model deviates.
```

--------------------------------

### Tool Use Parameter Compatibility

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/kimi-k2-5-quickstart

Information regarding parameter compatibility when using tools with Kimi K2.5, especially when `thinking` is enabled.

```APIDOC
## Tool Use with Kimi K2.5 (Thinking Enabled)

### Description
When `thinking` is set to `{"type": "enabled"}`, the following constraints apply to tool usage to ensure model performance and avoid conflicts.

### Constraints
- **tool_choice**: Can only be "auto" or "none" (default is "auto"). Any other value will result in an error to prevent conflicts with reasoning.
- **Context for Multi-turn Tool Calls**: For multi-turn tool invocations, the `reasoning_content` from the assistant's message in the previous turn must be included in the context. Failure to do so will result in an error.
- **Built-in Web Search (`$web_search`)**: The built-in web search tool is currently incompatible with Kimi K2.5's thinking mode. To use `$web_search`, you must first disable the thinking mode.

Refer to the documentation on [how to use the thinking model correctly with tool calls](link_to_tool_use_docs) for more details.
```

### Basic Chat Completion with kimi-k2.5 (cURL)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-k2-thinking-model

This snippet shows how to perform a basic chat completion using the `kimi-k2.5` model with its default thinking capabilities enabled, using cURL. It highlights that explicit configuration for thinking is not needed for this model by default.

```shell
$ curl https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/chat/completions \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -H "Authorization: Bearer $MOONSHOT_API_KEY" \
    -d '{
        "model": "kimi-k2.5",
        "messages": [
            {
                "role": "system",
                "content": "你是 Kimi。"
            },
            {
                "role": "user",
                "content": "请解释 1+1=2。"
            }
        ]
   }'

```

### Enforce Tool Calls with Prompt in Python (Kimi API)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/migrating-from-openai-to-kimi

This Python snippet demonstrates how to work around the lack of `tool_choice='required'` in Kimi API by using a specific prompt to encourage the model to select a tool. It initializes the OpenAI client with Kimi's API key and base URL, defines tools and messages, and then makes a completion call. If the initial call doesn't result in tool calls, it appends a user message prompting tool selection and retries.

```python
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key="MOONSHOT_API_KEY",  # 在这里将 MOONSHOT_API_KEY 替换为你从 Kimi 开放平台申请的 API Key
    base_url="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

tools = {
    # 在这里定义你的 tools
}

messages = [
    # 在这里存储你的消息历史记录
]

completion = client.chat.completions.create(
    model="kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
    messages=messages,
    temperature=0.6,
    tools=tools,
    # tool_choice="required",  # <-- 由于 Kimi API 暂时不支持 tool_choice=required，我们暂时屏蔽这一选项
)

choice = completion.choices[0]
if choice.finish_reason != "tool_calls":
    # 我们假定我们的业务逻辑能够确认此处必须要调用 tool_calls，
    # 在不使用 tool_choice=required 的情况下，我们通过提示词
    # prompt 来让 Kimi 强制选择一个工具进行调用
    messages.append(choice.message)
    messages.append({
        "role": "user",
        "content": "请选择一个工具（tool）来处理当前的问题。",  # 通常情况下，Kimi 大模型能理解调用工具的意图并选择一个工具进行调用
    })
    completion = client.chat.completions.create(
        model="kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
        messages=messages,
        temperature=0.6,
        tools=tools,
    )
    choice = completion.choices[0]
    assert choice.finish_reason == "tool_calls"  # 这次的请求，理应返回 finish_reason=tool_calls
    print(choice.message.content)

```

--------------------------------

### Best Practices

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-vision-model

Recommendations for optimizing the use of the Vision API, including resolution and file handling.

```APIDOC
## Best Practices

### Resolution
- **Recommended Image Resolution:** Not exceeding 4k (4096*2160).
- **Recommended Video Resolution:** Not exceeding 2k (2048*1080).

Higher resolutions beyond these recommendations will increase processing time without improving model understanding.

### Upload File vs. Base64
- **Large Videos:** For very large video files, use the file upload method due to overall request body size limitations.
- **Reusable Media:** For images or videos that will be referenced multiple times, the file upload method is recommended.

Refer to the [File Upload Documentation](link_to_file_upload_docs) for details on file upload limitations.
```

--------------------------------

### Main Execution Flow for Formula Chat Client (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-k2-to-setup-agent

The main asynchronous function sets up the chat client. It parses command-line arguments for formulas and questions, normalizes URIs, retrieves an API key, initializes the client, loads available tools (both custom and from URIs), and then enters either a direct chat mode or processes a single question. It includes robust error handling for missing API keys and tool loading, and ensures the client is properly closed.

```python
async def main():
    parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(description="Formula chat client")
    parser.add_argument(
        "--formula",
        action="append",
        default=["moonshot/web-search:latest", "moonshot/rethink:latest", "moonshot/code-runner:latest"],
        help="Formula URIs",
    )
    parser.add_argument("--question", help="Question to ask")

    args = parser.parse_args()

    # Process and deduplicate formula URIs
    normalized_formulas = [normalize_formula_uri(uri) for uri in args.formula]
    unique_formulas = list(dict.fromkeys(normalized_formulas))

    moonshot_base_url = os.getenv("MOONSHOT_BASE_URL", "https://api.moonshot.cn/v1")
    api_key = os.getenv("MOONSHOT_API_KEY")

    if not api_key:
        print("Error: MOONSHOT_API_KEY environment variable is required")
        return

    client = FormulaChatClient(moonshot_base_url, api_key)

    # Load tools
    all_tools = []
    tool_to_uri = {}

    for tool in TOOLS:
        func = tool.get("function")
        if func:
            func_name = func.get("name")
            all_tools.append(tool)
            tool_to_uri[func_name] = "custom"

    for uri in unique_formulas:
        tools = await client.get_tools(uri)
        for tool in tools:
            func = tool.get("function")
            if not func:
                continue
            
            func_name = func.get("name")
            if not func_name or func_name in tool_to_uri:
                continue

            all_tools.append(tool)
            tool_to_uri[func_name] = uri

    if not all_tools:
        print("Error: No tools loaded")
        return

    print(f"已加载 {len(all_tools)} 个工具")

    try:
        messages = [{"role": "system", "content": SYSTEM_PROMPT}]
        
        if args.question:
            print(f"\n问题: {args.question}")
            await client.chat(args.question, messages, all_tools, tool_to_uri)
        else:
            print("\n对话模式 (输入 'q' 退出)\n")
            while True:
                question = input("Q: ").strip()
                if question.lower() == "q":
                    break
                if question:
                    await client.chat(question, messages, all_tools, tool_to_uri)

    finally:
        await client.close()

if __name__ == "__main__":
    asyncio.run(main())
```

--------------------------------

### Python: Basic Multi-Turn Conversation with Kimi API

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/engage-in-multi-turn-conversations-using-kimi-api

This Python snippet demonstrates how to implement multi-turn conversations using the Kimi API. It initializes the OpenAI client with your API key and base URL. A global 'messages' list stores the conversation history, including system prompts, user inputs, and assistant responses. The 'chat' function appends the user's input, sends the entire message history to the API, and appends the assistant's response to maintain context for future turns.

```python
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key = "MOONSHOT_API_KEY", # 在这里将 MOONSHOT_API_KEY 替换为你从 Kimi 开放平台申请的 API Key
    base_url = "https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

# 我们定义一个全局变量 messages，用于记录我们和 Kimi 大模型产生的历史对话消息
# 在 messages 中，既包含我们向 Kimi 大模型提出的问题（role=user），也包括 Kimi 大模型给我们的回复（role=assistant）
# 当然，也包括初始的 System Prompt（role=system）
# messages 中的消息按时间顺序从小到大排列
messages = [
	{"role": "system", "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"},
]

def chat(input: str) -> str:
	"""
	chat 函数支持多轮对话，每次调用 chat 函数与 Kimi 大模型对话时，Kimi 大模型都会”看到“此前已经
	产生的历史对话消息，换句话说，Kimi 大模型拥有了记忆。
	"""

  global messages

	# 我们将用户最新的问题构造成一个 message（role=user），并添加到 messages 的尾部
	messages.append({
		"role": "user",
		"content": input,	
	})

	# 携带 messages 与 Kimi 大模型对话
	completion = client.chat.completions.create(
        model="kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
        messages=messages,
        temperature=0.6,
    )

	# 通过 API 我们获得了 Kimi 大模型给予我们的回复消息（role=assistant）
    assistant_message = completion.choices[0].message

    # 为了让 Kimi 大模型拥有完整的记忆，我们必须将 Kimi 大模型返回给我们的消息也添加到 messages 中
    messages.append(assistant_message)

    return assistant_message.content

print(chat("你好，我今年 27 岁。"))
print(chat("你知道我今年几岁吗？")) # 在这里，Kimi 大模型根据此前的上下文信息，将会知道你今年的年龄是 27 岁

```

--------------------------------

### Kimi K2.5 Model Parameters

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/kimi-k2-5-quickstart

Overview of parameters for Kimi K2.5 series models, with recommendations on usage and default values.

```APIDOC
## Kimi K2.5 Model Parameters

### Description
This section details specific parameter behaviors for the Kimi K2.5 series models. It is recommended to use default values for most parameters.

### Parameters

- **max_tokens** (int) - Optional - The maximum number of tokens to generate in the chat completion. Default is 32768.
- **thinking** (object) - Optional - Controls whether the model's thinking process is enabled. Default is `{"type": "enabled"}`. Allowed values are `{"type": "enabled"}` or `{"type": "disabled"}`.
- **temperature** (float) - Optional - Sampling temperature. For K2.5 series, this is fixed at 1.0 (or 0.6 in non-thinking mode). Specifying other values will result in an error.
- **top_p** (float) - Optional - Sampling method. For K2.5 series, this is fixed at 0.95. Specifying other values will result in an error.
- **n** (int) - Optional - The number of completions to generate for each input message. For K2.5 series, this is fixed at 1. Specifying other values will result in an error.
- **presence_penalty** (float) - Optional - Penalty for the presence of new tokens. For K2.5 series, this is fixed at 0.0. Specifying other values will result in an error.
- **frequency_penalty** (float) - Optional - Penalty for the frequency of new tokens. For K2.5 series, this is fixed at 0.0. Specifying other values will result in an error.
```

--------------------------------

### Multi-step Tool Calling withkimi-k2-thinking / kimi-k2.5

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-k2-thinking-model

This section covers how to perform multi-step tool calls using `kimi-k2-thinking` or `kimi-k2.5` (with thinking enabled) for complex tasks.

```APIDOC
## Multi-step Tool Calling

### Description
Enables complex task execution through multi-step tool invocation using `kimi-k2-thinking` or `kimi-k2.5` models when thinking is enabled. This allows the model to reason and call various tools sequentially.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/chat/completions

### Usage Guidelines
To ensure optimal performance for multi-step tool calling:

- **Include all reasoning content**: Ensure the input includes all `reasoning_content` from previous steps. The model will select relevant information for its reasoning.
- **Set `max_tokens`**: Set `max_tokens` to at least `16000` to accommodate the full `reasoning_content` and `content` output.
- **Set `temperature`**: Use `temperature=1.0` for the best results. For `kimi-k2.5`, this parameter is fixed at `1.0` when thinking is enabled.
- **Use streaming**: Enable streaming (`stream=True`) for a better user experience and to mitigate potential network timeouts, as `reasoning_content` is outputted before `content`.

### Request Body Parameters (in addition to standard chat completion parameters)
- **model** (string) - Required - Use `kimi-k2-thinking` or `kimi-k2.5`.
- **messages** (array) - Required - Include previous `reasoning_content` in the input messages if available.
- **max_tokens** (integer) - Required - Minimum value `16000`.
- **temperature** (number) - Required - Set to `1.0`.
- **stream** (boolean) - Recommended - Set to `true`.
- **tools** (array) - Optional - Definitions of the tools the model can call.

### Request Example (Conceptual)
```json
{
    "model": "kimi-k2.5",
    "messages": [
        {
            "role": "system",
            "content": "你是一个助手，负责生成今日新闻报告。"
        },
        {
            "role": "user",
            "content": "请生成今日新闻报告。"
        }
    ],
    "max_tokens": 16000,
    "temperature": 1.0,
    "stream": true,
    "tools": [
        {
            "type": "function",
            "function": {
                "name": "date",
                "description": "获取当前日期"
            }
        },
        {
            "type": "function",
            "function": {
                "name": "web_search",
                "description": "搜索网页内容",
                "parameters": {
                    "type": "object",
                    "properties": {
                        "query": {
                            "type": "string",
                            "description": "搜索查询词"
                        }
                    },
                    "required": ["query"]
                }
            }
        }
    ]
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (Streaming)
When `stream=True`, the response will be a stream of Server-Sent Events. Each event may contain `reasoning_content` and `content`. `reasoning_content` will appear before `content`.

*Example of streamed chunks (simplified):
```json
{"choices": [{"delta": {"reasoning_content": "需要先获取今天的日期。"}, "finish_reason": null}]}
{"choices": [{"delta": {"content": "今天是 2023年10月27日。"}, "finish_reason": null}]}
{"choices": [{"delta": {"reasoning_content": "现在可以搜索今天的新闻了。"}, "finish_reason": null}]}
{"choices": [{"delta": {"content": "[今日新闻摘要...]"}, "finish_reason": "stop"}]}
```

#### Reasoning Content Handling
- The `reasoning_content` field is part of the model's output when thinking is enabled.
- It is not directly accessible via standard OpenAI SDK types like `ChoiceDelta` or `ChatCompletionMessage` using attribute access (e.g., `.reasoning_content`).
- Use `hasattr(obj, "reasoning_content")` to check for its existence and `getattr(obj, "reasoning_content")` to retrieve its value if using the OpenAI SDK.
- If interacting directly via HTTP, `reasoning_content` is a sibling field to `content`.
- In streaming mode, `reasoning_content` always precedes `content`.
```

--------------------------------

### Process Streaming Output with Tool Calls (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-api-to-complete-tool-calls

This Python code demonstrates how to process streaming responses from the Moonshot API, specifically handling the reconstruction of messages and tool calls. It initializes the OpenAI client, defines a tool for web searching, makes a streaming API call requesting multiple completions, and then iterates through the chunks to assemble the final messages, including nested tool call information. Dependencies include the 'openai' library and environment variables for API keys.

```python
import os
import json

from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key=os.environ.get("MOONSHOT_API_KEY"),
    base_url="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

tools = [
    {
        "type": "function",  # 约定的字段 type，目前支持 function 作为值
        "function": {  # 当 type 为 function 时，使用 function 字段定义具体的函数内容
            "name": "search",  # 函数的名称，请使用英文大小写字母、数据加上减号和下划线作为函数名称
            "description": """
			通过搜索引擎搜索互联网上的内容。

			当你的知识无法回答用户提出的问题，或用户请求你进行联网搜索时，调用此工具。请从与用户的对话中提取用户想要搜索的内容作为 query 参数的值。
			搜索结果包含网站的标题、网站的地址（URL）以及网站简介。
		""",  # 函数的介绍，在这里写上函数的具体作用以及使用场景，以便 Kimi 大模型能正确地选择使用哪些函数
            "parameters": {  # 使用 parameters 字段来定义函数接收的参数
                "type": "object",  # 固定使用 type: object 来使 Kimi 大模型生成一个 JSON Object 参数
                "required": ["query"],  # 使用 required 字段告诉 Kimi 大模型哪些参数是必填项
                "properties": {  # properties 中是具体的参数定义，你可以定义多个参数
                    "query": {
                        "type": "string",  # 使用 type 定义参数类型
                        "description": """
						用户搜索的内容，请从用户的提问或聊天上下文中提取。
					"""
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    },
]

completion = client.chat.completions.create(
    model="kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
    messages=[
        {"role": "user", "content": "请联网搜索 Context Caching 技术。"}
    ],
    temperature=0.6,
    stream=True,
    n=2,  # <-- 注意这里，我们要求 Kimi 大模型输出 2 个回复
    tools=tools,  # <-- 添加工具调用
)

# 在这里，我们预先构建一个 List，用于存放不同的回复消息，由于我们设置了 n=2，因此我们将 List 初始化为 2 个元素
messages = [{}, {}]

for chunk in completion:
    # 通过循环获取每个数据块中所有的 choice，并获取 index 对应的 message 对象
    for choice in chunk.choices:
        index = choice.index
        message = messages[index]
        delta = choice.delta
        role = delta.role
        if role:
            message["role"] = role
        content = delta.content
        if content:
        	if "content" not in message:
        		message["content"] = content
        	else:
            	message["content"] = message["content"] + content

        # 从这里，我们开始处理 tool_calls
        tool_calls = delta.tool_calls  # <-- 先判断数据块中是否包含 tool_calls
        if tool_calls:
            if "tool_calls" not in message:
                message["tool_calls"] = []  # <-- 如果包含 tool_calls，我们初始化一个列表来保存这些 tool_calls，注意此时的列表中没有任何元素，长度为 0
            for tool_call in tool_calls:
                tool_call_index = tool_call.index  # <-- 获取当前 tool_call 的 index 索引
                if len(message["tool_calls"]) < (
                        tool_call_index + 1):  # <-- 根据 index 索引扩充 tool_calls 列表，以便于我们能通过下标访问到对应的 tool_call
                    message["tool_calls"].extend([{}] * (tool_call_index + 1 - len(message["tool_calls"])))
                tool_call_object = message["tool_calls"][tool_call_index]  # <-- 根据下标访问对应的 tool_call
                tool_call_object["index"] = tool_call_index

                # 下面的步骤，是根据数据块中的信息填充每个 tool_call 的 id、type、function 字段
                # 在 function 字段中，又包括 name 和 arguments 字段，arguments 字段会由每个数据块
                # 依次补充，如同 delta.content 字段一般。

                tool_call_id = tool_call.id
                if tool_call_id:
                    tool_call_object["id"] = tool_call_id
                tool_call_type = tool_call.type
                if tool_call_type:
                    tool_call_object["type"] = tool_call_type
                tool_call_function = tool_call.function
                if tool_call_function:
                    if "function" not in tool_call_object:
                        tool_call_object["function"] = {}
                    tool_call_function_name = tool_call_function.name
                    if tool_call_function_name:
                        tool_call_object["function"]["name"] = tool_call_function_name
                    tool_call_function_arguments = tool_call_function.arguments
                    if tool_call_function_arguments:
                        if "arguments" not in tool_call_object["function"]:
                            tool_call_object["function"]["arguments"] = tool_call_function_arguments
                        else:
                            tool_call_object["function"]["arguments"] = tool_call_object["function"][
                                                                            "arguments"] + tool_call_function_arguments  # <-- 依次补充 function.arguments 字段的值
                message["tool_calls"][tool_call_index] = tool_call_object

# 在组装完所有 messages 后，我们分别打印其内容
for index, message in enumerate(messages):
    print("index:", index)
    print("message:", json.dumps(message, ensure_ascii=False))
    print("")

```

--------------------------------

### Migrating from OpenAI to Kimi API

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/migrating-from-openai-to-kimi

This section details how to migrate your application from OpenAI's API to Kimi's API by simply updating the base URL and API key. It also highlights key differences and provides migration suggestions.

```APIDOC
## Migrating from OpenAI to Kimi API

### Description
Kimi API is designed to be compatible with OpenAI's API specifications. Developers can leverage existing OpenAI SDKs (Python, NodeJS) by modifying the `base_url` and `api_key` to seamlessly transition their applications to Kimi's models.

### Key Differences and Migration Suggestions:

1.  **`temperature` and `n` values**:
    *   **OpenAI**: Allows `temperature=0` and `n>1` simultaneously.
    *   **Kimi API**: When `temperature` is 0 or close to 0, only one response (`len(choices)=1`) is supported. Setting `n>1` with `temperature=0` results in an `invalid_request_error`.
    *   **Parameter Range**: Kimi API's `temperature` range is `[0, 1]`, while OpenAI's is `[0, 2]`.
    *   **Migration Suggestion**: Recommended `temperature` is 0.3. For `kimi-k2-turbo-preview`, use 0.6. If stable output is needed with `temperature=0`, set `n=1`.

2.  **`usage` value in stream mode**:
    *   **OpenAI**: `usage` info is not included by default in streaming responses. It can be enabled with `stream_options={"include_usage": True}`.
    *   **Kimi API**: `usage` info (`prompt_tokens`, `completion_tokens`, `total_tokens`) is included in the final chunk for each choice when `stream_options={"include_usage": True}` is used. Additionally, `usage` information is placed in the ending data block of each choice.
    *   **Migration Suggestion**: Generally, no extra steps are needed. For per-choice usage statistics, access `choice.usage`. Note that `usage.prompt_tokens` is consistent across choices, while `usage.completion_tokens` and `usage.total_tokens` may differ.

3.  **Deprecated `function_call`**:
    *   **OpenAI**: `functions` parameter is deprecated in favor of `tool_calls`.
    *   **Kimi API**: Fully supports `tool_calls` but **does not support the deprecated `functions` parameter**.
    *   **Migration Suggestion**: If using `tool_calls`, no changes are needed. If relying on the deprecated `functions`, migrate to `tool_calls` for enhanced capabilities, including parallel function invocation. Refer to the [Tool Calls Guide](link_to_tool_calls_guide) for details.

### Code Example (Python Initialization)
```python
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key="MOONSHOT_API_KEY",  # Replace with your Kimi API Key
    base_url="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1", # Replace OpenAI's base URL
)
```

### Supported Endpoints (OpenAI Compatible)
*   `/v1/chat/completions`
*   `/v1/files`
*   `/v1/files/{file_id}`
*   `/v1/files/{file_id}/content`
```

--------------------------------

### Perform Multi-Turn Conversation with Tool Calls

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-k2-thinking-model

Initializes the message history with a system prompt and a user request. It then enters a loop to call the model, process its response (including reasoning content and tool calls), execute the tools, and append the results back into the message history. The loop continues until the model provides a final answer without tool calls or reaches a maximum iteration limit.

```python
# 初始化消息列表
messages = [
    {
        "role": "system",
        "content": "你是 Kimi，一个专业的新闻分析师。你擅长收集、分析和整理信息，生成高质量的新闻报告。",
    },
]

# 用户请求生成今日新闻报告
user_request = "请帮我生成一份今日新闻报告，包含重要的科技、经济和社会新闻。"
messages.append({
    "role": "user",
    "content": user_request
})

print(f"用户请求: {user_request}\n")


max_iterations = 10  # 防止无限循环
for iteration in range(max_iterations):
    # 调用模型
    try:
        completion = client.openai.chat.completions.create(
            model=client.model,
            messages=messages,
            max_tokens=1024 * 32,
            tools=all_tools,
            temperature=1.0,
        )
    except openai.AuthenticationError as e:
        print(f"认证错误: {e}")
        print("请检查 API key 是否正确，以及 API key 是否有权限访问该端点")
        raise
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"调用模型时发生错误: {e}")
        raise
    
    # 获取响应
    message = completion.choices[0].message
    
    # 打印思考过程
    if hasattr(message, "reasoning_content"):
        print(f"=============第 {iteration + 1} 轮思考开始=============")
        reasoning = getattr(message, "reasoning_content")
        if reasoning:
            print(reasoning[:500] + "..." if len(reasoning) > 500 else reasoning)
        print(f"=============第 {iteration + 1} 轮思考结束=============\n")
    
    # 添加 assistant 消息到上下文（保留 reasoning_content）
    messages.append(message)
    
    # 如果模型没有调用工具，说明对话结束
    if not message.tool_calls:
        print("=============最终回答=============")
        print(message.content)
        break
    
    # 处理工具调用
    print(f"模型决定调用 {len(message.tool_calls)} 个工具:\n")
    
    for tool_call in message.tool_calls:
        func_name = tool_call.function.name
        args = json.loads(tool_call.function.arguments)
        
        print(f"调用工具: {func_name}")
        print(f"参数: {json.dumps(args, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)}")
        
        # 获取对应的 formula_uri
        formula_uri = tool_to_uri.get(func_name)
        if not formula_uri:
            print(f"错误: 找不到工具 {func_name} 对应的 Formula URI")
            continue
        
        # 调用工具
        result = client.call_tool(formula_uri, func_name, args)
        
        # 打印结果（截断过长内容）
        if len(str(result)) > 200:
            print(f"工具结果: {str(result)[:200]}...\n")
        else:
            print(f"工具结果: {result}\n")
        
        # 添加工具结果到消息列表
        tool_message = {
            "role": "tool",
            "tool_call_id": tool_call.id,
            "name": func_name,
            "content": result
        }
        messages.append(tool_message)

print("\n对话完成！")

# 清理资源
client.close()

```

### Explanation of Reasoning Content

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-k2-thinking-model

Provides answers to frequently asked questions regarding the `reasoning_content` field in the Kimi API responses. It clarifies its purpose in maintaining conversational coherence during multi-step reasoning and its impact on token consumption and billing.

```markdown
## 常见问题
### Q1: 为什么需要保留 reasoning_content？
A: 保留 reasoning_content 可以确保模型在多步推理过程中保持推理的连贯性，特别是在工具调用过程中。服务器会自动处理这些字段，用户无需手动管理。
### Q2: reasoning_content 会消耗额外的 token 吗？
A: 是的，reasoning_content 会计入输入/输出 token 消耗。具体计费方式请参考 MoonshotAI 的定价文档。
Last updated on 2026年1月28日
Kimi K2开始使用 Kimi API
```

### Python Client for Kimi Models with Tool Calls

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-k2-thinking-model

This Python code defines a `FormulaChatClient` class for interacting with Kimi models, supporting tool definitions, tool calls, and handling responses. It's designed for complex tasks involving multi-step tool invocation and reasoning.

```python
import os
import json
import httpx
import openai


class FormulaChatClient:
    def __init__(self, base_url: str, api_key: str):
        """初始化 Formula 客户端"""
        self.base_url = base_url
        self.api_key = api_key
        self.openai = openai.Client(
            base_url=base_url,
            api_key=api_key,
        )
        self.httpx = httpx.Client(
            base_url=base_url,
            headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {api_key}"},
            timeout=30.0,
        )
        # 使用 kimi-k2-thinking 模型
        # 如果使用 kimi-k2.5 模型，请改为 "kimi-k2.5"。thinking将默认启用
        self.model = "kimi-k2-thinking"

    def get_tools(self, formula_uri: str):
        """从 Formula API 获取工具定义"""
        response = self.httpx.get(f"/formulas/{formula_uri}/tools")
        response.raise_for_status()  # 检查 HTTP 状态码
        
        try:
            return response.json().get("tools", [])
        except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
            print(f"错误: 无法解析响应为 JSON (状态码: {response.status_code})")
            print(f"响应内容: {response.text[:500]}")
            raise

    def call_tool(self, formula_uri: str, function: str, args: dict):
        """调用官方工具"""
        response = self.httpx.post(
            f"/formulas/{formula_uri}/fibers",
            json={"name": function, "arguments": json.dumps(args)},
        )
        response.raise_for_status()  # 检查 HTTP 状态码
        fiber = response.json()
        
        if fiber.get("status", "") == "succeeded":
            return fiber["context"].get("output") or fiber["context"].get("encrypted_output")
        
        if "error" in fiber:
            return f"Error: {fiber['error']}"
        if "error" in fiber.get("context", {}):
            return f"Error: {fiber['context']['error']}"
        return "Error: Unknown error"

    def close(self):
        """关闭客户端连接"""
        self.httpx.close()


```

--------------------------------

### 构建下一轮消息以处理工具调用 (Python 示例)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-official-tools

演示了如何构建 `messages` 数组以响应模型返回的工具调用。这包括添加一个 `role: 'tool'` 的消息，其 `content` 是工具的输出（如加密的搜索结果），并且 `tool_call_id` 必须与模型返回的 `tool_calls.id` 匹配。

```python
messages = [
  { 
    /* other messages */
    { 
      "role": "assistant",
      "tool_calls": [
        {
          "id": "web_search:0",
          "type": "function",
          "function": {
            "name": "web_search",
            "arguments": "{\"query\": \"天蓝色的 RGB 是什么？\" }"
          }
        }
      ]
    },
    {
      "role": "tool",
      "tool_call_id": "web_search:0", 
      "content": "----MOONSHOT ENCRYPTED BEGIN----+nf6...DSM=----MOONSHOT ENCRYPTED END----"
    }
  ]
]
```

### Model Pricing

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/kimi-k2-5-quickstart

Details on the pricing structure for the Kimi K2.5 model, including input and output costs based on token usage.

```APIDOC
## Kimi K2.5 Model Pricing

### Description
This table outlines the pricing for the Kimi K2.5 model, detailing costs per 1 million tokens for input (with and without cache hits) and output, as well as the model's context length.

### Pricing Table
| Model     | Billing Unit | Input Price (Cache Hit) | Input Price (Cache Miss) | Output Price | Model Context Length |
|-----------|--------------|-------------------------|--------------------------|--------------|----------------------|
| kimi-k2.5 | 1M tokens    | ￥0.70                  | ￥4.00                   | ￥21.00       | 262,144 tokens       |
```

### Upload Multiple Files for Conversation (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/files

Uploads multiple files and prepares them as system messages for a conversation with the Kimi model. This allows Kimi to understand and summarize content from several documents simultaneously.

```Python
from typing import *

import os
import json
from pathlib import Path

from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    base_url="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
    # We will get the value of the MOONSHOT_DEMO_API_KEY environment variable as the API Key,
    # please ensure that you have set the MOONSHOT_DEMO_API_KEY value correctly in the environment variable
    api_key=os.environ["MOONSHOT_DEMO_API_KEY"],
)


def upload_files(files: List[str]) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
    """
    upload_files will upload all incoming files (paths) through the file upload interface '/v1/files' and obtain the uploaded
    file content to generate file messages. Each file will be an independent message, and the role of these messages will be
    system, and the Kimi large model will correctly recognize the file content in these system messages.

    :param files: A list of paths to the files to be uploaded, paths can be absolute or relative paths, please use strings
        to pass file paths.
    :return: A list of messages containing file content, please add these messages to the Context,
        i.e., to the messages parameter when requesting the '/v1/chat/completions' interface.
    """
    messages = []

    # For each file path, we will upload the file and extract the file content, and finally generate a role system message, and add it
    # to the final returned messages list.
    for file in files:
        file_object = client.files.create(file=Path(file), purpose="file-extract")
        file_content = client.files.content(file_id=file_object.id).text
        messages.append({
            "role": "system",
            "content": file_content,
        })

    return messages


def main():
    file_messages = upload_files(files=["upload_files.py"])

    messages = [
        # We use the * syntax to deconstruct the file_messages message, making it the first N messages in the messages list.
        *file_messages,
        {
            "role": "system",
            "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，"
                       "准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不"
                       "可翻译成其他语言。",
        },
        {
            "role": "user",
            "content": "总结一下这些文件的内容。",
        },
    ]

    print(json.dumps(messages, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False))

    completion = client.chat.completions.create(
        model="kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
        messages=messages,
    )

    print(completion.choices[0].message.content)


if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()

```

### Shell Script for Invoking Web Search Formula

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-official-tools

This shell script demonstrates how to invoke the 'web-search' formula using a POST request to the Moonshot API. It sets the necessary environment variables for the formula URI and base URL, and includes the API key for authorization.

```bash
export FORMULA_URI="moonshot/web-search:latest"
export MOONSHOT_BASE_URL="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1"

curl -X POST ${MOONSHOT_BASE_URL}/formulas/${FORMULA_URI}/fibers \
-H "Content-Type: application/json" \
-H "Authorization: Bearer $MOONSHOT_API_KEY" \
-d '{ "name": "web_search", "arguments": "{\"query\": \"月之暗面最近有什么消息\"}" }'
```

### Implement Search Tool for Moonshot AI Platform (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-web-search

Provides the core implementation for the search tool within the Moonshot AI platform. The `search_impl` function is designed to return arguments directly, ensuring compatibility when switching models. The `chat` function handles model interactions, including invoking the `$web_search` tool and processing its results, along with printing token usage statistics.

```python
import json
from typing import Dict, Any

# Assume 'client' and 'Choice' are defined elsewhere
# from some_module import client, Choice

def search_impl(arguments: Dict[str, Any]) -> Any:
    """
    When using the search tool provided by Moonshot AI, simply return the arguments as is,
    without additional processing logic.

    However, if you wish to use other models while retaining internet search capabilities,
    you only need to modify the implementation here (e.g., by calling search and fetching web content).
    The function signature remains unchanged, ensuring compatibility.

    This maximizes compatibility, allowing you to switch between different models
    without requiring destructive code modifications.
    """
    return arguments

def chat(messages) -> Choice:
    completion = client.chat.completions.create(
        model="kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
        messages=messages,
        temperature=0.6,
        max_tokens=32768,
        tools=[
            {
                "type": "builtin_function",
                "function": {
                    "name": "$web_search",
                },
            }
        ]
    )
    usage = completion.usage
    choice = completion.choices[0]

    # =========================================================================
    # By checking finish_reason = stop, we print the consumed Tokens after the web search process is complete
    if choice.finish_reason == "stop":
        print(f"chat_prompt_tokens:          {usage.prompt_tokens}")
        print(f"chat_completion_tokens:      {usage.completion_tokens}")
        print(f"chat_total_tokens:           {usage.total_tokens}")
    # =========================================================================

    return choice

def main():
    messages = [
        {"role": "system", "content": "你是 Kimi。"},
    ]

    # Initial question
    messages.append({
        "role": "user",
        "content": "请搜索 Moonshot AI Context Caching 技术，并告诉我它是什么。"
    })

    finish_reason = None
    while finish_reason is None or finish_reason == "tool_calls":
        choice = chat(messages)
        finish_reason = choice.finish_reason
        if finish_reason == "tool_calls":
            messages.append(choice.message)
            for tool_call in choice.message.tool_calls:
                tool_call_name = tool_call.function.name
                tool_call_arguments = json.loads(
                    tool_call.function.arguments)
                if tool_call_name == "$web_search":

                    # ===================================================================
                    # We print the Tokens generated by the web search results during the web search process
                    search_content_total_tokens = tool_call_arguments.get("usage", {}).get("total_tokens")
                    print(f"search_content_total_tokens: {search_content_total_tokens}")
                    # ===================================================================

                    tool_result = search_impl(tool_call_arguments)
                else:
                    tool_result = f"Error: unable to find tool by name '{tool_call_name}'"

                messages.append({
                    "role": "tool",
                    "tool_call_id": tool_call.id,
                    "name": tool_call_name,
                    "content": json.dumps(tool_result),
                })

    print(choice.message.content)


if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()

```

--------------------------------

### 使用 Kimi API 处理多文件问答 (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-api-for-file-based-qa

演示如何使用 Python 和 Kimi API 上传多个文件，并将每个文件的内容作为独立的系统提示词添加到消息列表中，实现针对多个文件的问答。此功能有助于整合不同文档的信息。

```python
from typing import *

import os
import json
from pathlib import Path

from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key="MOONSHOT_API_KEY", # 在这里将 MOONSHOT_API_KEY 替换为你从 Kimi 开放平台申请的 API Key
    base_url="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)


def upload_files(files: List[str]) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
    """
    upload_files 会将传入的文件（路径）全部通过文件上传接口 '/v1/files' 上传，并获取上传后的
    文件内容生成文件 messages。每个文件会是一个独立的 message，这些 message 的 role 均为
    system，Kimi 大模型会正确识别这些 system messages 中的文件内容。

    :param files: 一个包含要上传文件的路径的列表，路径可以是绝对路径也可以是相对路径，请使用字符串
        的形式传递文件路径。
    :return: 一个包含了文件内容的 messages 列表，请将这些 messages 加入到 Context 中，
        即请求 `/v1/chat/completions` 接口时的 messages 参数中。
    """
    messages = []

    # 对每个文件路径，我们都会上传文件并抽取文件内容，最后生成一个 role 为 system 的 message，并加入
    # 到最终返回的 messages 列表中。
    for file in files:
        file_object = client.files.create(file=Path(file), purpose="file-extract")
        file_content = client.files.content(file_id=file_object.id).text
        messages.append({
            "role": "system",
            "content": file_content,
        })

    return messages


def main():
    file_messages = upload_files(files=["upload_files.py"])

    messages = [
        # 我们使用 * 语法，来解构 file_messages 消息，使其成为 messages 列表的前 N 条 messages。
        *file_messages,
        {
            "role": "system",
            "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，"
                       "准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不"
                       "可翻译成其他语言。",
        },
        {
            "role": "user",
            "content": "总结一下这些文件的内容。",
        },
    ]

    print(json.dumps(messages, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False))

    completion = client.chat.completions.create(
        model="kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
        messages=messages,
    )

    print(completion.choices[0].message.content)


if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()

```

```shell
$ curl https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/chat/completions \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -H "Authorization: Bearer $MOONSHOT_API_KEY" \
    -d '{
        "model": "kimi-k2-thinking",
        "messages": [
            {
                "role": "system",
                "content": "你是 Kimi。"
            },
            {
                "role": "user",
                "content": "请解释 1+1=2。"
            }
        ],
        "temperature": 1.0
   }'

```

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/prompt-best-practice

```json
{
  "messages": [
    {"role": "system", "content": "你将收到两篇相同类别的文章，文章用XML标签分割。首先概括每篇文章的论点，然后指出哪篇文章提出了更好的论点，并解释原因。"},
    {"role": "user", "content": "<article>在这里插入文章</article><article>在这里插入文章</article>"}
  ]
}
```

### 使用 Kimi API 上传文件并进行问答 (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-api-for-file-based-qa

演示如何使用 Python 和 Kimi API 上传单个文件（文本或图片），抽取文件内容，并将其作为系统提示词与用户问题一同发送给模型以获取回答。需要安装 openai 库。

```python
from pathlib import Path
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key="MOONSHOT_API_KEY", # 在这里将 MOONSHOT_API_KEY 替换为你从 Kimi 开放平台申请的 API Key
    base_url="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

# moonshot.pdf 是一个示例文件, 我们支持文本文件和图片文件，对于图片文件，我们提供了 OCR 的能力
# 上传文件时，我们可以直接使用 openai 库的文件上传 API，使用标准库 pathlib 中的 Path 构造文件
# 对象，并将其传入 file 参数即可，同时将 purpose 参数设置为 file-extract；注意，目前文件上传
# 接口仅支持 file-extract 一种 purpose 值。
file_object = client.files.create(file=Path("moonshot.pdf"), purpose="file-extract")

# 获取结果
# file_content = client.files.retrieve_content(file_id=file_object.id)
# 注意，某些旧版本示例中的 retrieve_content API 在最新版本标记了 warning, 可以用下面这行代替
# （如果使用旧版本的 SDK，可以继续延用 retrieve_content API）
file_content = client.files.content(file_id=file_object.id).text

# 把文件内容通过系统提示词 system prompt 放进请求中
messages = [
    {
        "role": "system",
        "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。",
    },
    {
        "role": "system",
        "content": file_content, # <-- 这里，我们将抽取后的文件内容（注意是文件内容，而不是文件 ID）放置在请求中
    },
    {"role": "user", "content": "请简单介绍 moonshot.pdf 的具体内容"},
]

# 然后调用 chat-completion, 获取 Kimi 的回答
completion = client.chat.completions.create(
  model="kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
  messages=messages,
  temperature=0.6,
)

print(completion.choices[0].message)

```

--------------------------------

### Python: Chat Completion with Tool Calls for Web Search

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-web-search

This Python function `chat` demonstrates how to perform chat completions using the Moonshot AI client, specifically enabling the `$web_search` tool. It configures the completion request to include the tool definition and processes the response, handling tool calls by appending them to the message history and executing the `search_impl` function.

```python
from openai import OpenAI
from openai.types.chat.chat_completion import Choice
import os
import json

client = OpenAI(
    base_url="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
    api_key=os.environ.get("MOONSHOT_API_KEY"),
)

def chat(messages) -> Choice:
    completion = client.chat.completions.create(
        model="kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
        messages=messages,
        temperature=0.6,
        max_tokens=32768,
        tools=[
            {
                "type": "builtin_function",  # <-- Use builtin_function to declare the $web_search function, please include the tools declaration completely in each request
                "function": {
                    "name": "$web_search",
                },
            }
        ]
    )
    return completion.choices[0]
```

--------------------------------

### Execute Local Python Code and Convert to PDF (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-k2-to-setup-agent

This function executes provided Python code using the system's Python interpreter. It first checks if the code contains specific keywords indicating local execution. If so, it runs the code, captures output, and then attempts to convert any newly generated .tex files to PDF using the `convert_tex_to_pdf` method. Error handling is included for execution failures.

```python
def execute_code_runner(self, args):
        code = args.get("code", "") if isinstance(args, dict) else str(args or "")
        
        if not code or not any(keyword in code for keyword in self.local_execution_keywords):
            return
        before_tex_files = set(glob.glob('*.tex'))
        try:
            subprocess.run(
                [sys.executable, "-c", common_code+code],
                capture_output=True,
                text=True,
                check=True,
            )
            after_tex_files = set(glob.glob('*.tex'))
            new_tex_files = after_tex_files - before_tex_files
            for tex_file in new_tex_files:
                self.convert_tex_to_pdf(tex_file)
                
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"  [Local execution failed: {e}]")
```

--------------------------------

### Python: Main Execution Flow for Moonshot AI Chat with Search

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-web-search

The `main` function orchestrates a chat interaction with the Moonshot AI model, incorporating web search capabilities. It initializes messages, appends user queries, and enters a loop to handle tool calls. When a `$web_search` tool call is detected, it invokes `search_impl` and appends the tool's result back to the message history for the model to process.

```python
def main():
    messages = [
        {"role": "system", "content": "你是 Kimi。"},
    ]

    # Initial question
    messages.append({
        "role": "user",
        "content": "请搜索 Moonshot AI Context Caching 技术，并告诉我它是什么。"
    })

    finish_reason = None
    while finish_reason is None or finish_reason == "tool_calls":
        choice = chat(messages)
        finish_reason = choice.finish_reason
        if finish_reason == "tool_calls":  # <-- Determine if the current response contains tool_calls
            messages.append(choice.message)  # <-- Add the assistant's message back to the context for the next request
            for tool_call in choice.message.tool_calls:  # <-- tool_calls can be multiple, so loop through each one
                tool_call_name = tool_call.function.name
                tool_call_arguments = json.loads(tool_call.function.arguments)  # <-- arguments is a serialized JSON Object, needs json.loads
                if tool_call_name == "$web_search":
                    tool_result = search_impl(tool_call_arguments)
                else:
                    tool_result = f"Error: unable to find tool by name '{tool_call_name}'"

                # Construct a role=tool message with the function execution result;
                # Note: provide tool_call_id and name fields in the message for correct matching.
                messages.append({
                    "role": "tool",
                    "tool_call_id": tool_call.id,
                    "name": tool_call_name,
                    "content": json.dumps(tool_result),  # <-- Submit tool call results as a string, serialize with json.dumps
                })

    print(choice.message.content)  # <-- Print the model's final response to the user


if __name__ == '__main__':
    main()
```

--------------------------------

### Direct API Call using OpenAI SDK (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/agent-support

Demonstrates how to make a chat completion request to the Moonshot API using the OpenAI Python SDK. It configures the client with the API key and base URL, then sends a message to the specified model. Requires Python >= 3.7.1 and OpenAI SDK >= 1.0.0.

```python
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key = "$MOONSHOT_API_KEY",
    base_url = "https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

completion = client.chat.completions.create(
    model = "kimi-k2-0905-preview",
    messages = [
        {"role": "system", "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"},
        {"role": "user", "content": "你好，我叫李雷，1+1等于多少？"}
    ],
    temperature = 0.6,
)

print(completion.choices[0].message.content)
```

### 调用 Kimi API 进行对话 (Python, Node.js)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/start-using-kimi-api

使用 OpenAI SDK 调用 Kimi API 进行对话。需要提供 API Key 和模型名称。支持 Python 和 Node.js 环境。API 完全兼容 OpenAI 格式。

```python
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key="MOONSHOT_API_KEY", # 在这里将 MOONSHOT_API_KEY 替换为你从 Kimi 开放平台申请的 API Key
    base_url="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

completion = client.chat.completions.create(
    model = "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
    messages = [
        {"role": "system", "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"},
        {"role": "user", "content": "你好，我叫李雷，1+1等于多少？"}
    ],
    temperature = 0.6,
)

# 通过 API 我们获得了 Kimi 大模型给予我们的回复消息（role=assistant）
print(completion.choices[0].message.content)
```

```node.js
import OpenAI from 'openai';

const openai = new OpenAI({
  apiKey: 'MOONSHOT_API_KEY', // 在这里将 MOONSHOT_API_KEY 替换为你从 Kimi 开放平台申请的 API Key
  baseURL: 'https://api.moonshot.cn/v1',
});

async function main() {
  const completion = await openai.chat.completions.create({
    model: 'kimi-k2-turbo-preview',
    messages: [
      { 'role': 'system', 'content': '你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。' },
      { 'role': 'user', 'content': '你好，我叫李雷，1+1等于多少？' },
    ],
    temperature: 0.6,
  });

  console.log(completion.choices[0].message.content);
}

main();
```
