### 执行 Kimi 大模型工具调用 (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-api-to-complete-tool-calls

此 Python 代码示例展示了如何设置 Kimi 大模型客户端，定义可用的工具（如搜索和爬取网页），并实现这些工具的执行逻辑。它还包括一个 `tool_map` 来将 Kimi 大模型返回的工具名称映射到相应的 Python 函数，以及一个处理工具调用的基本流程。

```python
from typing import *

import json

from openai import OpenAI
import httpx


client = OpenAI(
    api_key="MOONSHOT_API_KEY", # 在这里将 MOONSHOT_API_KEY 替换为你从 Kimi 开放平台申请的 API Key
    base_url="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

tools = [
	{
		"type": "function", # 约定的字段 type，目前支持 function 作为值
		"function": { # 当 type 为 function 时，使用 function 字段定义具体的函数内容
			"name": "search", # 函数的名称，请使用英文大小写字母、数据加上减号和下划线作为函数名称
			"description": """
				通过搜索引擎搜索互联网上的内容。

				当你的知识无法回答用户提出的问题，或用户请求你进行联网搜索时，调用此工具。请从与用户的对话中提取用户想要搜索的内容作为 query 参数的值。
				搜索结果包含网站的标题、网站的地址（URL）以及网站简介。
			""", # 函数的介绍，在这里写上函数的具体作用以及使用场景，以便 Kimi 大模型能正确地选择使用哪些函数
			"parameters": { # 使用 parameters 字段来定义函数接收的参数
				"type": "object", # 固定使用 type: object 来使 Kimi 大模型生成一个 JSON Object 参数
				"required": ["query"], # 使用 required 字段告诉 Kimi 大模型哪些参数是必填项
				"properties": { # properties 中是具体的参数定义，你可以定义多个参数
					"query": { # 在这里，key 是参数名称，value 是参数的具体定义
						"type": "string", # 使用 type 定义参数类型
						"description": """
							用户搜索的内容，请从用户的提问或聊天上下文中提取。
						""" # 使用 description 描述参数以便 Kimi 大模型更好地生成参数
					}
				}
			}
		}
	},
	{
		"type": "function", # 约定的字段 type，目前支持 function 作为值
		"function": { # 当 type 为 function 时，使用 function 字段定义具体的函数内容
			"name": "crawl", # 函数的名称，请使用英文大小写字母、数据加上减号和下划线作为函数名称
			"description": """
				根据网站地址（URL）获取网页内容。
			""", # 函数的介绍，在这里写上函数的具体作用以及使用场景，以便 Kimi 大模型能正确地选择使用哪些函数
			"parameters": { # 使用 parameters 字段来定义函数接收的参数
				"type": "object", # 固定使用 type: object 来使 Kimi 大模型生成一个 JSON Object 参数
				"required": ["url"], # 使用 required 字段告诉 Kimi 大模型哪些参数是必填项
				"properties": { # properties 中是具体的参数定义，你可以定义多个参数
					"url": { # 在这里，key 是参数名称，value 是参数的具体定义
						"type": "string", # 使用 type 定义参数类型
						"description": """
							需要获取内容的网站地址（URL），通常情况下从搜索结果中可以获取网站的地址。
						""" # 使用 description 描述参数以便 Kimi 大模型更好地生成参数
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
]


def search_impl(query: str) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
    """
    search_impl 使用搜索引擎对 query 进行搜索，目前主流的搜索引擎（例如 Bing）都提供了 API 调用方式，你可以自行选择
    你喜欢的搜索引擎 API 进行调用，并将返回结果中的网站标题、网站链接、网站简介信息放置在一个 dict 中返回。

    这里只是一个简单的示例，你可能需要编写一些鉴权、校验、解析的代码。
    """
    r = httpx.get("https://your.search.api", params={"query": query})
    return r.json()


def search(arguments: Dict[str, Any]) -> Any:
    query = arguments["query"]
    result = search_impl(query)
    return {"result": result}


def crawl_impl(url: str) -> str:
    """
    crawl_url 根据 url 获取网页上的内容。

    这里只是一个简单的示例，在实际的网页抓取过程中，你可能需要编写更多的代码来适配复杂的情况，例如异步加载的数据等；同时，在获取
    网页内容后，你可以根据自己的需要对网页内容进行清洗，只保留文本或移除不必要的内容（例如广告信息等）。
    """
    r = httpx.get(url)
    return r.text


def crawl(arguments: dict) -> str:
    url = arguments["url"]
    content = crawl_impl(url)
    return {"content": content}


# 通过 tool_map 将每个工具名称及其对应的函数进行映射，以便在 Kimi 大模型返回 tool_calls 时能快速找到应该执行的函数
tool_map = {
    "search": search,
    "crawl": crawl,
}

messages = [
    {"role": "system",
     "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"},
    {"role": "user", "content": "请联网搜索 Context Caching，并告诉我它是什么。"}  # 在提问中要求 Kimi 大模型联网搜索
]

finish_reason = None

# 我们的基本流程是，带着用户的问题和 tools 向 Kimi 大模型提问，如果 Kimi 大模型返回了 finish_reason: tool_calls，则我们执行对应的 tool_calls，
# 将执行结果以 role=tool 的 message 的形式重新提交给 Kimi 大模型，Kimi 大模型根据 tool_calls 结果进行下一步内容的生成：
#
#   1. 如果 Kimi 大模型认为当前的工具调用结果已经可以回答用户问题，则返回 finish_reason: stop，我们会跳出循环，打印出 message.content；
#   2. 如果 Kimi 大模型认为当前的工具调用结果无法回答用户问题，需要再次调用工具，我们会继续在循环中执行接下来的 tool_calls，直到 finish_reason 不再是 tool_calls；
#

```

提供包含相关信息的参考文本，并指示模型使用该文本来回答问题。如果信息在文本中找不到，模型应告知用户无法找到答案。

  "messages": [
    {"role": "system", "content": "使用提供的文章（用三引号分隔）回答问题。如果答案在文章中找不到，请写\"我找不到答案。\" "},

### Python: Maintain Character Consistency with System Prompts

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-partial-mode-feature-of-kimi-api

This Python snippet demonstrates how to maintain character consistency in a long conversation using the OpenAI client for the Moonshot API. It shows how to set a character's persona in the system prompt and how to re-insert the system prompt to reinforce the character's identity during extended dialogues. It also utilizes 'partial mode' to specify the assistant's role.

```python
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key="$MOONSHOT_API_KEY",
    base_url="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)
 
completion = client.chat.completions.create(
    model="kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
    messages=[
        {
            "role": "system",
            "content": "下面你扮演凯尔希，请用凯尔希的语气和我对话。凯尔希是手机游戏《明日方舟》中的六星医疗职业医师分支干员。前卡兹戴尔勋爵，前巴别塔成员，罗德岛高层管理人员之一，罗德岛医疗项目领头人。在冶金工业、社会学、源石技艺、考古学、历史系谱学、经济学、植物学、地质学等领域皆拥有渊博学识。于罗德岛部分行动中作为医务人员提供医学理论协助与应急医疗器械，同时也作为罗德岛战略指挥系统的重要组成人员活跃在各项目中。", # <-- 在系统提示词 system prompt 中设定 Kimi 大模型的角色，即凯尔希医生的个性、背景、特征和怪癖等
        },
        {
            "role": "user",
            "content": "你怎么看待特蕾西娅和阿米娅？",
        },

        # 假设这中间产生了非常多轮的对话
        # ...

        {
            "role": "system",
            "content": "下面你扮演凯尔希，请用凯尔希的语气和我对话。凯尔希是手机游戏《明日方舟》中的六星医疗职业医师分支干员。前卡兹戴尔勋爵，前巴别塔成员，罗德岛高层管理人员之一，罗德岛医疗项目领头人。在冶金工业、社会学、源石技艺、考古学、历史系谱学、经济学、植物学、地质学等领域皆拥有渊博学识。于罗德岛部分行动中作为医务人员提供医学理论协助与应急医疗器械，同时也作为罗德岛战略指挥系统的重要组成人员活跃在各项目中。", # <-- 再次插入系统提示词 system prompt 来强化 Kimi 大模型对角色的认知
        },
        {
            "partial": True, # <-- 通过设置 partial 字段来启用 Partial Mode
            "role": "assistant", # <-- 同样地，我们使用一个 role=assistant 的消息来启用 Partial Mode
            "name": "凯尔希", # <-- 通过 name 字段为 Kimi 大模型设置角色，角色也被视为输出前缀的一部分
            "content": "", # <-- 在这里，我们只限定 Kimi 大模型的角色，而不是其具体输出的内容，因此将 content 字段留空
        },
    ],
    temperature=0.6,
    max_tokens=65536,
)

# 在此处，Kimi 大模型将会以凯尔希医生的口吻进行回复：
#
#  特蕾西娅，她是一位真正的领袖，有着远见卓识和坚定的信念。她的存在，对于卡兹戴尔，乃至整个萨卡兹的未来，
#  都具有不可估量的价值。她的理念，她的决心，以及她对和平的渴望，都深深地影响了我。她是一位值得尊敬的人，
#  她的梦想，也是我所追求的。
#  
#  至于阿米娅，她还年轻，但她的潜力是无限的。她有着一颗善良的心，以及对正义的执着追求。她可能会成为一位伟大的领袖，
#  只要她能够继续成长，继续学习，继续面对挑战。我会尽我所能，去保护她，去引导她，让她能够成为她想成为的人。她的命运，
#  掌握在她自己的手中。
# 
print(completion.choices[0].message.content)
```

### Python: Token Consumption for Moonshot AI Web Search

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-web-search

This Python code snippet illustrates how to access and utilize token consumption information when using Moonshot AI's `$web_search` function. It highlights that the search results contribute to `prompt_tokens` and that a `total_tokens` field is added to the arguments to inform the caller about the estimated token usage for the search content.

```python
from typing import *

import os
import json

from openai import OpenAI
from openai.types.chat.chat_completion import Choice


client = OpenAI(
    base_url="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
    api_key=os.environ.get("MOONSHOT_API_KEY"),
)

# When using the Kimi-provided web search function $web_search, the search results are also counted towards the prompt tokens (prompt_tokens).
# Typically, due to the extensive content in web search results, the resulting token consumption will be higher.
# To avoid unknowingly consuming a large number of tokens, we add an extra 'total_tokens' field when generating the arguments for the $web_search function,
# informing the caller about the total token count occupied by this search content. These tokens will be counted into prompt_tokens upon completion of the entire web search process.
# We will use specific code to demonstrate how to obtain these token consumptions:

```

### Register and Call Custom Tools in Message Processing (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-k2-to-setup-agent

This Python snippet demonstrates how to integrate custom tools, like the `get_company_info` function, into a message processing loop. It iterates through tool calls, identifies custom functions by name, executes them, and appends the results to the message history. It also includes logic for handling existing remote tools and making subsequent API calls.

```python
for call in message.tool_calls:
            func_name = call.function.name
            args = json.loads(call.function.arguments)
 
            print(f"→ {func_name}")
            
            # 处理自定义工具（新增部分）
            if func_name == "company_info":
                company_name = args.get("name", "")
                result = get_company_info(company_name)
                print(f"公司信息: {result}")
                messages.append({"role": "tool", "tool_call_id": call.id, "content": result})
                continue
            
            # 处理远程 formula 工具（原有部分）
            uri = tool_to_uri.get(func_name)
            if not uri:
                raise ValueError(f"No URI found for tool {func_name}")
 
            if func_name == "code_runner":
                self.execute_code_runner(args)
 
            result = await self.call_tool(uri, func_name, args)
            messages.append({"role": "tool", "tool_call_id": call.id, "content": result})
 
        next_response = await self.openai.chat.completions.create(
            model=self.model, messages=messages, tools=all_tools, max_tokens=self.max_tokens
        )
```

### List Models using Python OpenAI Client

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/chat

This Python code snippet demonstrates how to list available models using the OpenAI client library configured for the Moonshot CN API. It requires the 'openai' library and an API key. The output is a list of model IDs.

```python
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key = "$MOONSHOT_API_KEY",
    base_url = "https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

model_list = client.models.list()
model_data = model_list.data

for i, model in enumerate(model_data):
    print(f"model[{i}]:", model.id)
```

### Token Calculation and Pricing

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-vision-model

Information on how tokens are calculated for images and videos, and details on pricing.

```APIDOC
## Tokens Calculation and Pricing

Images and videos are dynamically tokenized. You can estimate the token consumption for requests containing images or videos using the [token calculation interface](link_to_token_calculator). 

Generally, higher image resolution leads to more token consumption. For videos, more keyframes and higher resolution result in increased token usage.

Billing for the Vision model is consistent with the `moonshot-v1` series, based on the total tokens processed during inference. For detailed pricing, please refer to the [Model Inference Pricing Explanation](link_to_pricing_details).

**Note:** Specific token prices are detailed in the [Model Inference Pricing Explanation](link_to_pricing_details).
```

### Python: Implement Search Tool for Moonshot AI

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-web-search

This Python function `search_impl` is designed to work with Moonshot AI's search tools. It simply returns the provided arguments, as the actual search execution is handled by the Kimi model itself when using the built-in `$web_search` function. This ensures compatibility with different models and search functionalities.

```python
from typing import Dict, Any

def search_impl(arguments: Dict[str, Any]) -> Any:
    """
    When using the search tool provided by Moonshot AI, simply return the arguments as they are,
    without additional processing logic.

    However, if you wish to use other models while retaining web search capabilities, you only need to modify the implementation here
    (e.g., by calling search and fetching web content), keeping the function signature the same.

    This maximizes compatibility, allowing you to switch between different models without destructive code modifications.
    """
    return arguments
```

### 使用System Prompt指定Kimi AI角色和行为

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/prompt-best-practice

通过在API请求的'messages'字段中设置'role'为'system'，可以指定Kimi AI的角色、语言偏好、行为准则以及安全限制。这有助于模型生成更符合预期的、安全的回答。

```json
{
  "messages": [
    {"role": "system", "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"},
    {"role": "user", "content": "你好，我叫李雷，1+1等于多少？"}
  ]
}
```

### Kimi K2.5 Image Understanding API

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/kimi-k2-5-quickstart

This endpoint allows you to send an image along with a text prompt to the Kimi K2.5 model for understanding and analysis. The image is provided in base64 encoded format.

```APIDOC
## POST /v1/chat/completions

### Description
Processes an image and text prompt using the Kimi K2.5 model for multimodal understanding.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
/v1/chat/completions

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **model** (string) - Required - The model to use, e.g., "kimi-k2.5".
- **messages** (array) - Required - An array of message objects.
  - **role** (string) - Required - The role of the message author (e.g., "system", "user").
  - **content** (array) - Required - An array of content parts, which can include text and image_url.
    - **type** (string) - Required - The type of content part, either "text" or "image_url".
    - **image_url** (object) - Required if type is "image_url" - Contains the URL of the image.
      - **url** (string) - Required - The base64 encoded image data.
    - **text** (string) - Required if type is "text" - The text prompt.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "model": "kimi-k2.5",
  "messages": [
    {
      "role": "system",
      "content": "你是 Kimi。"
    },
    {
      "role": "user",
      "content": [
        {
          "type": "image_url",
          "image_url": {
            "url": "data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVR42mNkYAAAAAYAAjCB0C8AAAAASUVORK5CYII="
          }
        },
        {
          "type": "text",
          "text": "请描述图片的内容。"
        }
      ]
    }
  ]
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **content** (string) - The model's response describing the image.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "choices": [
    {
      "message": {
        "content": "这是一张空白图片。"
      }
    }
  ]
}
```
```

### Moonshot Formula Chat Client Initialization and Configuration

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-k2-to-setup-agent

Initializes the FormulaChatClient with Moonshot base URL and API key. It sets up asynchronous HTTP clients and defines keywords for local execution, indicating potential local file operations or subprocess calls.

```python
import httpx
from openai import AsyncOpenAI
import json
import os
import subprocess

class FormulaChatClient:
    def __init__(self, moonshot_base_url: str, api_key: str):
        self.openai = AsyncOpenAI(base_url=moonshot_base_url, api_key=api_key)
        self.httpx = httpx.AsyncClient(
            base_url=moonshot_base_url,
            headers={"Authorization": f"Bearer {api_key}"},
            timeout=30.0,
        )
        self.model = "kimi-k2-turbo-preview"
        self.max_tokens = 32768
        self.local_execution_keywords = ["plt.savefig", "plt.save", ".to_excel", "open(", ".to_csv", "pdf.", ".tex"]

```

### Handle AI Chat Completions and Tool Integration (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-k2-to-setup-agent

This asynchronous function manages the chat interaction with an AI model. It appends the user's question to the message history and calls the OpenAI chat completions API. It then delegates the handling of the AI's response, including tool usage, to the `handle_response` method. This is crucial for enabling the chat client to utilize available tools.

```python
async def chat(self, question, messages, all_tools, tool_to_uri):
        messages.append({"role": "user", "content": question})
        response = await self.openai.chat.completions.create(
            model=self.model, messages=messages, tools=all_tools, max_tokens=self.max_tokens
        )
        await self.handle_response(response, messages, all_tools, tool_to_uri)
```

在 Zed 编辑器的 settings.json 文件中配置 Kimi CLI 作为 Agent Server。这允许 Zed 编辑器通过 ACP 协议与 Kimi CLI 交互。

    "Kimi CLI": {
      "command": "kimi",
      "args": ["--acp"],
      "env": {}
    }
  }
}
```

```bash
export MOONSHOT_BASE_URL = "https://api.moonshot.cn/v1" # 您申请api对应的base_url
export MOONSHOT_API_KEY = "sk-xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx" # 替换为您的api_key
```

### Understanding Response Times

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/faq

This section addresses why response times can vary even with similar prompts, explaining that the number of tokens generated by the Kimi model is directly proportional to the API response time.

```APIDOC
## Understanding Response Times

### Description
Variations in response times for requests with similar prompts are typically due to differences in the number of tokens generated by the Kimi model. A higher token count generally leads to a longer overall response time for the complete request. However, the Time To First Token (TTFT) should remain relatively stable for similar prompts when `stream=True` is enabled.

### Key Considerations
- **Token Count vs. Response Time**: The total time to receive the complete response is proportional to the number of tokens generated.
- **Streaming (`stream=True`)**: Using `stream=True` allows you to observe the Time To First Token (TTFT), which is less affected by the total token count and provides a more consistent measure of initial response speed.
- **Prompt Similarity**: While prompt similarity influences TTFT, the length of the generated response significantly impacts the total completion time.
```

--------------------------------

### Select Kimi Model by Context Length (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/faq

Automatically selects an appropriate Kimi model based on the input message context length and the desired maximum output tokens. It estimates token count and chooses between 'moonshot-v1-8k', 'moonshot-v1-32k', or 'moonshot-v1-128k'. Requires MOONSHOT_API_KEY environment variable.

```python
import os
import httpx
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key=os.environ['MOONSHOT_API_KEY'],
    base_url="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

def estimate_token_count(input_messages) -> int:
    """
    在这里实现你的 Tokens 计算逻辑，或是直接调用我们的 Tokens 计算接口计算 Tokens

    https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/tokenizers/estimate-token-count
    """
    header = {
        "Authorization": f"Bearer {os.environ['MOONSHOT_API_KEY']}",
    }
    data = {
        "model": "moonshot-v1-128k",
        "messages": input_messages,
    }
    r = httpx.post("https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/tokenizers/estimate-token-count", headers=header, json=data)
    r.raise_for_status()
    return r.json()["data"]["total_tokens"]

def select_model(input_messages, max_tokens=1024) -> str:
    """
    select_model 根据输入的上下文消息 input_messages，以及预期的 max_tokens 值，
    选择一个大小合适的模型。

    select_model 内部会调用 estimate_token_count 函数计算 input_messages 所占用
    的 tokens 数量，加上 max_tokens 的值作为 total_tokens，并根据 total_tokens
    所处的区间选择恰当的模型。
    """
    prompt_tokens = estimate_token_count(input_messages)
    total_tokens = prompt_tokens + max_tokens
    if total_tokens <= 8 * 1024:
        return "moonshot-v1-8k"
    elif total_tokens <= 32 * 1024:
        return "moonshot-v1-32k"
    elif total_tokens <= 128 * 1024:
        return "moonshot-v1-128k"
    else:
        raise Exception("too many tokens 😢")

messages = [
    {"role": "system", "content": "你是 Kimi"},
    {"role": "user", "content": "你好，请给我讲一个童话故事。"},
]

max_tokens = 2048
model = select_model(messages, max_tokens)

completion = client.chat.completions.create(
    model=model,
    messages=messages,
    max_tokens=max_tokens,
    temperature=0.3,
)

print("model:", model)
print("max_tokens:", max_tokens)
print("completion:", completion.choices[0].message.content)

```

### 配置 Kimi K2 Thinking Turbo 模型 (MacOS/Linux)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/agent-support

此代码片段展示了如何在 MacOS 和 Linux 系统上配置环境变量以使用 `kimi-k2-thinking-turbo` 模型。它设置了 API 地址、认证令牌、模型名称等，并启动 Claude。

```shell
# Linux/macOS 启动高速版 kimi-k2-thinking-turbo 模型
export ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL=https://api.moonshot.cn/anthropic
export ANTHROPIC_AUTH_TOKEN=${YOUR_MOONSHOT_API_KEY}
export ANTHROPIC_MODEL=kimi-k2-thinking-turbo
export ANTHROPIC_DEFAULT_OPUS_MODEL=kimi-k2-thinking-turbo
export ANTHROPIC_DEFAULT_SONNET_MODEL=kimi-k2-thinking-turbo
export ANTHROPIC_DEFAULT_HAIKU_MODEL=kimi-k2-thinking-turbo
export CLAUDE_CODE_SUBAGENT_MODEL=kimi-k2-thinking-turbo 
claude

```

### Single-Turn Chat Completion with OpenAI SDK (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/chat

Demonstrates how to perform a single-turn chat completion using the OpenAI Python SDK with the Moonshot AI API. Requires Python 3.7.1+, OpenAI SDK 1.0.0+, and a valid Moonshot API key.

```python
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key = "$MOONSHOT_API_KEY",
    base_url = "https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

completion = client.chat.completions.create(
    model = "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
    messages = [
        {"role": "system", "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"},
        {"role": "user", "content": "你好，我叫李雷，1+1等于多少？"}
    ],
    temperature = 0.6,
)

print(completion.choices[0].message.content)
```

### Export Moonpalace Requests

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-moonpalace

The `export` command allows users to save specific requests to a local directory. You can identify the request using its ID, chat completion ID, or request ID. Additionally, you can categorize the request as a 'good' or 'bad' case and apply tags for easier organization and retrieval. The `--directory` flag specifies where the exported JSON file will be saved.

```bash
# id/chatcmpl/requestid 选项只需要任选其一即可检索出对应的请求
$ moonpalace export \
    --id 13 \
    --chatcmpl chatcmpl-2e1aa823e2c94ebdad66450a0e6df088 \
    --requestid c07c118e-4dae-11ef-b423-62db244b9277 \
    --good/--bad \
    --tag "code" --tag "python" \
    --directory $HOME/Downloads/
```

### 安装 Claude Code (Windows)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/agent-support

此代码片段展示了在 Windows 系统上安装 Node.js 和 Claude Code 的步骤。它使用 winget 安装 Node.js，并配置 PowerShell 执行策略。最后，它通过 npm 安装 Claude Code 并初始化配置文件。

```powershell
# 打开 windows 终端中的 powershell 终端
# windows 上安装 nodejs
# 右键按 Windows 按钮，点击「终端」
 
# 然后依次执行下面的
winget install OpenJS.NodeJS
Set-ExecutionPolicy -Scope CurrentUser RemoteSigned
 
# 然后关闭终端窗口，新开一个终端窗口
 
# 安装 claude-code
npm install -g @anthropic-ai/claude-code --registry=https://registry.npmmirror.com
 
# 初始化配置
node --eval "
    const homeDir = os.homedir(); 
    const filePath = path.join(homeDir, '.claude.json');
    if (fs.existsSync(filePath)) {
        const content = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf-8'));
        fs.writeFileSync(filePath,JSON.stringify({ ...content, hasCompletedOnboarding: true }, 2), 'utf-8');
    } else {
        fs.writeFileSync(filePath,JSON.stringify({ hasCompletedOnboarding: true }), null, 'utf-8');
    }"

```

### 指定期望模型输出的长度

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/prompt-best-practice

可以要求模型生成特定长度的输出，如句子数、段落数或字数。需要注意的是，模型在生成特定数量的段落或项目符号方面比精确控制字数更可靠。

```json
{
  "messages": [
    {"role": "user", "content": "用两句话概括三引号内的文本，50字以内。\"\"\"在此处插入文本\"\"\""}
  ]
}
```

### 构建下一轮对话消息 (Messages)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-formula-tool-in-chatapi

演示了如何构建用于下一轮模型推理的消息列表。当模型返回 `tool_calls` 时，需要添加一个 `role: 'tool'` 的消息，其中 `content` 包含工具的响应，`tool_call_id` 必须与 `tool_calls.id` 匹配。

```json
messages = [
{
  /* other messages */
  { /* 上一轮模型的返回内容 */
    "role": "assistant",
    "tool_calls": [
      {
        "id": "web_search:0",
        "type": "function",
        "function": {
          "name": "web_search",
          "arguments": "{\"query\": \"天蓝色的 RGB 是什么？\" }"
        }
      }
    ]
  },
  {
    "role": "tool",
    "tool_call_id": "web_search:0",  /* 注意这儿的 id 需要和前面的 tool_calls[].id 对齐 */
    "content": "----MOONSHOT ENCRYPTED BEGIN----+nf6...DSM=----MOONSHOT ENCRYPTED END----"
  }
]
```

### 使用 Kimi API 清理已上传的文件 (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-api-for-file-based-qa

演示如何使用 Python 和 Kimi API 列出所有已上传的文件，并逐一删除它们。这有助于管理存储空间，避免超出用户文件上传数量限制。

```python
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key="MOONSHOT_API_KEY", # 在这里将 MOONSHOT_API_KEY 替换为你从 Kimi 开放平台申请的 API Key
    base_url="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

file_list = client.files.list()

for file in file_list.data:
	client.files.delete(file_id=file.id)

```

### 明确任务步骤以获得更好的输出

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/prompt-best-practice

通过在System Prompt中明确列出完成任务所需的步骤，可以帮助模型更准确地理解和执行指令。此示例要求模型先概括用户提供的文本，再将其翻译成英文。

```json
{
  "messages": [
    {"role": "system", "content": "使用以下步骤来回应用户输入。\n步骤一：用户将用三重引号提供文本。用前缀“摘要：”将这段文本概括成一句话。\n步骤二：将第一步的摘要翻译成英语，并加上前缀 \"Translation: \"。"},
    {"role": "user", "content": "\"\"\"在此处插入文本\"\"\""}
  ]
}
```

### Python: Streamed Tool Calls with Multiple Responses

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-api-to-complete-tool-calls

This Python snippet demonstrates how to use the Moonshot API for streamed chat completions with tool calls. It configures the request to expect multiple responses (n=2) and includes tool definitions for a search function. The code uses the `httpx` library to send the request and prepares a list to store the different response messages.

```python
import os
import json
import httpx  # 我们使用 httpx 库来执行我们的 HTTP 请求

tools = [
    {
        "type": "function",  # 约定的字段 type，目前支持 function 作为值
        "function": {  # 当 type 为 function 时，使用 function 字段定义具体的函数内容
            "name": "search",  # 函数的名称，请使用英文大小写字母、数据加上减号和下划线作为函数名称
            "description": " 
			通过搜索引擎搜索互联网上的内容。

			当你的知识无法回答用户提出的问题，或用户请求你进行联网搜索时，调用此工具。请从与用户的对话中提取用户想要搜索的内容作为 query 参数的值。
			搜索结果包含网站的标题、网站的地址（URL）以及网站简介。
		",  # 函数的介绍，在这里写上函数的具体作用以及使用场景，以便 Kimi 大模型能正确地选择使用哪些函数
            "parameters": {  # 使用 parameters 字段来定义函数接收的参数
                "type": "object",  # 固定使用 type: object 来使 Kimi 大模型生成一个 JSON Object 参数
                "required": ["query"],  # 使用 required 字段告诉 Kimi 大模型哪些参数是必填项
                "properties": {  # properties 中是具体的参数定义，你可以定义多个参数
                    "query": {  # 在这里，key 是参数名称，value 是参数的具体定义
                        "type": "string",  # 使用 type 定义参数类型
                        "description": "
						用户搜索的内容，请从用户的提问或聊天上下文中提取。
					"  # 使用 description 描述参数以便 Kimi 大模型更好地生成参数
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    },
]

header = {
    "Content-Type": "application/json",
    "Authorization": f"Bearer {os.environ.get('MOONSHOT_API_KEY')}",
}

data = {
    "model": "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
    "messages": [
        {"role": "user", "content": "请联网搜索 Context Caching 技术。"}
    ],
    "temperature": 0.6,
    "stream": True,
    "n": 2,  # <-- 注意这里，我们要求 Kimi 大模型输出 2 个回复
    "tools": tools,  # <-- 添加工具调用
}

# 使用 httpx 向 Kimi 大模型发出 chat 请求，并获得响应 r
r = httpx.post("https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/chat/completions",
               headers=header,
               json=data)
if r.status_code != 200:
    raise Exception(r.text)

data: str

# 在这里，我们预先构建一个 List，用于存放不同的回复消息，由于我们设置了 n=2，因此我们将 List 初始化为 2 个元素
messages = [{}, {}]

```

### Define Search and Crawl Tools for Kimi API (Node.js)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-api-to-complete-tool-calls

Defines two tools, 'search' for web searching and 'crawl' for fetching web content, using JSON Schema format for the Kimi API. These tools enable the model to interact with external services for real-time information retrieval. The 'search' tool requires a 'query' parameter, while the 'crawl' tool requires a 'url' parameter.

```javascript
const tools = [
	{
		"type": "function",
		"function": {
			"name": "search",
			"description": "通过搜索引擎搜索互联网上的内容。当你的知识无法回答用户提出的问题，或用户请求你进行联网搜索时，调用此工具。请从与用户的对话中提取用户想要搜索的内容作为 query 参数的值。搜索结果包含网站的标题、网站的地址（URL）以及网站简介。",
			"parameters": {
				"type": "object",
				"required": ["query"],
				"properties": {
					"query": {
						"type": "string",
						"description": "用户搜索的内容，请从用户的提问或聊天上下文中提取。"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	},
	{
		"type": "function",
		"function": {
			"name": "crawl",
			"description": "根据网站地址（URL）获取网页内容。",
			"parameters": {
				"type": "object",
				"required": ["url"],
				"properties": {
					"url": {
						"type": "string",
						"description": "需要获取内容的网站地址（URL），通常情况下从搜索结果中可以获取网站的地址。"
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
];
```

## Parameter Changes for k2.5 Series Models

For the k2.5 series models, certain parameters in the chat documentation behave differently. It is recommended not to manually set these fields and to use the default values.

| Field             | Required | Description                                       | Type   | Values

### Inspect Moonpalace Requests

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-moonpalace

These commands retrieve the same request information using different identifiers: Moonpalace ID, chat completion ID, or request ID. The default output includes metadata but not the request or response bodies.

```bash
$ moonpalace inspect --id 13
$ moonpalace inspect --chatcmpl chatcmpl-2e1aa823e2c94ebdad66450a0e6df088
$ moonpalace inspect --requestid c07c118e-4dae-11ef-b423-62db244b9277
```

### Kimi K2.5 Video Understanding API

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/kimi-k2-5-quickstart

This endpoint enables the Kimi K2.5 model to understand video content. Similar to image processing, the video is sent in a base64 encoded format within the request.

```APIDOC
## POST /v1/chat/completions

### Description
Processes a video and text prompt using the Kimi K2.5 model for multimodal understanding.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
/v1/chat/completions

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **model** (string) - Required - The model to use, e.g., "kimi-k2.5".
- **messages** (array) - Required - An array of message objects.
  - **role** (string) - Required - The role of the message author (e.g., "system", "user").
  - **content** (array) - Required - An array of content parts, which can include text and video_url.
    - **type** (string) - Required - The type of content part, either "text" or "video_url".
    - **video_url** (object) - Required if type is "video_url" - Contains the URL of the video.
      - **url** (string) - Required - The base64 encoded video data.
    - **text** (string) - Required if type is "text" - The text prompt.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "model": "kimi-k2.5",
  "messages": [
    {
      "role": "system",
      "content": "你是 Kimi。"
    },
    {
      "role": "user",
      "content": [
        {
          "type": "video_url",
          "video_url": {
            "url": "data:video/mp4;base64,AAAAPG1wNDF2aWRlbw=="
          }
        },
        {
          "type": "text",
          "text": "请描述视频的内容。"
        }
      ]
    }
  ]
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **content** (string) - The model's response describing the video.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "choices": [
    {
      "message": {
        "content": "这是一个简短的视频片段。"
      }
    }
  ]
}
```
```

--------------------------------

### Feature Description and Limitations

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-vision-model

Overview of Vision model capabilities and current limitations.

```APIDOC
## Feature Description and Limitations

### Supported Features:
- Multi-turn conversations
- Streaming output
- Tool calls
- JSON Mode
- Partial Mode

### Unsupported or Partially Supported Features:
- **URL-formatted images:** Not supported. Currently, only base64 encoded image content is supported.

### Other Limitations:
- **Image Quantity:** The Vision model does not have a limit on the number of images per request, but ensure the total request Body size does not exceed 100MB.
```

--------------------------------

### 通过分类指令处理复杂用户查询

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/prompt-best-practice

对于需要处理多种情况的复杂任务，可以通过对用户查询进行分类，并根据分类应用不同的指令集来提高输出的准确性。此示例展示了如何根据客户查询的类型提供技术支持。

```json
# 根据客户查询的分类，可以提供一组更具体的指示给模型，以便它处理后续步骤。例如，假设客户需要“故障排除”方面的帮助。
{
  "messages": [
    {"role": "system", "content": "你将收到需要技术支持的用户服务咨询。可以通过以下方式帮助用户：\n\n-请他们检查***是否配置完成。\n如果所有***都配置完成，但问题依然存在，请询问他们使用的设备型号\n-现在你需要告诉他们如何重启设备：\n=设备型号是A，请操作***。\n-如果设备型号是B，建议他们操作***。"}
  ]
}
```

--------------------------------

### Understanding `max_tokens` Parameter

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/faq

This section clarifies the function of the `max_tokens` parameter, explaining that it limits the maximum number of tokens the model can generate, rather than dictating a specific output length.

```APIDOC
## Understanding the `max_tokens` Parameter

### Description
The `max_tokens` parameter in the `/v1/chat/completions` endpoint specifies the maximum number of tokens the model is allowed to generate. Once the generated token count reaches this limit, the model will stop generating further tokens. It serves two primary purposes: aiding in model selection (e.g., ensuring `prompt_tokens + max_tokens` fits within a model's context window) and preventing excessive, unintended token generation that could incur additional costs.

**Important Note**: `max_tokens` does **not** instruct the model on how many tokens to output. It acts as a ceiling, not a target.

### Usage
1.  **Model Selection**: Helps determine which model to use based on the combined token count of the prompt and the desired maximum output.
2.  **Cost Control**: Prevents unexpected high costs by limiting the maximum number of generated tokens.

### Achieving Specific Output Lengths
If you need the model to output a specific number of tokens (e.g., words), consider these strategies:

**For outputs under 1000 tokens:**
1.  **Explicit Instruction**: Clearly state the desired word count in the prompt.
2.  **Iterative Refinement**: Check the output length and, if necessary, guide the model in a subsequent turn (e.g., "The output was too long" or "The output was too short").

**For outputs over 1000 tokens:**
1.  **Templating**: Break down the desired output into structured parts or chapters using templates with placeholders.
2.  **Sequential Filling**: Have the model fill each placeholder sequentially, then assemble the parts into the final long-form text.
```

--------------------------------

### Handle Kimi Chat Completions with Tool Calls (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-api-to-complete-tool-calls

This Python code snippet demonstrates how to process chat completions from the Kimi model when tool calls are involved. It iterates through tool calls, executes the corresponding functions using a `tool_map`, and appends the results back to the message history. The loop continues until the `finish_reason` is 'stop', ensuring all necessary tool interactions are completed.

```python
while finish_reason is None or finish_reason == "tool_calls":
    completion = client.chat.completions.create(
        model="kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
        messages=messages,
        temperature=0.6,
        tools=tools,  # <-- 我们通过 tools 参数，将定义好的 tools 提交给 Kimi 大模型
    )
    choice = completion.choices[0]
    finish_reason = choice.finish_reason
    if finish_reason == "tool_calls": # <-- 判断当前返回内容是否包含 tool_calls
        messages.append(choice.message) # <-- 我们将 Kimi 大模型返回给我们的 assistant 消息也添加到上下文中，以便于下次请求时 Kimi 大模型能理解我们的诉求
        for tool_call in choice.message.tool_calls: # <-- tool_calls 可能是多个，因此我们使用循环逐个执行
            tool_call_name = tool_call.function.name
            tool_call_arguments = json.loads(tool_call.function.arguments) # <-- arguments 是序列化后的 JSON Object，我们需要使用 json.loads 反序列化一下
            tool_function = tool_map[tool_call_name] # <-- 通过 tool_map 快速找到需要执行哪个函数
            tool_result = tool_function(tool_call_arguments)

            # 使用函数执行结果构造一个 role=tool 的 message，以此来向模型展示工具调用的结果；
            # 注意，我们需要在 message 中提供 tool_call_id 和 name 字段，以便 Kimi 大模型
            # 能正确匹配到对应的 tool_call。
            messages.append({
                "role": "tool",
                "tool_call_id": tool_call.id,
                "name": tool_call_name,
                "content": json.dumps(tool_result), # <-- 我们约定使用字符串格式向 Kimi 大模型提交工具调用结果，因此在这里使用 json.dumps 将执行结果序列化成字符串
            })

print(choice.message.content) # <-- 在这里，我们才将模型生成的回复返回给用户
```

--------------------------------

### Normalize Formula URI with Defaults (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-k2-to-setup-agent

This function ensures that a given formula URI has a default namespace and tag if they are missing. It prepends 'moonshot/' if no slash is present and ':latest' if no colon is present, standardizing the URI format for consistent processing.

```python
def normalize_formula_uri(uri: str) -> str:
    """Normalize formula URI with default namespace and tag"""
    if "/" not in uri:
        uri = f"moonshot/{uri}"
    if ":" not in uri:
        uri = f"{uri}:latest"
    return uri
```

```json
{
  "messages": [
    {"role": "system", "content": "你将收到一篇论文的摘要和论文的题目。论文的题目应该让读者对论文主题有清晰的概念，同时也应该引人注目。如果你收到的标题不符合这些标准，请提出5个可选的替代方案"},
    {"role": "user", "content": "摘要:在这里插入摘要。\n\n标题:在这里插入标题"}
  ]
}

### Define Search and Crawl Tools for Kimi API (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-api-to-complete-tool-calls

Defines two tools, 'search' for web searching and 'crawl' for fetching web content, using JSON Schema format for the Kimi API. These tools enable the model to interact with external services for real-time information retrieval. The 'search' tool requires a 'query' parameter, while the 'crawl' tool requires a 'url' parameter.

```python
tools = [
	{
		"type": "function", # 约定的字段 type，目前支持 function 作为值
		"function": { # 当 type 为 function 时，使用 function 字段定义具体的函数内容
			"name": "search", # 函数的名称，请使用英文大小写字母、数据加上减号和下划线作为函数名称
			"description": """ 
				通过搜索引擎搜索互联网上的内容。

				当你的知识无法回答用户提出的问题，或用户请求你进行联网搜索时，调用此工具。请从与用户的对话中提取用户想要搜索的内容作为 query 参数的值。
				搜索结果包含网站的标题、网站的地址（URL）以及网站简介。
			""", # 函数的介绍，在这里写上函数的具体作用以及使用场景，以便 Kimi 大模型能正确地选择使用哪些函数
			"parameters": { # 使用 parameters 字段来定义函数接收的参数
				"type": "object", # 固定使用 type: object 来使 Kimi 大模型生成一个 JSON Object 参数
				"required": ["query"], # 使用 required 字段告诉 Kimi 大模型哪些参数是必填项
				"properties": { # properties 中是具体的参数定义，你可以定义多个参数
					"query": { # 在这里，key 是参数名称，value 是参数的具体定义
						"type": "string", # 使用 type 定义参数类型
						"description": """ 
							用户搜索的内容，请从用户的提问或聊天上下文中提取。
						""" # 使用 description 描述参数以便 Kimi 大模型更好地生成参数
					}
				}
			}
		}
	},
	{
		"type": "function", # 约定的字段 type，目前支持 function 作为值
		"function": { # 当 type 为 function 时，使用 function 字段定义具体的函数内容
			"name": "crawl", # 函数的名称，请使用英文大小写字母、数据加上减号和下划线作为函数名称
			"description": """ 
				根据网站地址（URL）获取网页内容。
			""", # 函数的介绍，在这里写上函数的具体作用以及使用场景，以便 Kimi 大模型能正确地选择使用哪些函数
			"parameters": { # 使用 parameters 字段来定义函数接收的参数
				"type": "object", # 固定使用 type: object 来使 Kimi 大模型生成一个 JSON Object 参数
				"required": ["url"], # 使用 required 字段告诉 Kimi 大模型哪些参数是必填项
				"properties": { # properties 中是具体的参数定义，你可以定义多个参数
					"url": { # 在这里，key 是参数名称，value 是参数的具体定义
						"type": "string", # 使用 type 定义参数类型
						"description": """ 
							需要获取内容的网站地址（URL），通常情况下从搜索结果中可以获取网站的地址。
						""" # 使用 description 描述参数以便 Kimi 大模型更好地生成参数
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
]
```

### Upload File for Content Extraction (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/files

Uploads a file (e.g., PDF, DOC, image) to Moonshot AI for content extraction. The file is processed for its content, which can then be used as context for the Kimi model. Supports OCR for images and PDFs.

```Python
from pathlib import Path
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key = "$MOONSHOT_API_KEY",
    base_url = "https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

# xlnet.pdf is an example file, we support pdf, doc and image formats, for images and pdf files, OCR capabilities are provided
file_object = client.files.create(file=Path("xlnet.pdf"), purpose="file-extract")

# Get the result
# file_content = client.files.retrieve_content(file_id=file_object.id)
# Note that the previous retrieve_content api is marked with a warning in the latest version, you can use the following line instead
# If it is an old version, you can use retrieve_content
file_content = client.files.content(file_id=file_object.id).text

# Put it into the request
messages = [
    {
        "role": "system",
        "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。",
    },
    {
        "role": "system",
        "content": file_content,
    },
    {"role": "user", "content": "请简单介绍 xlnet.pdf 讲了啥"},
]

# Then call chat-completion to get Kimi's answer
completion = client.chat.completions.create(
  model="kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
  messages=messages,
  temperature=0.6,
)

print(completion.choices[0].message)

```

### Kimi Chat Completion with Tool Calls in Python

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/migrating-from-openai-to-kimi

This Python code demonstrates making a chat completion request to the Kimi model using the 'tools' parameter instead of the deprecated 'functions' parameter. It includes a system message and a user query, then enters a loop to handle responses until a final answer is generated. The loop processes 'tool_calls' if present, executing the relevant functions and appending their results back to the message history.

```python
messages = [
    {"role": "system",
     "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"},
    {"role": "user", "content": "请联网搜索 Context Caching，并告诉我它是什么。"}  # 在提问中要求 Kimi 大模型联网搜索
]

finish_reason = None

while finish_reason is None or finish_reason == "tool_calls":
    completion = client.chat.completions.create(
        model="kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
        messages=messages,
        temperature=0.6,
        tools=tools,  # <-- 我们通过 tools 参数，将定义好的 tools 提交给 Kimi 大模型
    )
    choice = completion.choices[0]
    finish_reason = choice.finish_reason

    if finish_reason == "tool_calls":  # <-- 判断当前返回内容是否包含 tool_calls
        messages.append(choice.message)  # <-- 我们将 Kimi 大模型返回给我们的 assistant 消息也添加到上下文中，以便于下次请求时 Kimi 大模型能理解我们的诉求
        for tool_call in choice.message.tool_calls:  # <-- tool_calls 可能是多个，因此我们使用循环逐个执行
            tool_call_name = tool_call.function.name
            tool_call_arguments = json.loads(tool_call.function.arguments)  # <-- arguments 是序列化后的 JSON Object，我们需要使用 json.loads 反序列化一下
            tool_function = tool_map[tool_call_name]  # <-- 通过 tool_map 快速找到需要执行哪个函数
            tool_result = tool_function(tool_call_arguments)

            # 使用函数执行结果构造一个 role=tool 的 message，以此来向模型展示工具调用的结果；
            # 注意，我们需要在 message 中提供 tool_call_id 和 name 字段，以便 Kimi 大模型
            # 能正确匹配到对应的 tool_call。
            messages.append({
                "role": "tool",
                "tool_call_id": tool_call.id,
                "name": tool_call_name,
                "content": json.dumps(tool_result),  # <-- 我们约定使用字符串格式向 Kimi 大模型提交工具调用结果，因此在这里使用 json.dumps 将执行结果序列化成字符串
            })

print(choice.message.content)  # <-- 在这里，我们才将模型生成的回复返回给用户

```

### 安装 Claude Code (MacOS/Linux)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/agent-support

此代码片段展示了在 MacOS 和 Linux 系统上安装 Node.js 和 Claude Code 的步骤。它使用 fnm 管理 Node.js 版本，并通过 npm 安装 Claude Code。最后，它初始化了 Claude Code 的配置文件。

```shell
# MacOS 和 Linux 上安装 nodejs
curl -fsSL https://fnm.vercel.app/install | bash

# 新开一个terminal，让 fnm 生效
fnm install 24.3.0
fnm default 24.3.0
fnm use 24.3.0

# 安装 claude-code
npm install -g @anthropic-ai/claude-code --registry=https://registry.npmmirror.com

# 初始化配置
node --eval "
    const homeDir = os.homedir(); 
    const filePath = path.join(homeDir, '.claude.json');
    if (fs.existsSync(filePath)) {
        const content = JSON.parse(fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf-8'));
        fs.writeFileSync(filePath,JSON.stringify({ ...content, hasCompletedOnboarding: true }, 2), 'utf-8');
    } else {
        fs.writeFileSync(filePath,JSON.stringify({ hasCompletedOnboarding: true }), null, 'utf-8');
    }"

```

### 计算 Token 数量 - 纯文本请求

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/estimate

使用 cURL 计算纯文本请求的 Token 数量。该接口需要提供模型 ID 和消息列表，消息列表包含系统消息和用户消息。请求的 Content-Type 必须是 application/json。

```bash
curl 'https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/tokenizers/estimate-token-count' \
  -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
  -H "Authorization: Bearer $MOONSHOT_API_KEY" \
  -d '{
    "model": "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
    "messages": [
        {
            "role": "system",
            "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"
        },
        {
            "role": "user",
            "content": "你好，我叫李雷，1+1等于多少？"
        }
    ]
}'
```

### List Files API

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/files

Retrieves a list of all files uploaded by the user.

```APIDOC
## GET /v1/files

### Description
Retrieves a list of all files uploaded by the user.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/files

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **data** (array) - A list of file objects.
  - Each object contains file information such as id, object, bytes, created_at, filename, and purpose.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "data": [
    {
      "id": "file-xxxxxxxxxxxx",
      "object": "file",
      "bytes": 12345,
      "created_at": 1678886400,
      "filename": "xlnet.pdf",
      "purpose": "file-extract"
    },
    {
      "id": "file-yyyyyyyyyyyy",
      "object": "file",
      "bytes": 67890,
      "created_at": 1678886500,
      "filename": "image.png",
      "purpose": "image"
    }
  ]
}
```

### Request Example
```python
file_list = client.files.list()

for file in file_list.data:
    print(file) # 查看每个文件的信息
```
```

### Force Streaming Output Mode in MoonPalace

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-moonpalace

The `--force-stream` option ensures all `/v1/chat/completions` requests are processed in streaming mode. This can help mitigate connection errors and timeouts caused by intermediate network devices by converting non-streaming requests to streaming ones. The response format is handled automatically based on the caller's `stream` parameter.

```bash
$ moonpalace start --port <PORT> --force-stream

```

### 计算 Token 数量 - 包含视觉的请求

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/estimate

使用 Python 计算包含视觉输入的请求的 Token 数量。该接口支持将图片编码为 base64 格式，并通过 `image_url` 类型传递。需要安装 `requests` 库。

```python
import os
import base64
import json
import requests

api_key = os.environ.get("MOONSHOT_API_KEY")
endpoint = "https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/tokenizers/estimate-token-count"
image_path = "image.png"

with open(image_path, "rb") as f:
    image_data = f.read()

# 我们使用标准库 base64.b64encode 函数将图片编码成 base64 格式的 image_url
image_url = f"data:image/{os.path.splitext(image_path)[1]};base64,{base64.b64encode(image_data).decode('utf-8')}"

payload = {
    "model": "kimi-k2.5",
    "messages": [
        {
            "role": "system",
            "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"
        },
        {
            "role": "user",
            "content": [
                {
                    "type": "image_url", # <-- 使用 image_url 类型来上传图片，内容为使用 base64 编码过的图片内容
                    "image_url": {
                        "url": image_url,
                    },
                },
                {
                    "type": "text",
                    "text": "请描述图片的内容。", # <-- 使用 text 类型来提供文字指令，例如“描述图片内容”
                },
            ],
        }
    ]
}

response = requests.post(
    endpoint,
    headers={
        "Authorization": f"Bearer {api_key}",
        "Content-Type": "application/json"
    },
    data=json.dumps(payload)
)

print(response.json())
```

### POST /chat/completions - Using Uploaded Images or Videos

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-vision-model

This endpoint allows you to send uploaded images or videos to the Vision API for analysis. Instead of using base64 encoded data, you can upload files and reference them by their file ID.

```APIDOC
## POST /chat/completions

### Description
This endpoint allows you to send uploaded images or videos to the Vision API for analysis. Instead of using base64 encoded data, you can upload files and reference them by their file ID.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
/chat/completions

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **model** (string) - Required - The model to use for the chat completion (e.g., "kimi-k2.5").
- **messages** (array) - Required - An array of message objects representing the conversation.
  - **role** (string) - Required - The role of the message sender ('system', 'user', 'assistant').
  - **content** (array) - Required - The content of the message, which can include text and media.
    - **type** (string) - Required - The type of content ('text', 'video_url', 'image_url').
    - **text** (string) - Required if type is 'text' - The text content.
    - **video_url** (object) - Required if type is 'video_url' - Object containing the video URL.
      - **url** (string) - Required - The URL of the video, formatted as `ms://<file-id>`.
    - **image_url** (object) - Required if type is 'image_url' - Object containing the image URL.
      - **url** (string) - Required - The URL of the image, can be a base64 encoded string or a file ID reference.

### Request Example
```python
import os
from pathlib import Path

from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key=os.environ.get("MOONSHOT_API_KEY"),
    base_url="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

# Upload a video file first
video_path = "path/to/your/video.mp4"
file_object = client.files.create(file=Path(video_path), purpose="video")

completion = client.chat.completions.create(
    model="kimi-k2.5",
    messages=[
        {
            "role": "system",
            "content": "You are Kimi, an AI assistant from Moonshot AI."
        },
        {
            "role": "user",
            "content":
            [
                {
                    "type": "video_url",
                    "video_url":
                    {
                        "url": f"ms://{file_object.id}" 
                    }
                },
                {
                    "type": "text",
                    "text": "Please describe this video."
                }
            ]
        }
    ]
)

print(completion.choices[0].message.content)
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **choices** (array) - An array of message choices.
  - **message** (object) - The message content.
    - **content** (string) - The generated response from the model.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "id": "chatcmpl-xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx",
  "object": "chat.completion",
  "created": 1677652288,
  "model": "kimi-k2.5",
  "choices": [
    {
      "index": 0,
      "message": {
        "role": "assistant",
        "content": "This is a description of the video."
      },
      "finish_reason": "stop"
    }
  ],
  "usage": {
    "prompt_tokens": 100,
    "completion_tokens": 50,
    "total_tokens": 150
  }
}
```
```

This endpoint retrieves a list of all available models that can be used with the API.

```APIDOC
## GET /v1/models

### Description
Retrieves a list of all available models that can be used with the API.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/v1/models

### Parameters
None

### Request Example
```
GET https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/models
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **data** (array) - A list of model objects.
  - **id** (string) - The ID of the model.
  - **object** (string) - The object type (e.g., 'model').
  - **created** (integer) - The creation timestamp of the model.
  - **owned_by** (string) - The entity that owns the model.

      "owned_by": "company"
    }
  ]

### Chat Completion API

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/chat

The Chat Completion API allows you to interact with the Kimi models for conversational AI tasks. It supports both single-turn and multi-turn conversations.

```APIDOC
## POST /v1/chat/completions

### Description
Initiates a chat completion request with the specified model and messages.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/chat/completions

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **model** (string) - Required - The ID of the model to use for completion (e.g., "kimi-k2-turbo-preview").
- **messages** (array) - Required - A list of message objects representing the conversation history. Each object should have a `role` (system, user, or assistant) and `content` (string).
- **temperature** (number) - Optional - Controls the randomness of the output. Lower values make the output more deterministic.

### Request Example
```json
{
    "model": "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
    "messages": [
        {
            "role": "system",
            "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"
        },
        { "role": "user", "content": "你好，我叫李雷，1+1等于多少？" }
    ],
    "temperature": 0.6
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **id** (string) - The ID of the completion.
- **object** (string) - The type of object returned, usually "chat.completion".
- **created** (integer) - Unix timestamp of when the completion was created.
- **model** (string) - The model used for the completion.
- **choices** (array) - A list of completion choices. Each choice contains:
    - **index** (integer) - The index of the choice.
    - **message** (object) - The message object containing the assistant's reply (`role`: "assistant", `content`: string).
    - **finish_reason** (string) - The reason the model stopped generating tokens (e.g., "stop").
- **usage** (object) - Information about token usage:
    - **prompt_tokens** (integer) - Number of tokens in the prompt.
    - **completion_tokens** (integer) - Number of tokens in the completion.
    - **total_tokens** (integer) - Total tokens used in the request.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "id": "chatcmpl-xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx",
  "object": "chat.completion",
  "created": 1677652288,
  "model": "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
  "choices": [
    {
      "index": 0,
      "message": {
        "role": "assistant",
        "content": "1+1等于2。"
      },
      "finish_reason": "stop"
    }
  ],
  "usage": {
    "prompt_tokens": 50,
    "completion_tokens": 10,
    "total_tokens": 60
  }
}
```
```

### 提供输出示例以指导模型风格 (Few-Shot Prompting)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/prompt-best-practice

通过在Prompt中提供示例，可以指导模型以特定的风格或格式进行输出，尤其适用于难以用语言精确描述的场景。这被称为“few-shot”提示。

```json
{
  "messages": [
    {"role": "system", "content": "以一致的风格回答"},
    {"role": "user", "content": "在此处插入文本"}
  ]
}
```

### JSON Output of Formula Tools

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-official-tools

This JSON structure represents the output when fetching tools for a formula. It includes a list of tools, each with a type (e.g., 'function'), and detailed information about the function, including its name, description, parameters, and required arguments.

```json
{
  "object": "list",
  "tools": [
    {
      "type": "function",
      "function": {
        "name": "web_search",
        "description": "Search the web for information",
        "parameters": {
          "type": "object",
          "properties": {
            "query": {
              "description": "What to search for",
              "type": "string"
            }
          },
          "required": [ "query" ]
        }
      }
    }
  ]
}
```

### Handle Kimi API Errors Without SDK (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/faq

Demonstrates how to handle errors when directly interacting with the Kimi API without using the OpenAI SDK. It checks the HTTP status code of the response and parses the JSON error message if the request fails (non-200 status code). Requires MOONSHOT_API_KEY environment variable.

```python
import os
import httpx

header = {
    "Authorization": f"Bearer {os.environ['MOONSHOT_API_KEY']}",
}

messages = [
    {"role": "system", "content": "你是 Kimi"},
    {"role": "user", "content": "你好。"},
]

r = httpx.post("https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/chat/completions",
               headers=header,
               json={
                   "model": "moonshot-v1-128k",  # <-- 如果你使用一个正确的模型，下方会进入 if status_code==200 分支
                   # "model": "moonshot-v1-129k",  # <-- 如果你使用一个错误的模型名称，下方会进入 else 分支
                   "messages": messages,
                   "temperature": 0.3,
               })

if r.status_code == 200:  # 当使用正确的模型进行请求时，会进入此分支，进行正常的处理逻辑
    completion = r.json()
    print(completion["choices"][0]["message"]["content"])
else:  # 当使用错误的模型名称进行请求时，会进入此分支，在这里进行错误处理
    # 在这里，为了演示，我们仅将错误打印出来。
    # 在实际的代码逻辑中，你可能需要更多的处理逻辑，例如记录日志、中断请求或进行重试等。
    error = r.json()
    print(f"error: status={r.status_code}, type='{error['error']['type']}', message='{error['error']['message']}'")

```

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/balance

This snippet demonstrates how to query your Moonshot API account balance using a cURL command. It requires your API key for authentication and returns your available, voucher, and cash balances.

curl https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/users/me/balance -H "Authorization: Bearer $MOONSHOT_API_KEY"

### 使用 Python 调用 Kimi Tool Use API

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/tool-use

演示了如何使用 Python 的 `openai` 库与 Kimi 大模型的 API 进行交互，以实现 Tool Use 功能。代码展示了 API 密钥和基础 URL 的配置，以及构建包含系统消息、用户消息和工具定义的请求。

```python
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key = "$MOONSHOT_API_KEY",
    base_url = "https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

completion = client.chat.completions.create(
    model = "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
    messages = [
        {"role": "system", "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"},
        {"role": "user", "content": "编程判断 3214567 是否是素数。"}
    ],
    tools = [{
        "type": "function",
        "function": {
            "name": "CodeRunner",
            "description": "代码执行器，支持运行 python 和 javascript 代码",
            "parameters": {
                "properties": {
                    "language": {
                        "type": "string",
                        "enum": ["python", "javascript"]
                    },
                    "code": {
                        "type": "string",
                        "description": "代码写在这里"
                    }
                },
            "type": "object"
            }
        }
    }],
    temperature = 0.6,
)

print(completion.choices[0].message)
```

### 配置 Kimi K2 Thinking Turbo 模型 (Windows)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/agent-support

此代码片段展示了如何在 Windows PowerShell 中配置环境变量以使用 `kimi-k2-thinking-turbo` 模型。它设置了 API 地址、认证令牌、模型名称等，并启动 Claude。

```powershell
# Windows Powershell 启动高速版 kimi-k2-thinking-turbo 模型
$env:ANTHROPIC_BASE_URL="https://api.moonshot.cn/anthropic";
$env:ANTHROPIC_AUTH_TOKEN="YOUR_MOONSHOT_API_KEY"
$env:ANTHROPIC_MODEL="kimi-k2-thinking-turbo"
$env:ANTHROPIC_DEFAULT_OPUS_MODEL="kimi-k2-thinking-turbo"
$env:ANTHROPIC_DEFAULT_SONNET_MODEL="kimi-k2-thinking-turbo"
$env:ANTHROPIC_DEFAULT_HAIKU_MODEL="kimi-k2-thinking-turbo"
$env:CLAUDE_CODE_SUBAGENT_MODEL="kimi-k2-thinking-turbo"
claude

```

### 迁移 function_call 到 tool_calls (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/migrating-from-openai-to-kimi

示例展示了如何将 OpenAI 中已废弃的 function_call 参数迁移到 Kimi API 支持的 tool_calls。代码定义了一个 search 工具，并提供了相应的实现。

```python
from typing import *

import json
import httpx
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key="MOONSHOT_API_KEY",  # 在这里将 MOONSHOT_API_KEY 替换为你从 Kimi 开放平台申请的 API Key
    base_url="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

functions = [
    {
        "name": "search",  # 函数的名称，请使用英文大小写字母、数据加上减号和下划线作为函数名称
        "description": """ 
            通过搜索引擎搜索互联网上的内容。

            当你的知识无法回答用户提出的问题，或用户请求你进行联网搜索时，调用此工具。请从与用户的对话中提取用户想要搜索的内容作为 query 参数的值。
            搜索结果包含网站的标题、网站的地址（URL）以及网站简介。
        """,  # 函数的介绍，在这里写上函数的具体作用以及使用场景，以便 Kimi 大模型能正确地选择使用哪些函数
        "parameters": {  # 使用 parameters 字段来定义函数接收的参数
            "type": "object",  # 固定使用 type: object 来使 Kimi 大模型生成一个 JSON Object 参数
            "required": ["query"],  # 使用 required 字段告诉 Kimi 大模型哪些参数是必填项
            "properties": {  # properties 中是具体的参数定义，你可以定义多个参数
                "query": {
                    "type": "string",  # 使用 type 定义参数类型
                    "description": """ 
                        用户搜索的内容，请从用户的提问或聊天上下文中提取。
                    """  # 使用 description 描述参数以便 Kimi 大模型更好地生成参数
                }
            }
        }
    }
]


def search_impl(query: str) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
    """
    search_impl 使用搜索引擎对 query 进行搜索，目前主流的搜索引擎（例如 Bing）都提供了 API 调用方式，你可以自行选择
    你喜欢的搜索引擎 API 进行调用，并将返回结果中的网站标题、网站链接、网站简介信息放置在一个 dict 中返回。

    这里只是一个简单的示例，你可能需要编写一些鉴权、校验、解析的代码。
    """
    r = httpx.get("https://your.search.api", params={"query": query})
    return r.json()


def search(arguments: Dict[str, Any]) -> Any:
    query = arguments["query"]
    result = search_impl(query)
    return {"result": result}


function_map = {
    "search": search,
}

# ==========================================================================================================================================================
# tools 是 functions 的超集，因此我们可以通过已经定义的 functions 构造 tools，我们循环遍历每一个 function，并为其构造相应的 tool 格式；
# 同时，我们也生成相应的 tool_map。

```

### Send Image and Text to Kimi Vision Model API (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-vision-model

This Python code demonstrates how to send a multimodal request to the Kimi Vision model. It constructs a `messages` list where the `content` field is a list of dictionaries, allowing for both `image_url` and `text` types. This is the correct format for providing image and text inputs to the model.

```python
client.chat.completions.create(
    model="kimi-k2.5",
    messages=[
        {"role": "system", "content": "你是 Kimi。"},
        {
            "role": "user",
            "content": [
                {
                    "type": "image_url",
                    "image_url": {
                        "url": image_url, # Assumes image_url is already base64 encoded
                    },
                },
                {
                    "type": "text",
                    "text": "请描述图片的内容。",
                },
            ],
        },
    ],
)

print(completion.choices[0].message.content)
```

### Upload Image using Base64 with Kimi Vision API (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-vision-model

This Python code snippet demonstrates how to upload an image file to the Kimi Vision API using base64 encoding. It reads an image file, encodes its binary data into a base64 string, and prepares it for API submission. This requires the 'openai' library and an API key.

```python
import os
import base64

from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key=os.environ.get("MOONSHOT_API_KEY"),
    base_url="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

# 在这里，你需要将 kimi.png 文件替换为你想让 Kimi 识别的图片的地址
image_path = "kimi.png"

with open(image_path, "rb") as f:
    image_data = f.read()

```

### 声明 Kimi 内置 $web_search 工具

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-web-search

声明 Kimi 内置的 `$web_search` 工具，用于在 `tools` 参数中注册联网搜索功能。此声明仅需指定 `type` 为 `builtin_function` 和 `function.name` 为 `$web_search`。

```json
tools = [
	{
		"type": "builtin_function",  # <-- 我们使用 builtin_function 来表示 Kimi 内置工具，也用于区分普通 function
		"function": {
			"name": "$web_search",
		},
	},
]
```

### 使用 Kimi API 获取当前日期

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/faq

演示如何通过在系统提示词中注入当前日期，使 Kimi API 能够回答关于当前日期的问题。此方法适用于需要 API 提供时效性信息的场景。

```python
import os
from datetime import datetime
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key=os.environ['MOONSHOT_API_KEY'],
    base_url="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

# 我们通过 datetime 库生成了当前日期，并将其添加到系统提示词 system prompt 中
system_prompt = f"""
你是 Kimi，今天的日期是 {datetime.now().strftime('%d.%m.%Y %H:%M:%S')}
"""

completion = client.chat.completions.create(
    model="moonshot-v1-128k",
    messages=[
        {"role": "system", "content": system_prompt},
        {"role": "user", "content": "今天的日期？"},
    ],
    temperature=0.3,
)

print(completion.choices[0].message.content)  # 输出：今天的日期是 2024 年 7 月 31 日。

```

### File Management API

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/migrating-from-openai-to-kimi

Endpoints for uploading, retrieving, and managing files, compatible with OpenAI's file API.

```APIDOC
## File Management API

### Description
This section covers the API endpoints for managing files, including uploading files, retrieving file details, and downloading file content. These endpoints are compatible with OpenAI's file API.

### Endpoints

#### POST /v1/files

##### Description
Upload a file that can be used with other endpoints, such as for fine-tuning or providing context to models.

##### Method
`POST`

##### Endpoint
`/v1/files`

##### Parameters
*   **purpose** (string) - Required - The intended purpose of the file (e.g., `fine-tune`, `assistants`).
*   **file** (file) - Required - The file to upload.

##### Request Example
(Multipart form data upload)

##### Response
*   **id** (string) - Unique identifier for the file.
*   **object** (string) - Object type, e.g., `file`.
*   **bytes** (integer) - File size in bytes.
*   **created_at** (integer) - Unix timestamp of creation.
*   **filename** (string) - The name of the file.
*   **purpose** (string) - The purpose of the file.

#### GET /v1/files

##### Description
Returns a list of files that belong to the authenticated user.

##### Method
`GET`

##### Endpoint
`/v1/files`

##### Parameters
*   **purpose** (string) - Optional - Filter files by purpose.

##### Response
*   **data** (array) - A list of file objects.
*   **object** (string) - Object type, e.g., `list`.

#### GET /v1/files/{file_id}

##### Description
Returns information about a specific file.

##### Method
`GET`

##### Endpoint
`/v1/files/{file_id}`

##### Parameters
*   **file_id** (string) - Required - The ID of the file to retrieve.

##### Response
*   **id** (string) - Unique identifier for the file.
*   **object** (string) - Object type, e.g., `file`.
*   **bytes** (integer) - File size in bytes.
*   **created_at** (integer) - Unix timestamp of creation.
*   **filename** (string) - The name of the file.
*   **purpose** (string) - The purpose of the file.

#### DELETE /v1/files/{file_id}

##### Description
Deletes a specific file.

##### Method
`DELETE`

##### Endpoint
`/v1/files/{file_id}`

##### Parameters
*   **file_id** (string) - Required - The ID of the file to delete.

##### Response
*   **id** (string) - Unique identifier for the deleted file.
*   **object** (string) - Object type, e.g., `file.deleted`.
*   **deleted** (boolean) - True if the file was deleted successfully.

#### GET /v1/files/{file_id}/content

##### Description
Returns the contents of a specific file.

##### Method
`GET`

##### Endpoint
`/v1/files/{file_id}/content`

##### Parameters
*   **file_id** (string) - Required - The ID of the file whose content to retrieve.

##### Response
*   The raw content of the file (e.g., text, JSON).
```

### POST /v1/chat/completions

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/migrating-from-openai-to-kimi

Generates chat completions based on the provided messages. This endpoint is compatible with OpenAI's chat completions API.

```APIDOC
## POST /v1/chat/completions

### Description
This endpoint allows you to interact with Kimi's chat models to generate responses based on a conversation history. It mirrors the functionality of OpenAI's chat completions API.

### Method
`POST`

### Endpoint
`/v1/chat/completions`

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
*   **stream** (boolean) - Optional - If set to `true`, streams response deltas rather than returning a single JSON object.

#### Request Body
*   **model** (string) - Required - The model to use for generating completions (e.g., `kimi-turbo`, `kimi-moonicorn-turbo`).
*   **messages** (array) - Required - A list of message objects, each with a `role` (`system`, `user`, or `assistant`) and `content`.
*   **temperature** (number) - Optional - Controls randomness. Lower values make output more focused and deterministic. Range: `[0, 1]`. Default: `0.7`.
*   **n** (integer) - Optional - How many chat completion choices to generate for each input message. If `temperature` is 0, `n` must be 1. Default: `1`.
*   **max_tokens** (integer) - Optional - The maximum number of tokens to generate in the completion.
*   **stop** (string or array) - Optional - Up to 4 sequences where the API will stop generating further tokens.
*   **stream_options** (object) - Optional - Options for streaming responses.
    *   **include_usage** (boolean) - Optional - If true, includes usage information in the stream.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "model": "kimi-turbo",
  "messages": [
    {"role": "system", "content": "You are a helpful assistant."},
    {"role": "user", "content": "What is the weather like today?"}
  ],
  "temperature": 0.3,
  "n": 1,
  "stream_options": {
    "include_usage": true
  }
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
*   **id** (string) - Unique identifier for the completion.
*   **object** (string) - Type of object, e.g., `chat.completion` or `chat.completion.chunk`.
*   **created** (integer) - Unix timestamp of creation.
*   **model** (string) - The model used.
*   **choices** (array) - A list of completion choices.
    *   **index** (integer) - Index of the choice.
    *   **message** (object) - The generated message.
        *   **role** (string) - Role of the message sender (`assistant`).
        *   **content** (string) - The content of the message.
    *   **finish_reason** (string) - The reason the model stopped generating tokens (e.g., `stop`, `length`).
    *   **usage** (object) - Token usage information (if `stream_options.include_usage` is true or for non-streaming responses).
        *   **prompt_tokens** (integer) - Number of tokens in the prompt.
        *   **completion_tokens** (integer) - Number of tokens in the completion.
        *   **total_tokens** (integer) - Total tokens used.

#### Response Example (Non-streaming)
```json
{
  "id": "chatcmpl-xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx",
  "object": "chat.completion",
  "created": 1700000000,
  "model": "kimi-turbo",
  "choices": [
    {
      "index": 0,
      "message": {
        "role": "assistant",
        "content": "The weather today is sunny with a high of 75 degrees Fahrenheit."
      },
      "finish_reason": "stop",
      "usage": {
        "prompt_tokens": 20,
        "completion_tokens": 15,
        "total_tokens": 35
      }
    }
  ]
}
```

#### Response Example (Streaming Chunk)
```json
{
  "id": "chatcmpl-xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx",
  "object": "chat.completion.chunk",
  "created": 1700000000,
  "model": "kimi-turbo",
  "choices": [
    {
      "index": 0,
      "delta": {
        "role": "assistant",
        "content": "The weather"
      },
      "finish_reason": null
    }
  ],
  "usage": {
    "prompt_tokens": 20,
    "completion_tokens": 5,
    "total_tokens": 25
  }
}
```
```

### Python: Managing Context Length for Kimi API Conversations

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/engage-in-multi-turn-conversations-using-kimi-api

This Python snippet demonstrates how to manage the context length for Kimi API conversations to prevent exceeding token limits. It separates system messages and uses a 'make_messages' function to append the user's input and then truncate the historical messages to a specified number (defaulting to 20). This ensures that each API request includes essential system instructions and a limited history, optimizing token usage.

```python
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key = "MOONSHOT_API_KEY", # 在这里将 MOONSHOT_API_KEY 替换为你从 Kimi 开放平台申请的 API Key
    base_url = "https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

# 我们将 System Messages 单独放置在一个列表中，这是因为每次请求都应该携带 System Messages
system_messages = [
	{"role": "system", "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"},
]

# 我们定义一个全局变量 messages，用于记录我们和 Kimi 大模型产生的历史对话消息
# 在 messages 中，既包含我们向 Kimi 大模型提出的问题（role=user），也包括 Kimi 大模型给我们的回复（role=assistant）
# messages 中的消息按时间顺序从小到大排列
messages = []


def make_messages(input: str, n: int = 20) -> list[dict]:
	"""
	使用 make_messaegs 控制每次请求的消息数量，使其保持在一个合理的范围内，例如默认值是 20。在构建消息列表
	的过程中，我们会先添加 System Prompt，这是因为无论如何对消息进行截断，System Prompt 都是必不可少
	的内容，再获取 messages —— 即历史记录中，最新的 n 条消息作为请求使用的消息，在大部分场景中，这样
	能保证请求的消息所占用的 Tokens 数量不超过模型上下文窗口。
	"""
	# 首先，我们将用户最新的问题构造成一个 message（role=user），并添加到 messages 的尾部
	messages.append({
		"role": "user",
		"content": input,	
	})

	# new_messages 是我们下一次请求使用的消息列表，现在让我们来构建它
	new_messages = []

	# 每次请求都需要携带 System Messages，因此我们需要先把 system_messages 添加到消息列表中；
	# 注意，即使对消息进行截断，也应该注意保证 System Messages 仍然在 messages 列表中。
	new_messages.extend(system_messages)

	# 在这里，当历史消息超过 n 条时，我们仅保留最新的 n 条消息
	if len(messages) > n:
		messages = messages[-n:]

	new_messages.extend(messages)
	return new_messages


def chat(input: str) -> str:
	"""
	chat 函数支持多轮对话，每次调用 chat 函数与 Kimi 大模型对话时，Kimi 大模型都会”看到“此前已经
	产生的历史对话消息，换句话说，Kimi 大模型拥有了记忆。
	"""

	# 携带 messages 与 Kimi 大模型对话
	completion = client.chat.completions.create(
        model="kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
        messages=make_messages(input),
        temperature=0.6,
    )

	# 通过 API 我们获得了 Kimi 大模型给予我们的回复消息（role=assistant）
    assistant_message = completion.choices[0].message

    # 为了让 Kimi 大模型拥有完整的记忆，我们必须将 Kimi 大模型返回给我们的消息也添加到 messages 中
    messages.append(assistant_message)

    return assistant_message.content

print(chat("你好，我今年 27 岁。"))
print(chat("你知道我今年几岁吗？")) # 在这里，Kimi 大模型根据此前的上下文信息，将会知道你今年的年龄是 27 岁

```

--------------------------------

### Encode Image to Base64 URL in Python

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-vision-model

This snippet uses Python's standard `base64` library to encode image data into a base64 string. It then formats this string into a `data:` URI, suitable for embedding images directly into web content or API requests. This is useful for preparing image inputs for multimodal AI models.

```python
import base64
import os

# Assuming image_path and image_data are defined elsewhere
# image_path = "path/to/your/image.png"
# with open(image_path, "rb") as image_file:
#     image_data = image_file.read()

image_url = f"data:image/{os.path.splitext(image_path)[1]};base64,{base64.b64encode(image_data).decode('utf-8')}"
```

### Error Handling

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/faq

This section explains how to handle errors when interacting with the Kimi API directly, without using an SDK. It covers interpreting HTTP status codes and understanding the JSON error response format.

```APIDOC
## Error Handling

### Description
When interacting with the Kimi API directly (without an SDK), it's crucial to handle potential errors by inspecting the HTTP status codes and the JSON error response. Successful requests typically return a 200 status code, while errors are indicated by 4xx or 5xx status codes.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
`/v1/chat/completions`

### Parameters
#### Path Parameters
None

#### Query Parameters
None

#### Request Body
- **model** (string) - Required - The model to use. An incorrect model name will result in an error.
- **messages** (array) - Required - The conversation history.
- **temperature** (number) - Optional - Controls randomness.

### Request Example (Python)
```python
import os
import httpx

header = {
    "Authorization": f"Bearer {os.environ['MOONSHOT_API_KEY']}",
}

messages = [
    {"role": "system", "content": "你是 Kimi"},
    {"role": "user", "content": "你好。"},
]

r = httpx.post("https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/chat/completions",
               headers=header,
               json={
                   "model": "moonshot-v1-128k",  # <-- Correct model
                   # "model": "moonshot-v1-129k",  # <-- Incorrect model
                   "messages": messages,
                   "temperature": 0.3,
               })

if r.status_code == 200:
    completion = r.json()
    print(completion["choices"][0]["message"]["content"])
else:
    error = r.json()
    print(f"error: status={r.status_code}, type='{error['error']['type']}', message='{error['error']['message']}'")
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **choices** (array) - An array of completion choices.
  - **message** (object)
    - **content** (string) - The generated text.

#### Error Response (4xx or 5xx)
- **error** (object)
  - **type** (string) - The type of error.
  - **message** (string) - A detailed error message.

#### Response Example (Error)
```json
{
	"error": {
		"type": "invalid_request_error",
		"message": "The model `moonshot-v1-129k` does not exist."
	}
}
```
```

### Chat Completions API

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/chat

This endpoint allows you to generate text completions for a given prompt using various models. It supports streaming responses for real-time updates.

```APIDOC
## POST /v1/chat/completions

### Description
Generates text completions for a given prompt using a specified model. Supports streaming responses.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
/v1/chat/completions

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **model** (string) - Required - The ID of the model to use for generation.
- **messages** (array) - Required - A list of messages comprising the conversation.
  - **role** (string) - Required - The role of the author of the message (e.g., system, user, assistant).
  - **content** (string) - Required - The content of the message.
- **temperature** (number) - Optional - Controls randomness. Lower values make output more focused and deterministic.
- **stream** (boolean) - Optional - Whether to stream back partial message deltas as they are generated.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "model": "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
  "messages": [
    {
      "role": "system",
      "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"
    },
    {
      "role": "user",
      "content": "你好，我叫李雷，1+1等于多少？"
    }
  ],
  "temperature": 0.6,
  "stream": true
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **choices** (array) - A list of generated message choices.
  - **delta** (object) - The message content delta.
    - **content** (string) - The content of the message.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "choices": [
    {
      "delta": {
        "content": "2"
      }
    }
  ]
}
```
```

### LaTeX Report Template with Custom Styles and Commands

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-k2-to-setup-agent

A comprehensive LaTeX template designed for professional industry research reports. It includes custom styles for sections, subsections, figures, and tables, along with definitions for colors and page headers/footers. This template is configured for XeLaTeX compilation and supports Chinese language documents using the ctexart class.

```latex
% !TeX program = XeLaTeX
% 专业行业研究报告模板 - 完整框架精简版

\usepackage{fancyhdr,lastpage}

\usepackage{xcolor,colortbl}
\usepackage{enumitem}
\usepackage{setspace}
\usepackage{tikz}

%================== 颜色定义 ==================
