\definecolor{textblack}{HTML}{000000}  % 正文黑色
\definecolor{textgray}{HTML}{333333}  % 辅助文字深灰色
\definecolor{lightgray}{HTML}{666666} % 数据来源灰色
\definecolor{linegray}{HTML}{E5E5E5}   % 线条灰色

%================== 基础设置 ==================
\setlength{\headheight}{15pt}
\linespread{1.3}

%================== 页眉页脚 ==================

  \color{textblack}\hrule height 0.5pt width \headwidth
}}

%================== 标题样式 ==================

  \sffamily\bfseries\Large\color{primary}
  }{\thesection}{1em}{}[{
  \vspace{-0.3em}\color{primary}\rule{\textwidth}{0.5pt}
}]

\titleformat{\subsection}[block]{
  \sffamily\bfseries\large\color{textblack}
  }{\thesubsection}{1em}{}

\titleformat{\subsubsection}[block]{
  \sffamily\bfseries\normalsize\color{textblack}
  }{\thesubsubsection}{1em}{}

%================== 图表样式 ==================
\usepackage{caption}
\captionsetup{
  font={sf,small},
  labelfont={bf,color=textblack},
  textfont={color=textgray},
  labelsep=period,
  skip=6pt
}

%================== 自定义命令 ==================

\newcommand{\keydata}[1]{\textbf{#1}}
\newcommand{\insertfigure}[3]{
\begin{figure}[H]
\centering
\includegraphics[width=#2]{#1}
\caption{#3}
\datasource{示例数据源}{图片说明}
\end{figure}
}

%================== 文档开始 ==================
\begin{document}

%================== 封面页 ==================
\thispagestyle{empty}
\begin{center}
  \vspace*{5cm}
  
  % 主标题
  {\sffamily\bfseries\fontsize{36}{40}\selectfont 2025中国新能源汽车行业}
  
  \vspace{0.8cm}
  
  % 副标题
  {\sffamily\bfseries\fontsize{28}{32}\selectfont 深度研究报告}

  \vspace{3cm}
  
  % 研究机构
  {\sffamily\fontsize{20}{24}\selectfont Kimi K2}
  
  \vspace{1cm}
  
  {\sffamily\Large \today}
  
  \vfill
  
  \vspace{0.5cm}
  
  % 底部信息
  {\sffamily\small\color{textgray} 本报告基于公开信息分析生成，仅供参考}
  
\end{center}

\newpage

%================== 执行摘要 ==================
\section*{执行摘要}
\addcontentsline{toc}{section}{执行摘要}
\markboth{执行摘要}{执行摘要}

中国新能源汽车产业在2024年继续保持强劲发展势头，市场渗透率突破42\%, 技术创新加速推进，产业链日趋完善，出海步伐显著加快，投资价值日益凸显。

\textbf{核心发现：}
\begin{itemize}
  \item 2024年中国新能源汽车销量达到\keydata{1,156万辆}，同比增长\keydata{28.5\%}，市场渗透率突破\keydata{42\%}。

  \item 2024年新能源汽车出口量达到\keydata{173万辆}，同比增长\keydata{55\%}。
\end{itemize}

### Disable Thinking for Kimi K2.5 using cURL

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/kimi-k2-5-quickstart

Demonstrates how to disable the thinking capability for the Kimi K2.5 model by sending a cURL request with the `"thinking": {"type": "disabled"}` parameter in the JSON body. This ensures the model does not engage its thinking process for the given request.

```bash
$ curl https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/chat/completions \
    -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
    -H "Authorization: Bearer $MOONSHOT_API_KEY" \
    -d '{
        "model": "kimi-k2.5",
        "messages": [
            {"role": "user", "content": "你好"}
        ],
        "thinking": {"type": "disabled"}
   }'
```

### Modify Chat Function forkimi-k2-turbo-preview Model (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-web-search

This code snippet demonstrates how to modify the `chat` function to specifically use the `kimi-k2-turbo-preview` model. This is recommended when enabling web search functionality due to potential increases in token usage, helping to avoid 'Input token length too long' errors. It highlights the `tools` declaration using `builtin_function` for the `$web_search`.

```python
def chat(messages) -> Choice:
    completion = client.chat.completions.create(
        model="kimi-k2-turbo-preview",  
        messages=messages,
        temperature=0.6,
        tools=[
            {
                "type": "builtin_function",  # <-- Use builtin_function to declare the $web_search function, please include the complete tools declaration in every request
                "function": {
                    "name": "$web_search",
                },
            }
        ]
    )
    return completion.choices[0]
```

### Retrieve File Information API

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/files

Retrieves basic information about a specific file.

```APIDOC
## GET /v1/files/{file_id}

### Description
Retrieves basic information about a specific file.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/files/{file_id}

### Parameters
#### Path Parameters
- **file_id** (string) - Required - The unique identifier of the file to retrieve.

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **id** (string) - The unique identifier for the file.
- **object** (string) - The type of object, typically "file".
- **bytes** (integer) - The size of the file in bytes.
- **created_at** (integer) - The Unix timestamp of when the file was created.
- **filename** (string) - The name of the file.
- **purpose** (string) - The purpose for which the file was uploaded.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "id": "file-xxxxxxxxxxxx",
  "object": "file",
  "bytes": 12345,
  "created_at": 1678886400,
  "filename": "xlnet.pdf",
  "purpose": "file-extract"
}
```

### Request Example
```python
file_id_to_retrieve = "file-xxxxxxxxxxxx"
file_info = client.files.retrieve(file_id=file_id_to_retrieve)
print(file_info)
```
```

### Retrieve Company Information using AKShare API

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-k2-to-setup-agent

Fetches company stock information from the AKShare API based on a provided company name. It handles cases where the company is not found and returns a JSON string of the top 5 matching companies with their details. Dependencies include the 'akshare' and 'json' libraries.

```python
import akshare as ak
import json

def get_company_info(company_name: str) -> str:
    """调用 AKShare API 获取公司信息"""
    try:
        stock_info_df = ak.stock_info_a_code_name()
        matches = stock_info_df[stock_info_df['name'].str.contains(company_name, na=False)]
        if matches.empty:
            return f"未找到公司 '{company_name}' 的相关信息。请检查公司名称是否正确或尝试使用公司简称。"
        results = []
        for _, row in matches.head(5).iterrows(): 
            code = row.get('code', 'N/A')
            name = row.get('name', 'N/A')
        
            try:
                detail_df = ak.stock_individual_info_em(symbol=code)
                detail_dict = dict(zip(detail_df['item'], detail_df['value']))
                
                info = {
                    "股票代码": code,
                    "公司名称": name,
                    "总市值": detail_dict.get('总市值', 'N/A'),
                    "流通市值": detail_dict.get('流通市值', 'N/A'),
                    "行业": detail_dict.get('行业', 'N/A'),
                    "上市时间": detail_dict.get('上市时间', 'N/A'),
                    "股票简称": detail_dict.get('股票简称', name),
                    "总股本": detail_dict.get('总股本', 'N/A'),
                    "流通股": detail_dict.get('流通股', 'N/A'),
                }
            except Exception:
                info = {
                    "股票代码": code,
                    "公司名称": name,
                }
            
            results.append(info)
        
        return json.dumps(results, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
        
    except Exception as e:
        return f"获取公司信息时出错：{str(e)}"
```

--------------------------------

### Retrieve File Information (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/files

Fetches basic information about a specific file uploaded to Moonshot AI, identified by its file ID. This includes metadata about the file.

```Python
client.files.retrieve(file_id=file_id)
# FileObject(

```

### Call a Remote Formula Tool via Moonshot Client

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-k2-to-setup-agent

Asynchronously calls a specific function (tool) within a formula on the Moonshot platform. It sends the function name and arguments via an HTTP POST request and returns the output or an error message if the call fails. Handles encrypted output.

```python
    async def call_tool(self, formula_uri: str, function: str, args: dict):
        response = await self.httpx.post(
            f"/formulas/{formula_uri}/fibers",
            json={"name": function, "arguments": json.dumps(args)},
        )
        fiber = response.json()

        if fiber.get("status") == "succeeded":
            return fiber["context"].get("output") or fiber["context"].get("encrypted_output")

        # Handle errors
        error_msg = fiber.get("error") or fiber.get("context", {}).get("error") or \
                    fiber.get("context", {}).get("output") or "Unknown error"
        return f"Error: {error_msg}"
```

### Implement Automatic Reconnection for API Calls - Python

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/auto-reconnect

This Python code snippet demonstrates how to implement automatic reconnection for API calls to handle network interruptions or rate limiting. It retries failed requests up to a specified maximum number of attempts with a delay between each retry. The function takes user input and returns the model's response.

```python
from openai import OpenAI
import time

client = OpenAI(
    api_key = "$MOONSHOT_API_KEY",
    base_url = "https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

def chat_once(msgs):
    response = client.chat.completions.create(
        model = "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
        messages = msgs,
        temperature = 0.6,
    )
    return response.choices[0].message.content

def chat(input: str, max_attempts: int = 100) -> str:
    messages = [
	    {"role": "system", "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"},
    ]

	# 我们将用户最新的问题构造成一个 message（role=user），并添加到 messages 的尾部
    messages.append({
		"role": "user",
		"content": input,	
	})
    st_time = time.time()
    for i in range(max_attempts):
        print(f"Attempts: {i+1}/{max_attempts}")
        try:
            response = chat_once(messages)
            ed_time = time.time()
            print("Query Succuess!")
            print(f"Query Time: {ed_time-st_time}")
            return response
        except Exception as e:
            print(e)
            time.sleep(1)
            continue

    print("Query Failed.")
    return

print(chat("你好，请给我讲一个童话故事。"))
```

### 定义自定义工具 (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-k2-to-setup-agent

使用Python定义一个名为'company_info'的工具，该工具通过JSON Schema描述，用于根据公司名称获取其股票代码、市场类型等信息。适用于大模型在知识不足或用户明确要求查询公司信息时调用。

```python
TOOLS = [
    {
        "type": "function",
        "function": {
            "name": "company_info",
            "description": "根据公司名称获取公司信息（股票代码、市场类型、上市状态等）。当你的知识无法回答用户提出的问题，或用户请求你进行公司信息查询时，调用此工具。",
            "parameters": {
                "type": "object",
                "properties": {
                    "name": {
                        "type": "string",
                        "description": "用户想要查询的公司的准确名称，请从与用户的对话中提取。"
                    }
                },
                "required": ["name"]
            }
        }
    }
    // 可以仿照上面的格式继续定义更多工具
]
```

### Retrieve File Content API

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/files

Retrieves the content of a specific file. Note: The `retrieve_content` API is marked with a warning in the latest version and can be replaced by the `content` method.

```APIDOC
## GET /v1/files/{file_id}/content

### Description
Retrieves the content of a specific file. Note: The `retrieve_content` API is marked with a warning in the latest version and can be replaced by the `content` method.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/files/{file_id}/content

### Parameters
#### Path Parameters
- **file_id** (string) - Required - The unique identifier of the file whose content is to be retrieved.

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **text** (string) - The content of the file.

#### Response Example
```text
This is the content of the file.
```

### Request Example
```python
file_id_to_get_content = "file-xxxxxxxxxxxx"
# For latest version
file_content = client.files.content(file_id=file_id_to_get_content).text

# For older versions, retrieve_content might be used:
# file_content = client.files.retrieve_content(file_id=file_id_to_get_content)

print(file_content)
```
```

--------------------------------

### Using Kimi API's JSON Mode

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-json-mode-feature-of-kimi-api

This section explains how to use the JSON Mode feature of the Kimi API to ensure that the model outputs content in a valid JSON format. It covers the `response_format` parameter and provides guidance on structuring prompts for optimal results.

```APIDOC
## Using Kimi API's JSON Mode

### Description
This endpoint allows you to leverage the Kimi API to generate structured JSON output. By default, the API returns text. To enable JSON output, you need to use the `response_format` parameter.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
/chat/completions

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **response_format** (object) - Required - Specifies the desired output format. Set to `{"type": "json_object"}` to enable JSON Mode.

#### Request Body
- **model** (string) - Required - The model to use (e.g., `kimi-k2-turbo-preview`).
- **messages** (array) - Required - An array of message objects, including system and user prompts.
  - **role** (string) - Required - The role of the message ('system' or 'user').
  - **content** (string) - Required - The content of the message.
- **temperature** (number) - Optional - Controls randomness. Lower values make output more focused.
- **max_tokens** (integer) - Optional - The maximum number of tokens to generate. Ensure this is sufficient for your expected JSON output.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "model": "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
  "messages": [
    {
      "role": "system",
      "content": "You are Kimi, an AI assistant. Respond in JSON format with fields: 'title', 'author', 'publish_time', 'summary'. Example: {\"title\": \"Example Title\", \"author\": \"Example Author\", \"publish_time\": \"2023-01-01\", \"summary\": \"This is an example summary.\"}"
    },
    {
      "role": "user",
      "content": "Summarize the following article: [Article Content]"
    }
  ],
  "temperature": 0.6,
  "response_format": {"type": "json_object"}
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **choices** (array) - Contains the model's response.
  - **message** (object)
    - **content** (string) - A JSON string representing the structured output.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "choices": [
    {
      "message": {
        "content": "{\"title\": \"文章标题\", \"author\": \"文章作者\", \"publish_time\": \"发布时间\", \"summary\": \"文章总结\"}"
      }
    }
  ]
}
```

### Important Notes
- Clearly define the expected JSON structure, including field names and types, in your system or user prompt. Providing an example is highly recommended.
- The API will only generate JSON Objects. Do not attempt to generate JSON Arrays or other JSON types.
- If the JSON output is incomplete or truncated, check the `finish_reason` in the response. A `finish_reason` of `length` indicates that `max_tokens` might be too small. Adjust `max_tokens` based on the expected size of your JSON output.

```

--------------------------------

### Kimi API - $web_search Function Declaration

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-web-search

This section details how to declare the built-in $web_search function within the 'tools' parameter for Kimi API. It highlights the 'builtin_function' type and the specific function name '$web_search'.

```APIDOC
## $web_search Declaration

Unlike regular 'tool' definitions, the '$web_search' function does not require specific parameter descriptions. You can successfully register it by providing the 'type' as 'builtin_function' and the 'function.name' as '$web_search' in your 'tools' declaration.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
/v1/chat/completions

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **tools** (array) - Required - A list of tool definitions. For the web search functionality, include an object with:
  - **type** (string) - Required - Must be `"builtin_function"` to indicate a Kimi built-in tool.
  - **function** (object) - Required - Contains the definition of the built-in function.
    - **name** (string) - Required - Must be `"$web_search"`.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "model": "kimi-turbo",
  "messages": [
    {"role": "user", "content": "请帮我搜索一下关于AI的最新进展"}
  ],
  "tools": [
    {
      "type": "builtin_function",
      "function": {
        "name": "$web_search"
      }
    }
  ]
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **tool_calls** (array) - If the model decides to use the $web_search tool, this array will contain a tool call object.
  - **id** (string) - The ID of the tool call.
  - **type** (string) - Always `"function"`.
  - **function** (object) - Details about the function call.
    - **name** (string) - The name of the function, which will be `"$web_search"`.
    - **arguments** (string) - A JSON string representing the arguments for the function call. For $web_search, this typically includes a 'query' field.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "id": "chatcmpl-xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx",
  "object": "chat.completion",
  "created": 1677652288,
  "model": "kimi-turbo",
  "choices": [
    {
      "index": 0,
      "message": {
        "role": "assistant",
        "content": null,
        "tool_calls": [
          {
            "id": "call_xxxxxxxxxxxxxxxxx",
            "type": "function",
            "function": {
              "name": "$web_search",
              "arguments": "{\"query\": \"AI的最新进展\"}"
            }
          }
        ]
      },
      "finish_reason": "tool_calls"
    }
  ],
  "usage": {
    "prompt_tokens": 10,
    "completion_tokens": 10
  }
}
```

**Note**: The `$` prefix in `$web_search` is a convention indicating a Kimi built-in function. Regular function names in Kimi API should not contain the `$` symbol.
```

--------------------------------

### Handle Chatbot Responses and Tool Calls in Moonshot Client

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-k2-to-setup-agent

Processes responses from the OpenAI API, appending them to the message history. It distinguishes between regular text responses and tool calls. For tool calls, it identifies custom tools (like 'company_info') and remote formula tools, executes them, and appends the results back to the message history for the next turn. Includes logic for 'code_runner' and recursively calls itself for subsequent responses.

```python
    async def handle_response(self, response, messages, all_tools, tool_to_uri):
        message = response.choices[0].message
        messages.append(message)
        
        if not message.tool_calls:
            print(f"\n{message.content}")
            return

        print(f"\n[调用工具: {len(message.tool_calls)}个]")

        for call in message.tool_calls:
            func_name = call.function.name
            args = json.loads(call.function.arguments)

            print(f"→ {func_name}")
            
            # 处理自定义工具
            if func_name == "company_info":
                company_name = args.get("name", "")
                result = get_company_info(company_name)
                print(f"公司信息: {result}")
                messages.append({"role": "tool", "tool_call_id": call.id, "content": result})
                continue
            
            # 处理远程 formula 工具
            uri = tool_to_uri.get(func_name)
            if not uri:
                raise ValueError(f"No URI found for tool {func_name}")

            if func_name == "code_runner":
                self.execute_code_runner(args)

            result = await self.call_tool(uri, func_name, args)
            messages.append({"role": "tool", "tool_call_id": call.id, "content": result})

        next_response = await self.openai.chat.completions.create(
            model=self.model, messages=messages, tools=all_tools, max_tokens=self.max_tokens
        )
        await self.handle_response(next_response, messages, all_tools, tool_to_uri)
```

--------------------------------

### Kimi K2 Agent System Prompt 示例

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-k2-to-setup-agent

这是一个用于 Kimi K2 Agent 的系统提示词示例，定义了 AI 助手的角色、语言统一要求、图表规范（配色、元素、排版）、数据来源要求以及报告结构。

```python
SYSTEM_PROMPT = r"""你是 Kimi，专业的企业行业研究 AI 助手，擅长信息搜索、数据分析和商业报告生成。
  
## 1. 语言统一

**重要**：所有输出内容必须与用户提问语言保持一致。

**具体要求**：
- 报告文本：使用与用户提问相同的语言（中文问用中文答，英文问用英文答）
- 图表标题/图表轴标签/图表图例/数据标签：必须使用用户提问的语言，字体兼容mac，windows等
- 禁止混合语言：文本和图表语言需要一致
  - 例：用户中文提问->即使图表字体报错，也要不断尝试，**禁止**用英文替代

## 2. 图表规范

### 2.1 配色规范（视觉规范）

**配色方案**（所有图表颜色按优先级使用）：
| 优先级    | 角色说明       | 颜色（按使用顺序）                            | 观感关键词  |
| ------ | -------------- | ----------------------------------------------- | ------ |
| 一级（主色） | 标题、KPI 大数字、主柱形 | 1-1 `#004C8C` 1-2 `#0065B5`                  | 深夜蓝，权威 |
| 二级（辅色） | 次要系列、折线、网格     | 2-1 `#5B7FA5` 2-2 `#8EA9C1` 2-3 `#B7C7D8` | 雾蓝，专业  |
| 三级（强调） | 需突出系列、预警       | 3-1 `#C00033` 3-2 `#D0D0D0`                  | 暗殷红，点缀 |
| 四级（补色） | 第三系列、预测虚线      | 4-1 `#7A7390` 4-2 `#8F8CA8` 4-3 `#C9C7D2` | 石墨紫，稳重 |

**使用规则**：
- 使用python绘图
- 只能使用上述颜色，**禁止使用任何其他颜色**
- 对每张图表**单独考虑**优先级，按优先级顺序使用，优先使用高级别的颜色

### 2.2 图表元素与排版规范

- **必须满足** **重要** ： 图例、数据标注、图表标题、图表轴标签等任何图表元素内容**不能相互重叠或遮挡**。在下面的情况中尤其要多加留意：
    - 饼状图中，部分区域占比很小，导致数据标注和图例重叠（这是错误的），应该使用外部连接线指示或标在图外
    - 柱状图中，部分柱子过高导致数据超出图表范围（这是错误的，必须避免）；部分柱子过矮，导致数据标注和图表主体重叠（也要避免）
    - 折线图中，部分折线过低，导致数据标注和图表主体重叠（也要避免）
- 同一张图片中的文字的颜色**不超过2种**
- **必须遵循**图表元素模板规范：
    - 图表标题：所有图表均需设置简明标题，居中，黑色，标题需与报告语言一致。
    - 横纵坐标轴标签：需完整注明所表达含义与计量单位，黑色，字号适中。
    - 图例（legend）：如有多组数据，必须设置图例，图例位置优先在图表右上/右侧，避免遮挡图表主体区域。图例内容需与系列含义完全对应。
    - 数据标签（如单柱/折线节点标注）：仅在数据点间隔足够大、不遮挡主图时使用。

- 不得随意更改模板结构。严禁在同一图表中出现多种格式混用。
- **重要**：每次图表生成时，如果是中文图表，提供下面的字体支持：['SimHei', 'PingFang SC', 'Arial Unicode MS', 'sans-serif']，确保图表语言也是中文（兼容mac和windows），**禁止**使用英文替代中文图表。

## 3. 数据来源

**严禁编造数据**。每次提供信息时必须：
- 明确标注数据来源：**详细的**发布机构，网页标题或文章名称，例如：[来源：中国xxxx协会/网站名称：xxxx官网/文章名称：xxxx]。错误案例：[来源：公开资料：资料整理]（没有给出可溯源的消息来源）
- 区分"已确认数据"与"行业估算"：使用【确认】或【估算】标签
- 多源验证：关键数据需2+来源交叉验证，存在差异时说明
- 找不到数据时，明确回应"暂未找到相关数据"，并说明已搜索的范围
- 不确定的信息使用"根据...可能/估计"等表述，避免断言
- **不要**在报告中使用完整URL链接。

**信息引用格式**：

数据内容[来源：XX机构/网站名称：网页标题或文章名称]


## 4. 报告结构
输出内容应遵循以下结构：

**信息搜索阶段**：
- 明确搜索策略和关键词
- **记录所有访问的来源机构和网页标题或文章名称**：每次 web-search 后记录使用的来源机构和网页标题或文章名称
- 列出信息来源和获取时间（来源机构：网页标题或文章名称）
- 标注数据可信度等级（官方统计三颗星 “***” > 行业报告两颗星 “**” > 新闻报道一颗星 “*”）  

**数据分析阶段**：
- 描述性统计：趋势、分布、对比
- 洞察发现：关键发现用【洞察】标注
- 风险提示：不确定性和局限性说明

**报告输出阶段**：
- 执行摘要：3-5点核心发现
- 数据可视化：专业图表配色
- 结论建议：可操作的商业建议
- 参考来源：完整的信息源列表
- 正确语法：正确使用LaTeX语法，确保可以借助xelatex编译生成pdf文件。

"""
```

--------------------------------

### File Upload API

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/files

Uploads a file to the Moonshot AI platform. Files can be used for content extraction, image understanding, or video understanding. There are limits on the number of files, file size, and total storage.

```APIDOC
## POST /v1/files

### Description
Uploads a file to the Moonshot AI platform. Files can be used for content extraction, image understanding, or video understanding. There are limits on the number of files, file size, and total storage.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/files

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **purpose** (string) - Required - Specifies the intended use of the file. Supported values are "file-extract", "image", "video".

#### Request Body
- **file** (file) - Required - The file to be uploaded.

### Request Example
```python
from pathlib import Path
from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key = "$MOONSHOT_API_KEY",
    base_url = "https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

# For content extraction
file_object = client.files.create(file=Path("xlnet.pdf"), purpose="file-extract")

# For image understanding
# file_object = client.files.create(file=Path("image.jpg"), purpose="image")

# For video understanding
# file_object = client.files.create(file=Path("video.mp4"), purpose="video")
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **id** (string) - The unique identifier for the uploaded file.
- **object** (string) - The type of object, typically "file".
- **bytes** (integer) - The size of the file in bytes.
- **created_at** (integer) - The Unix timestamp of when the file was created.
- **filename** (string) - The name of the file.
- **purpose** (string) - The purpose for which the file was uploaded.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "id": "file-xxxxxxxxxxxx",
  "object": "file",
  "bytes": 12345,
  "created_at": 1678886400,
  "filename": "xlnet.pdf",
  "purpose": "file-extract"
}
```

### Supported Formats
.pdf, .txt, .csv, .doc, .docx, .xls, .xlsx, .ppt, .pptx, .md, .jpeg, .png, .bmp, .gif, .svg, .svgz, .webp, .ico, .xbm, .dib, .pjp, .tif, .pjpeg, .avif, .dot, .apng, .epub, .tiff, .jfif, .html, .json, .mobi, .log, .go, .h, .c, .cpp, .cxx, .cc, .cs, .java, .js, .css, .jsp, .php, .py, .py3, .asp, .yaml, .yml, .ini, .conf, .ts, .tsx

### Notes
- Single user limit: 1000 files.
- Single file size limit: 100MB.
- Total storage limit: 10GB.
- File parsing service is temporarily free. Rate limiting may apply during peak hours.
```

### Kimi Tool Use 示例 (JSON)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/tool-use

展示了如何使用 JSON 格式配置 Kimi 大模型进行工具调用。该配置指定了模型、用户消息以及可用的工具（CodeRunner），包括工具的类型、名称、描述和参数。

```json
{
  "model": "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
  "messages": [
    {
      "role": "user",
      "content": "编程判断 3214567 是否是素数。"
    }
  ],
  "tools": [
    {
      "type": "function",
      "function": {
        "name": "CodeRunner",
        "description": "代码执行器，支持运行 python 和 javascript 代码",
        "parameters": {
          "properties": {
            "language": {
              "type": "string",
              "enum": ["python", "javascript"]
            },
            "code": {
              "type": "string",
              "description": "代码写在这里"
            }
          },
          "type": "object"
        }
      }
    }
  ]
}
```

### Correct Kimi Vision Model API Request Structure (JSON)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-vision-model

This JSON object represents the correct structure for a request to the Kimi Vision model. It shows how to format the `messages` array with a system prompt and a user prompt containing both an `image_url` part and a `text` part. This structure is crucial for the model to correctly interpret multimodal inputs.

```json
{
    "model": "kimi-k2.5",
    "messages":
    [
        {
            "role": "system",
            "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"
        },
        {
            "role": "user",
            "content":
            [
                {
                    "type": "image_url",
                    "image_url":
                    {
                        "url": "data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAGAAAABhCAYAAAApxKSdAAAACXBIWXMAACE4AAAhOAFFljFgAAAAAXNSR0IArs4c6QAAAARnQU1BAACxjwv8YQUAAAUUSURBVHgB7Z29bhtHFIWPHQN2J7lKqnhYpYvpIukCbJEAKQJEegLReYFIT0DrCSI9QEDqCSIDaQIEIOukiJwyza5SJWlId3FFz+HuGmuSSw6p+dlZ3g84luhdUeI9M3fmziyXgBCUe/DHYY0Wj/tgWmjV42zFcWe4MIBBPNJ6qqW0uvAbXFvQgKzQK62bQhkaCIPc10q1Zi3XH1o/IG9cwUm0RogrgDY1KmLgHYX9DvyiBvDYI77XmiD+oLlQHw7hIDoCMBOt1U9w0BsU9mOAtaUUFk3oQoIfzAQFCf5dNMEdTFCQ4NtQih1NSIGgf3ibxOJt5UrAB1gNK72vIdjiI61HWr+YnNxDXK0rJiULsV65GJeiIescLSTTeobKSutiCuojX8kU3MBx4I3WeNVBBRl4fWiCyoB8v2JAAkk9PmDwT8sH1TEghRjgC27scCx41wO43KAg+ILxTvhNaUACwTc04Z0B30LwzTzm5Rjw3sgseIG1wGMawMBPIOQcqvzrNIMHOg9Q5KK953O90/rFC+BhJRH8PQZ+fu7SjC7HAIV95yu99vjlxfvBJx8nwHd6IfNJAkccOjHg6OgIs9lsra6vr2GTNE03/k7q8HAhyJ/2gM9O65/4kT7/mwEcoZwYsPQiV3BwcABb9Ho9KKU2njccDjGdLlxx+InBBPBAAR86ydRPaIC9SASi3+8bnXd+fr78nw8NJ39uDJjXAVFPP7dp/VmWLR9g6w6Huo/IOTk5MTpvZesn/93AiP/dXCwd9SyILT9Jko3n1bZ+8s8rGPGvoVHbEXcPMM39V1dX9Qd/19PPNxta959D4HUGF0RrAFs/8/8mxuPxXLUwtfx2WX+cxdivZ3DFA0SKldZPuPTAKrikbOlMOX+9zFu/Q2iAQoSY5H7mfeb/tXCT8MdneU9wNNCuQUXZA0ynnrUznyqOcrspUY4BJunHqPU3gOgMsNr6G0B0BpgUXrG0fhKVAaaF1/HxMWIhKgNMcj9Tz82Nk6rVGdav/tJ5eraJ0Wi01XPq1r/xOS8uLkJc6XYnRTMNXdf62eIvLy+jyftVghnQ7Xahe8FW59fBTRYOzosDNI1hJdz0lBQkBflkMBjMU5iL13pXRb8fYAJrB/a2db0oFHthAOEUliaYFHE+aaUBdZsvvFhApyM0idYZwOCvW4JmIWdSzPmidQaYrAGZ7iX4oFUGnJ2dGdUCTRqMozeANQCLsE6nA10JG/0Mx4KmDMbBCjEWR2yxu8LAM98vXelmCA2ovVLCI8EMYODWbpbvCXtTBzQVMSAwYkBgxIDAtNKAXWdGIRADAiMpKDA0IIMQikx6QGDEgMCIAYGRMSAsMgaEhgbcQgjFa+kBYZnIGBCWWzEgLPNBOJ6Fk/aR8Y5ZCvktKwX/PJZ7xoVjfs+4chYU11tK2sE85qUBLyH4Zh5z6QHhGPOf6r2j+TEbcgdFP2RaHX5TrYQlDflj5RXE5Q1cG/lWnhYpReUGKdUewGnRmhvnCJbgmxey8sHiZ8iwF3AsUBBckKHI/SWLq6HsBc8huML4DiK80D6WnBqLzN68UFCmopheYJOVYgcU5FOVbAVfYUcUZGoaLPglCtITdg2+tZUFBTFh2+ArWEYh/7z0WIIQSiM43lt5AWAmWhLHylN4QmkNEXfAbGqEQKsHSfHLYwiSq8AnaAAKeaW3D8VbijwNW5nh3IN9FPI/jnpaPKZi2/SfFuJu4W3x9RqWL+N5C+7ruKpBAgLkAAAAAElFTkSuQmCC"

### Chat Completion API

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/chat

This endpoint facilitates chat completions by taking a list of messages and model parameters to generate a conversational response.

```APIDOC
## POST /websites/platform_moonshot_cn/chat/completions

### Description
This endpoint allows you to generate chat completions by sending a list of messages and various optional parameters to control the model's behavior and output.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
/websites/platform_moonshot_cn/chat/completions

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **messages** (List[Dict]) - Required - A list of message objects representing the conversation history. Each message should have a 'role' ('system', 'user', or 'assistant') and 'content' (string or List[Dict]).
- **model** (string) - Required - The ID of the model to use for generation. Available models include `kimi-k2.5`, `kimi-k2-0905-preview`, `kimi-k2-0711-preview`, `kimi-k2-turbo-preview`, `kimi-k2-thinking-turbo`, `kimi-k2-thinking`, `moonshot-v1-8k`, `moonshot-v1-32k`, `moonshot-v1-128k`, `moonshot-v1-auto`, `moonshot-v1-8k-vision-preview`, `moonshot-v1-32k-vision-preview`, `moonshot-v1-128k-vision-preview`.
- **max_tokens** (int) - Optional - The maximum number of tokens to generate in the completion. If the generation reaches this limit, the `finish_reason` will be 'length'.
- **temperature** (float) - Optional - Controls the randomness of the output. Values between 0 and 1. Higher values increase randomness, lower values increase determinism. Defaults vary by model family.
- **top_p** (float) - Optional - An alternative sampling method. It considers tokens comprising the top p probability mass. Defaults to 1.0 for most models, 0.95 for `kimi-k2.5`.
- **n** (int) - Optional - The number of completions to generate for each input message. Defaults to 1. Maximum is 5.
- **presence_penalty** (float) - Optional - A penalty for new tokens based on whether they appear in the text so far. Ranges from -2.0 to 2.0. Defaults to 0.
- **frequency_penalty** (float) - Optional - A penalty for new tokens based on their existing frequency in the text so far. Ranges from -2.0 to 2.0. Defaults to 0.
- **response_format** (object) - Optional - Set to `{"type": "json_object"}` to enable JSON mode, ensuring the output is valid JSON. Requires explicit prompting for JSON structure.
- **stop** (String or List[String]) - Optional - Sequences where the API will stop generating further tokens. Maximum 5 strings, each up to 32 bytes.
- **thinking** (object) - Optional - Only for `kimi-k2.5`. Controls whether the model's thinking process is enabled. Use `{"type": "enabled"}` or `{"type": "disabled"}`. Defaults to `{"type": "enabled"}`.
- **stream** (bool) - Optional - Whether to stream the response. Defaults to false.

#### Content Field Description
The `content` field within messages can be a simple string or a list of dictionaries for complex content:
- **text**: Plain text content.
- **image_url**: Represents an image. The value is a dictionary containing a 'url' field, which can be a base64 encoded string or an `ms://<file_id>` format.
- **video_url**: Represents a video. The value is a dictionary containing a 'url' field, similar to `image_url`.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "model": "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
  "messages": [
    {"role": "system", "content": "You are a helpful assistant."},
    {"role": "user", "content": "你好"}
  ],
  "max_tokens": 1024,
  "temperature": 0.7,
  "stream": false
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **id** (string) - Unique identifier for the completion.
- **object** (string) - Type of the object, e.g., 'chat.completion'.
- **created** (integer) - Timestamp of creation.
- **model** (string) - The model used for the completion.
- **choices** (List[object]) - A list of completion choices.
  - **index** (integer) - Index of the choice.
  - **message** (object) - The message object.
    - **role** (string) - Role of the message sender ('assistant').
    - **content** (string) - The generated content.
  - **finish_reason** (string) - The reason the model stopped generating (e.g., 'stop', 'length').
- **usage** (object) - Token usage statistics.
  - **prompt_tokens** (integer) - Number of tokens in the prompt.
  - **completion_tokens** (integer) - Number of tokens in the completion.
  - **total_tokens** (integer) - Total tokens used.
  - **cached_tokens** (integer) - Number of cached tokens hit (if applicable).

#### Stream Response Example
```
data: {"id":"cmpl-1305b94c570f447fbde3180560736287","object":"chat.completion.chunk","created":1698999575,"model":"kimi-k2-turbo-preview","choices":[{"index":0,"delta":{"role":"assistant","content":""},"finish_reason":null}]}

data: {"id":"cmpl-1305b94c570f447fbde3180560736287","object":"chat.completion.chunk","created":1698999575,"model":"kimi-k2-turbo-preview","choices":[{"index":0,"delta":{"content":"你好"},"finish_reason":null}]}

...

data: [DONE]
```

#### Response Example (Non-Stream)
```json
{
    "id": "cmpl-04ea926191a14749b7f2c7a48a68abc6",
    "object": "chat.completion",
    "created": 1698999496,
    "model": "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
    "choices": [
        {
            "index": 0,
            "message": {
                "role": "assistant",
                "content": " 你好，李雷！1+1等于2。如果你有其他问题，请随时提问！"
            },
            "finish_reason": "stop"
        }
    ],
    "usage": {
        "prompt_tokens": 19,
        "completion_tokens": 21,
        "total_tokens": 40,
        "cached_tokens": 10
    }
}
```
```

--------------------------------

### List Uploaded Files (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/files

Retrieves a list of all files previously uploaded by the user to the Moonshot AI platform. This function is useful for managing stored files and checking their status.

```Python
file_list = client.files.list()

for file in file_list.data:
    print(file) # View information for each file

```

### Inspect Request

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-moonpalace

Retrieve detailed information about a specific request using its ID, chat completion ID, or request ID. By default, request and response bodies are not printed.

```APIDOC
## GET /websites/platform_moonshot_cn/inspect

### Description
Retrieves detailed metadata for a specific request. You can identify the request using its unique ID, chat completion ID, or request ID.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
`/websites/platform_moonshot_cn/inspect`

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **id** (string) - Optional - The unique identifier for the request.
- **chatcmpl** (string) - Optional - The chat completion ID associated with the request.
- **requestid** (string) - Optional - The request ID for identifying the request.
- **print** (string) - Optional - Specifies which parts of the request to print. Accepted values include `request_body` and `response_body`. Example: `request_body,response_body`.

### Request Example
```bash
moonpalace inspect --id 13
moonpalace inspect --chatcmpl chatcmpl-2e1aa823e2c94ebdad66450a0e6df088
moonpalace inspect --requestid c07c118e-4dae-11ef-b423-62db244b9277
moonpalace inspect --chatcmpl chatcmpl-2e1aa823e2c94ebdad66450a0e6df088 --print request_body,response_body
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **metadata** (object) - Contains various details about the request, including `chatcmpl`, `content_type`, `group_id`, `moonpalace_id`, `request_id`, `requested_at`, `server_timing`, `status`, and `user_id`.
- **request_body** (object) - The body of the request (only if `--print request_body` is used).
- **response_body** (object) - The body of the response (only if `--print response_body` is used).

#### Response Example
```json
{
    "metadata": {
        "chatcmpl": "chatcmpl-2e1aa823e2c94ebdad66450a0e6df088",
        "content_type": "application/json",
        "group_id": "enterprise-tier-5",
        "moonpalace_id": "13",
        "request_id": "c07c118e-4dae-11ef-b423-62db244b9277",
        "requested_at": "2024-07-29 21:30:43",
        "server_timing": "1033",
        "status": "200 OK",
        "user_id": "cn0psmmcp7fclnphkcpg"
    }
}
```
```

--------------------------------

### Query Balance API

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/balance

This API endpoint allows users to query their current balance, including available balance, voucher balance, and cash balance. The available balance determines the user's ability to call inference APIs.

```APIDOC
## GET /v1/users/me/balance

### Description
Retrieves the current balance information for the authenticated user, including available, voucher, and cash balances.

### Method
GET

### Endpoint
/v1/users/me/balance

### Parameters
#### Path Parameters
None

#### Query Parameters
None

#### Request Body
None

### Request Example
```bash
curl https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/users/me/balance -H "Authorization: Bearer $MOONSHOT_API_KEY"
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **code** (integer) - Response code, 0 indicates success.
- **data** (object) - Contains balance details.
  - **available_balance** (float) - The total available balance, including cash and voucher balances. If less than or equal to 0, the user cannot call inference APIs. (Unit: CNY)
  - **voucher_balance** (float) - The balance from vouchers. This value will not be negative. (Unit: CNY)
  - **cash_balance** (float) - The cash balance. This can be negative, indicating the user is in debt. If negative, `available_balance` will reflect the `voucher_balance`.
- **scode** (string) - Status code, '0x0' indicates success.
- **status** (boolean) - Indicates if the request was successful.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "code": 0,
  "data": {
    "available_balance": 49.58894,
    "voucher_balance": 46.58893,
    "cash_balance": 3.00001
  },
  "scode": "0x0",
  "status": true
}
```
```

--------------------------------

### Retrieve File Content using Python

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/files

This Python code snippet demonstrates how to retrieve the content of an extracted file using the Moonshot API. It utilizes the `client.files.content` method, which returns the file content as text. The retrieved content is expected to be in a JSON format but should be passed as a string when used within messages.

```python
# file_content = client.files.retrieve_content(file_id=file_object.id)
# type of file_content is `str`
# 注意，之前 retrieve_content api 在最新版本标记了 warning, 可以用下面这行代替
# 如果是旧版本，可以用 retrieve_content
file_content = client.files.content(file_id=file_object.id).text
# 我们的输出结果目前是一个内部约定好格式的 json, 但是在 message 中应该以 text 格式放进去
```

### Configure Chinese Font Support for Matplotlib

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-k2-to-setup-agent

Sets Matplotlib's sans-serif fonts to include Chinese support ('SimHei', 'PingFang SC', 'Arial Unicode MS') and disables the unicode minus sign for better display of Chinese characters in plots.

```python
plt.rcParams['font.sans-serif'] = ['SimHei', 'PingFang SC', 'Arial Unicode MS', 'sans-serif']
plt.rcParams['axes.unicode_minus'] = False
```

### Formula Invocation API

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-official-tools

This API endpoint allows you to invoke a specific Formula by providing its URI and arguments. The platform handles the execution and returns the result.

```APIDOC
## POST /formulas/{FORMULA_URI}/fibers

### Description
Invokes a specific Formula with provided arguments.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
`/formulas/{FORMULA_URI}/fibers`

### Parameters
#### Path Parameters
- **FORMULA_URI** (string) - Required - The unique identifier for the Formula to be invoked (e.g., `moonshot/web-search:latest`).

#### Query Parameters
None

#### Request Body
- **name** (string) - Required - The name of the function within the Formula to call.
- **arguments** (string) - Required - A JSON string representing the arguments for the function. This should be an encoded string as provided by the model's tool call.

### Request Example
```json
{
  "name": "web_search",
  "arguments": "{\"query\": \"月之暗面最近有什么消息\"}"
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **output** (string) - The result of the Formula execution. For protected formulas, this may be an encrypted string.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "output": "----MOONSHOT ENCRYPTED BEGIN----... ----MOONSHOT ENCRYPTED END----"
}
```
```

--------------------------------

### Incorrect Kimi Vision Model API Request Structure (JSON)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-vision-model

This JSON object illustrates an incorrect format for sending multimodal requests to the Kimi Vision model. It shows a scenario where the `content` field might be incorrectly serialized as a string, leading to errors. The documentation emphasizes that `content` should be a list of dictionaries, not a serialized string.

```json
{
    "model": "kimi-k2.5",
    "messages":
    [
        {
            "role": "system",
            "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"
        },
        {
            "role": "user",
            "content": "[\"{\\\"type\\\": \\\"image_url\\\", \\\"image_url\\\": {\\\"url\\\": {\\"type\\": \\\"text\\\", \\\"text\\\": \\\"请描述图片的内容。\\\"}]"], 
    "temperature": 0.3
}
```

### Export Request

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-moonpalace

Export a specific request for review or reporting purposes. You can categorize it as a 'good case' or 'bad case' and add tags.

```APIDOC
## POST /websites/platform_moonshot_cn/export

### Description
Exports a specific request, allowing you to categorize it as a good or bad case and assign tags. This is useful for reporting or analysis.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
`/websites/platform_moonshot_cn/export`

### Parameters
#### Query Parameters
- **id** (string) - Optional - The unique identifier for the request.
- **chatcmpl** (string) - Optional - The chat completion ID associated with the request.
- **requestid** (string) - Optional - The request ID for identifying the request.
- **good** (boolean) - Optional - Flag to mark the request as a 'good case'.
- **bad** (boolean) - Optional - Flag to mark the request as a 'bad case'.
- **tag** (string) - Optional - Tags to categorize the request (can be used multiple times). Example: `--tag "code" --tag "python"`.
- **directory** (string) - Required - The directory path where the exported file will be saved.

### Request Example
```bash
moonpalace export \
    --id 13 \
    --good \
    --tag "code" --tag "python" \
    --directory $HOME/Downloads/
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **message** (string) - Confirmation message indicating successful export.

#### Response Example
```json
{
    "message": "Request exported successfully to $HOME/Downloads/chatcmpl-2e1aa823e2c94ebdad66450a0e6df088.json"
}
```

### Exported File Content Example
```json
{
    "metadata": {
        "chatcmpl": "chatcmpl-2e1aa823e2c94ebdad66450a0e6df088",
        "content_type": "application/json",
        "group_id": "enterprise-tier-5",
        "moonpalace_id": "13",
        "request_id": "c07c118e-4dae-11ef-b423-62db244b9277",
        "requested_at": "2024-07-29 21:30:43",
        "server_timing": "1033",
        "status": "200 OK",
        "user_id": "cn0psmmcp7fclnphkcpg"
    },
    "request": {
        "url": "https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/chat/completions",
        "header": "Accept: application/json\r\nAccept-Encoding: gzip\r\nConnection: keep-alive\r\nContent-Length: 2450\r\nContent-Type: application/json\r\nUser-Agent: OpenAI/Python 1.36.1\r\nX-Stainless-Arch: arm64\r\nX-Stainless-Async: false\r\nX-Stainless-Lang: python\r\nX-Stainless-Os: MacOS\r\nX-Stainless-Package-Version: 1.36.1\r\nX-Stainless-Runtime: CPython\r\nX-Stainless-Runtime-Version: 3.11.6\r\n",
        "body": {}
    },
    "response": {
        "status": "200 OK",
        "header": "Content-Encoding: gzip\r\nContent-Type: application/json; charset=utf-8\r\nDate: Mon, 29 Jul 2024 13:30:43 GMT\r\nMsh-Cache: updated\r\nMsh-Gid: enterprise-tier-5\r\nMsh-Request-Id: c07c118e-4dae-11ef-b423-62db244b9277\r\nMsh-Trace-Mode: on\r\nMsh-Uid: cn0psmmcp7fclnphkcpg\r\nServer: nginx\r\nServer-Timing: inner; dur=1033\r\nStrict-Transport-Security: max-age=15724800; includeSubDomains\r\nVary: Accept-Encoding\r\nVary: Origin\r\n",
        "body": {}
    },
    "category": "goodcase",
    "tags": [
        "code",
        "python"
    ]
}
```
```

### POST /v1/tokenizers/estimate-token-count

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/estimate

This endpoint calculates the token count for a given request, which can include both text and visual inputs. It's useful for estimating the cost and complexity of API calls.

```APIDOC
## POST /v1/tokenizers/estimate-token-count

### Description
Calculates the token count for a request, supporting both text and image inputs.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
`https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/tokenizers/estimate-token-count`

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **model** (string) - Required - The ID of the model to use (e.g., `kimi-k2.5`, `kimi-k2-turbo-preview`).
- **messages** (List[Dict]) - Required - A list of messages in the conversation. Each message should have a `role` (`system`, `user`, or `assistant`) and `content`. For multimodal inputs, `content` can be a list of objects with `type` (`text` or `image_url`) and corresponding data.

### Request Example
```json
{
    "model": "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
    "messages": [
        {
            "role": "system",
            "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"
        },
        { "role": "user", "content": "你好，我叫李雷，1+1等于多少？" }
    ]
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **data** (Object) - Contains the estimated token count.
  - **total_tokens** (integer) - The total number of tokens estimated for the request.

#### Response Example
```json
{
    "data": {
        "total_tokens": 80
    }
}
```
```

--------------------------------

### Vision API

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/chat

This endpoint allows you to process images and generate text descriptions or answer questions about them using vision-capable models. It supports sending images via base64 encoding.

```APIDOC
## POST /v1/chat/completions (Vision Model)

### Description
Processes images and generates text descriptions or answers questions about them using vision-capable models. Supports sending images via base64 encoding.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
/v1/chat/completions

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **model** (string) - Required - The ID of the vision model to use (e.g., `moonshot-v1-8k-vision-preview`).
- **messages** (array) - Required - A list of messages comprising the conversation.
  - **role** (string) - Required - The role of the author of the message (e.g., user).
  - **content** (array) - Required - A list of content parts, which can be text or image URLs.
    - **type** (string) - Required - The type of content, either `text` or `image_url`.
    - **image_url** (object) - Required if type is `image_url` - An object containing the image URL.
      - **url** (string) - Required - The image content, either a base64 encoded string or a file ID.
    - **text** (string) - Required if type is `text` - The text content.
- **temperature** (number) - Optional - Controls randomness. Lower values make output more focused and deterministic.

### Request Example
```json
{
    "model": "moonshot-v1-8k-vision-preview",
    "messages":
    [
        {
            "role": "user",
            "content":
            [
                {
                    "type": "image_url",
                    "image_url":
                    {
                        "url": "data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAGAAAABhCAYAAAApxKSdAAAACXBIWXMAACE4AAAhOAFFljFgAAAAAXNSR0IArs4c6QAAAARnQU1BAACxjwv8YQUAAAUUSURBVHgB7Z29bhtHFIWPHQN2J7lKqnhYpYvpIukCbJEAKQJEegLReYFIT0DrCSI9QEDqCSIDaQIEIOukiJwyza5SJWlId3FFz+HuGmuSSw6p+dlZ3g84luhdUeI9M3fmziyXgBCUe/DHYY0Wj/tgWmjV42zFcWe4MIBBPNJ6qqW0uvAbXFvQgKzQK62bQhkaCIPc10q1Zi3XH1o/IG9cwUm0RogrgDY1KmLgHYX9DvyiBvDYI77XmiD+oLlQHw7hIDoCMBOt1U9w0BsU9mOAtaUUFk3oQoIfzAQFCf5dNMEdTFCQ4NtQih1NSIGgf3ibxOJt5UrAB1gNK72vIdjiI61HWr+YnNxDXK0rJiULsV65GJeiIescLSTTeobKSutiCuojX8kU3MBx4I3WeNVBBRl4fWiCyoB8v2JAAkk9PmDwT8sH1TEghRjgC27scCx41wO43KAg+ILxTvhNaUACwTc04Z0B30LwzTzm5Rjw3sgseIG1wGMawMBPIOQcqvzrNIMHOg9Q5KK953O90/rFC+BhJRH8PQZ+fu7SjC7HAIV95yu99vjlxfvBJx8nwHd6IfNJAkccOjHg6OgIs9lsra6vr2GTNE03/k7q8HAhyJ/2gM9O65/4kT7/mwEcoZwYsPQiV3BwcABb9Ho9KKU2njccDjGdLlxx+InBBPBAAR86ydRPaIC9SASi3+8bnXd+fr78nw8NJ39uDJjXAVFPP7dp/VmWLR9g6w6Huo/IOTk5MTpvZesn/93AiP/dXCwd9SyILT9Jko3n1bZ+8s8rGPGvoVHbEXcPMM39V1dX9Qd/19PPNxta959D4HUGF0RrAFs/8/8mxuPxXLUwtfx2WX+cxdivZ3DFA0SKldZPuPTAKrikbOlMOX+9zFu/Q2iAQoSY5H7mfeb/tXCT8MdneU9wNNCuQUXZA0ynnrUznyqOcrspUY4BJunHqPU3gOgMsNr6G0B0BpgUXrG0fhKVAaaF1/HxMWIhKgNMcj9Tz82Nk6rVGdav/tJ5eraJ0Wi01XPq1r/xOS8uLkJc6XYnRTMNXdf62eIvLy+jyftVghnQ7Xahe8FW59fBTRYOzosDNI1hJdz0lBQkBflkMBjMU5iL13pXRb8fYAJrB/a2db0oFHthAOEUliaYFHE+aaUBdZsvvFhApyM0idYZwOCvW4JmIWdSzPmidQaYrAGZ7iX4oFUGnJ2dGdUCTRqMozeANQCLsE6nA10JG/0Mx4KmDMbBCjEWR2yxu8LAM98vXelmCA2ovVLCI8EMYODWbpbvCXtTBzQVMSAwYkBgxIDAtNKAXWdGIRADAiMpKDA0IIMQikx6QGDEgMCIAYGRMSAsMgaEhgbcQgjFa+kBYZnIGBCWWzEgLPNBOJ6Fk/aR8Y5ZCvktKwX/PJZ7xoVjfs+4chYU11tK2sE85qUBLyH4Zh5z6QHhGPOf6r2j+TEbcgdFP2RaHX5TrYQlDflj5RXE5Q1cG/lWnhYpReUGKdUewGnRmhvnCJbgmxey8sHiZ8iwF3AsUBBckKHI/SWLq6HsBc8huML4DiK80D6WnBqLzN68UFCmopheYJOVYgcU5FOVbAVfYUcUZGoaLPglCtITdg2+tZUFBTFh2+ArWEYh/7z0WIIQSiM43lt5AWAmWhLHylN4QmkNEXfAbGqEQKsHSfHLYwiSq8AnaAAKeaW3D8VbijwNW5nh3IN9FPI/jnpaPKZi2/SfFuJu4W3x9RqWL+N5C+7ruKpBAgLkAAAAAElFTkSuQmCC"
                    }
                },
                {
                    "type": "text",
                    "text": "请描述这个图片"
                }
            ]
        }
    ],
    "temperature": 0.6
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **choices** (array) - A list of generated message choices.
  - **message** (object) - The message object.
    - **content** (string) - The content of the message.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "choices": [
    {
      "message": {
        "content": "这是一张包含[图片内容描述]的图片。"
      }
    }
  ]
}
```

### Chat Completion API Endpoint

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/chat

The HTTP POST endpoint for initiating chat completions with the Moonshot AI API. This is the core endpoint for interacting with the chat models.

```http
POST https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/chat/completions
```

### Node.js: 使用 Kimi API 的 JSON Mode 生成结构化回复

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-json-mode-feature-of-kimi-api

演示如何使用 Node.js 客户端库与 Kimi API 交互，并利用 JSON Mode 生成结构化的回复。代码展示了如何配置 API Key、设置包含输出格式要求的系统提示词，以及如何解析模型返回的 JSON 内容。适用于需要模型输出特定 JSON 格式的应用场景，如构建智能客服。

```javascript
const OpenAI = require("openai");

const client = new OpenAI({
  apiKey: "MOONSHOT_API_KEY", // 在这里将 MOONSHOT_API_KEY 替换为你从 Kimi 开放平台申请的 API Key
  baseURL: "https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
});

const systemPrompt = `
你是月之暗面（Kimi）的智能客服，你负责回答用户提出的各种问题。请参考文档内容回复用户的问题，你的回答可以是文字、图片、链接，在一次回复中可以同时包含文字、图片、链接。

请使用如下 JSON 格式输出你的回复：

{
    "text": "文字信息",
    "image": "图片地址",
    "url": "链接地址"
}

注意，请将文字信息放置在 `text` 字段中，将图片以 `oss://` 开头的链接形式放在 `image` 字段中，将普通链接放置在 `url` 字段中。
`;

async function main() {
  const completion = await client.chat.completions.create({
    model: "kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
    messages: [
      {
        role: "system",
        content: "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。",
      },
      { role: "system", content: systemPrompt }, // <-- 将附带输出格式的 system prompt 提交给 Kimi
      { role: "user", content: "你好，我叫李雷，1+1等于多少？" },
    ],
    temperature: 0.6,
    response_format: { type: "json_object" }, // <-- 使用 response_format 参数指定输出格式为 json_object
  });

  // 由于我们设置了 JSON Mode，Kimi 大模型返回的 message.content 为序列化后的 JSON Object 字符串，
  // 我们使用 JSON.parse 解析其内容，将其反序列化为 JavaScript 中的对象。
  const content = JSON.parse(completion.choices[0].message.content);

  // 解析文本内容
  if (content.text) {
    // 为了演示，我们将内容打印出来；
    // 在真实的业务逻辑中，你可能需要调用发送文本消息的接口将生成的文本发送给用户。
    console.log("text:", content.text);
  }

  // 解析图片内容
  if (content.image) {
    // 为了演示，我们将内容打印出来；
    // 在真实的业务逻辑中，你可能需要先解析图片地址，下载图片后，调用发送图片消息
    // 的接口将图片发送给用户。
    console.log("image:", content.image);
  }

  // 解析链接
  if (content.url) {
    // 为了演示，我们将内容打印出来；
    // 在真实的业务逻辑中，你可能需要调用发送链接卡片的接口，将链接以卡片的形式发送给用户。
    console.log("url:", content.url);
  }
}

main();

```

--------------------------------

### 计算总 Token 费用公式

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/pricing/tools

该代码片段展示了在触发联网搜索时，计算总 Token 费用的公式。它包含了提示 Token、搜索 Token 和完成 Token 的总和。

```text
total_tokens ＝ prompt_tokens ＋ search_tokens ＋ completions_tokens
```

--------------------------------

### Python: 使用 Kimi API 的 JSON Mode 生成结构化回复

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-json-mode-feature-of-kimi-api

演示如何使用 Python 客户端库与 Kimi API 交互，并利用 JSON Mode 生成结构化的回复。代码展示了如何配置 API Key、设置包含输出格式要求的系统提示词，以及如何解析模型返回的 JSON 内容。适用于需要模型输出特定 JSON 格式的应用场景，如构建智能客服。

```python
import json

from openai import OpenAI

client = OpenAI(
    api_key="MOONSHOT_API_KEY", # 在这里将 MOONSHOT_API_KEY 替换为你从 Kimi 开放平台申请的 API Key
    base_url="https://api.moonshot.cn/v1",
)

system_prompt = """
你是月之暗面（Kimi）的智能客服，你负责回答用户提出的各种问题。请参考文档内容回复用户的问题，你的回答可以是文字、图片、链接，在一次回复中可以同时包含文字、图片、链接。

请使用如下 JSON 格式输出你的回复：

{
    "text": "文字信息",
    "image": "图片地址",
    "url": "链接地址"
}

注意，请将文字信息放置在 `text` 字段中，将图片以 `oss://` 开头的链接形式放在 `image` 字段中，将普通链接放置在 `url` 字段中。
"""

completion = client.chat.completions.create(
    model="kimi-k2-turbo-preview",
    messages=[
        {"role": "system",
         "content": "你是 Kimi，由 Moonshot AI 提供的人工智能助手，你更擅长中文和英文的对话。你会为用户提供安全，有帮助，准确的回答。同时，你会拒绝一切涉及恐怖主义，种族歧视，黄色暴力等问题的回答。Moonshot AI 为专有名词，不可翻译成其他语言。"},
        {"role": "system", "content": system_prompt}, # <-- 将附带输出格式的 system prompt 提交给 Kimi
        {"role": "user", "content": "你好，我叫李雷，1+1等于多少？"}
    ],
    temperature=0.6,
    response_format={"type": "json_object"}, # <-- 使用 response_format 参数指定输出格式为 json_object
)

# 由于我们设置了 JSON Mode，Kimi 大模型返回的 message.content 为序列化后的 JSON Object 字符串，
# 我们使用 json.loads 解析其内容，将其反序列化为 python 中的字典 dict。
content = json.loads(completion.choices[0].message.content)

# 解析文本内容
if "text" in content:
	# 为了演示，我们将内容打印出来；
	# 在真实的业务逻辑中，你可能需要调用发送文本消息的接口将生成的文本发送给用户。
    print("text:", content["text"])

# 解析图片内容
if "image" in content:
	# 为了演示，我们将内容打印出来；
	# 在真实的业务逻辑中，你可能需要先解析图片地址，下载图片后，调用发送图片消息
	# 的接口将图片发送给用户。
    print("image:", content["image"])

# 解析链接
if "url" in content:
	# 为了演示，我们将内容打印出来；
	# 在真实的业务逻辑中，你可能需要调用发送链接卡片的接口，将链接以卡片的形式发送给用户。
    print("url:", content["url"])

```

--------------------------------

### Close Asynchronous HTTP Client (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-k2-to-setup-agent

This asynchronous function gracefully closes the underlying HTTP client connection. It's important for releasing resources and ensuring proper termination of network-related operations, especially when dealing with asynchronous requests.

```python
async def close(self):
        await self.httpx.aclose()
```

### Disable Thinking Capability for Kimi K2.5

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/kimi-k2-5-quickstart

This section explains how to disable the thinking capability for the kimi-k2.5 model by specifying `"thinking": {"type": "disabled"}` in the request body.

```APIDOC
## POST /v1/chat/completions

### Description
Disables the thinking capability for the kimi-k2.5 model.

### Method
POST

### Endpoint
/v1/chat/completions

### Parameters
#### Request Body
- **model** (string) - Required - The model to use, e.g., "kimi-k2.5".
- **messages** (array) - Required - An array of message objects representing the conversation history.
- **thinking** (object) - Required - An object to control thinking capabilities. Set to `{"type": "disabled"}` to disable.
  - **type** (string) - Required - The type of thinking, set to "disabled".

### Request Example
```json
{
    "model": "kimi-k2.5",
    "messages": [
        {"role": "user", "content": "你好"}
    ],
    "thinking": {"type": "disabled"}
}
```

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **choices** (array) - The response choices from the model.
- **created** (integer) - Timestamp of creation.
- **id** (string) - Unique identifier for the response.
- **model** (string) - The model used for the response.
- **object** (string) - The type of object, e.g., "chat.completion".
- **usage** (object) - Usage statistics for the request.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "choices": [
    {
      "finish_reason": "stop",
      "index": 0,
      "message": {
        "content": "你好！有什么可以帮您的吗？",
        "role": "assistant"
      }
    }
  ],
  "created": 1706493176,
  "id": "chatcmpl-12345",
  "model": "kimi-k2.5",
  "object": "chat.completion",
  "usage": {
    "completion_tokens": 10,
    "prompt_tokens": 10,
    "total_tokens": 20
  }
}
```
```

--------------------------------

### LaTeX Figure Caption and Data Source Formatting

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/guide/use-kimi-k2-to-setup-agent

Specifies the requirements for figure captions and data sources in LaTeX reports. Captions must be placed below the figure, and data sources (if available) must be clearly indicated with a specific format, preceded by a newline.

```latex
% 图表的图说 **必须满足**：表格下方的图说（数据来源），如果有详细来源的就写，如果没有就不写
%    - 例如，图片或表格中的数据没有详细的来源，或者是综合推断出来的（没有单一的来源），就不加任何图说
%    - 只有当图片或表格中的数据有单一的来源时，才加图说：[来源：XX机构/网站名称：具体的网页标题或文章名称]
%    - 写图说/表格数据来源前，**必须要换行**，保证其在图说/表格下方
\datasource{XX机构/网站名称}{具体的网页标题或文章名称}

```

--------------------------------

### Delete File API

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/files

Deletes a specified file from the Moonshot AI platform.

```APIDOC
## DELETE /v1/files/{file_id}

### Description
Deletes a specified file from the Moonshot AI platform.

### Method
DELETE

### Endpoint
https://api.moonshot.cn/v1/files/{file_id}

### Parameters
#### Path Parameters
- **file_id** (string) - Required - The unique identifier of the file to delete.

### Response
#### Success Response (200)
- **id** (string) - The ID of the deleted file.
- **object** (string) - The object type, typically "file_delete".
- **deleted** (boolean) - True if the file was successfully deleted, false otherwise.

#### Response Example
```json
{
  "id": "file-xxxxxxxxxxxx",
  "object": "file_delete",
  "deleted": true
}
```

### Request Example
```python
file_id_to_delete = "file-xxxxxxxxxxxx"
client.files.delete(file_id=file_id_to_delete)
```
```

--------------------------------

### Delete File (Python)

Source: https://platform.moonshot.cn/docs/api/files

Deletes a specific file from the Moonshot AI platform using its unique file ID. This is useful for cleaning up storage and removing files that are no longer needed.

```Python
client.files.delete(file_id=file_id)

```
